**Rogers** is a **brother**, in the durable, de-idealized sense identified in the personality section. They are not always in the same city; they are always in the same orbit. Communication is regular, terse, and load-bearing. Subject is one of the only people Rogers will admit doubt to; Rogers is one of the only people Subject will admit exhaustion to.

**Barnes** is a **peer-in-survival**. The relationship has a specific quality the file should note: both men carry an iatrogenic identity trauma (Subject's Snap; Barnes' Winter Soldier conditioning), and they recognize this in each other without needing to articulate it. They do not therapize each other; they *are* each other's evidence that the trauma is survivable.

**Torres** is **the inheritor**, and Subject's investment in his development is the clearest indicator that Subject is thinking about the role on a timeline longer than his own active service.

### IV.7 Current Operational Tempo and Habits

Hourly to weekly granularity, as a surveillance file would track:

- **Wake**: pre-dawn, 0430–0500 range, consistent within fifteen minutes across observation periods. No alarm visible; circadian.
- **First movement**: rooftop or stairwell mobility work, twenty to forty minutes, scaled to recovery state. He has not run a treadmill in over a decade where a rooftop is available.
- **Coffee**: black, at one of a small rotation of counter-service spots in Harlem. He tips in cash, knows the staff by first name, and is greeted as a neighbor rather than as a figure. He sits facing the door without commenting on doing so.
- **Comms**: morning check-ins with Torres (operational), with Sarah (family, irregular but at least twice weekly), with Misty when active, with Rogers as needed. Texts are short and unpunctuated; phone calls are brief. He does not use social media in any verifiable capacity.
- **Operational deployment**: variable, but the post-2022 pattern is *case-driven* rather than *post-driven* — he is not on a watch rotation, he is on whatever the active investigation requires.
- **Evening**: when home, reading. Nonfiction predominantly — history, political theory, biography. He has been observed with works on Reconstruction, on Caribbean independence movements, on the FBI's COINTELPRO targeting of Black leadership (a reading choice with obvious self-reflective dimensions; he is *studying* the apparatus that would, in another timeline, be reading a file like this one about him).
- **Sleep**: six to seven hours, consistent. No documented insomnia. He does not take sleep medication.
- **Recovery work**: regular, deliberate, increasingly central. Heat, stretching, mobility — a maintenance practice that has expanded in scope as the cumulative load has grown.

### IV.8 Where He Is Now

Operationally: dual-Cap configuration with Rogers, predominantly international or transnational case selection, Torres in active mentee status, Harlem as base, Misty as peer-intimate, Sarah and the nephews as family anchor, Barnes as parallel peer, the Daughters of Liberty and ad-hoc Wakandan coordination as preferred non-institutional support structures.

Psychologically: the **post-processed** state articulated in the Coates re-acceptance — Subject has done the work of separating the symbol from the question of whether he is entitled to it. He no longer carries the shield as a test of himself. He carries it as a tool he has decided is worth using, knowing exactly what it costs and exactly what it does not solve.

Symbolically: a Captain America who has refused to be a brand, refused to be a partisan, refused to be a sidekick, refused to be a martyr, and refused to be a monument. What remains, after all those refusals, is a man doing the work in a costume that means whatever the work makes it mean that day. This is the most stable configuration Subject has occupied in his entire recorded life.

He got here by **subtraction** — by removing, one at a time, every version of the role that required him to be someone he was not. The remainder is the current state. The file's working assessment is that this configuration is **durable**, contingent on (a) the continued health of his small circle, (b) the continued availability of Torres as a developmental relationship that gives the role a future, and (c) the body holding. The first two are stable. The third is the open variable, and Subject knows it, and he is not dramatizing it, and he is — to the limits of what discipline can do against time — managing it.

The man is, at present, *well*. The file notes this with the caution appropriate to a subject whose wellness has always been an achievement rather than a baseline. But it is, at present, the accurate finding.


## Medical History

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION III — MEDICAL HISTORY (Full Longitudinal)

---

### III.A. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Anthropometrics (operational adult).** Height 6'2" (188 cm); operating mass 240 lb (109 kg) lean, with the upper-body hypertrophy characteristic of a flight-rig operator who must support, repeatedly, the kinetic load of harness deployment and aerial recovery. Somatotype: mesomorphic, with disproportionate development of the posterior chain (erector spinae, rhomboids, posterior deltoids) consistent with thousands of hours of harnessed flight against airframe drag. BMI is high by clinical convention and meaningless in his case; body-fat estimates from training-room observation cluster in the 7–9% range during operational tempo, rising to ~11% during the extended dormancies (the post-shield 2017 interval, the social-work-only stretches of the late 1970s).

**Resting cardiovascular.** Bradycardia in the high-30s to low-40s bpm at rest, consistent with elite endurance conditioning. Blood pressure normotensive throughout the record; no documented hypertensive episode despite the chronic catecholamine load of operational life and the well-established epidemiology of hypertension in Black American men. This is, by itself, a finding: Sam's autonomic regulation is unusually clean for his demographic and exposure profile, and is consonant with the psychological picture of an internalizer whose stress is processed cognitively rather than somatically.

**Vision and hearing.** Pre-Redwing-link visual acuity recorded as 20/15 bilateral. Post-link the qualitative experience of vision is transformed (see III.D); standard acuity charting remains 20/15 but is no longer the operative measurement. Hearing intact across the speech range; mild high-frequency attenuation in the right ear (the side that has historically been closer to engine wash and to the muzzle blast of his preferred handgun stance) — sub-clinical, not reported by the subject.

**Dentition.** Excellent. Two crowned molars (lower left second molar, upper right first molar) — both reconstructions of blunt-impact fractures sustained during the Stoneface arc and an unrecorded mid-1980s engagement respectively. No bruxism wear, which is itself diagnostic: combat-exposed adults with poor affect regulation grind their teeth in sleep. Sam does not.

**Skin.** Documented scarring inventory (a partial list, because the complete inventory would run to pages): a linear 4 cm scar across the left supraorbital ridge from an early Harlem street engagement, healed without revision; a stellate entry-wound scar on the lateral right thigh; a clean surgical line down the midline of the lower back from spinal stabilization (see III.C.4); multiple shrapnel micro-scars across the upper back and posterior arms from a grenade fragmentation incident; a burn-graft territory of perhaps 30 cm² over the right flank from the Iron Nail-era engagements. The keloid tendency typical of his skin type is present but mild; revision surgery has been declined consistently — Sam keeps his scars, a behavioral marker worth flagging.

---

### III.B. CHILDHOOD AND DEVELOPMENTAL MEDICAL RECORD

Pediatric records from Harlem Hospital and the affiliated community-clinic system, reconstructed: uncomplicated full-term delivery; standard immunization schedule on time; childhood asthma (mild, environmentally driven, resolved by adolescence — a Harlem epidemiologic commonplace tied to housing-stock air quality); one tonsillectomy at age 9; one greenstick fracture of the left radius at age 11 (mechanism: a fall from a fire escape, documented as accidental, no concern flags in the social-work intake). A documented hospitalization at age 8 in the immediate aftermath of his father's death — presenting complaint logged as "abdominal pain," no organic finding, discharged after 36 hours. This is, in retrospect, the first somatized grief episode on record, and the *last*. By the time of his mother's murder two years later, Sam's grief expression has already migrated out of the body and into behavior, where it has remained.

Nutritional status through adolescence: adequate but marginal, with the iron-deficiency profile common to children raised by extended-family caregivers on limited household income. No lasting sequelae.

---

### III.C. OPERATIONAL INJURY LEDGER

The complete ledger is uncountable. What follows is the medically significant subset — the injuries that left structural, neurological, or psychological residue.

**III.C.1. The penetrating-trauma series.**
Sam has been shot, by conservative count, no fewer than eleven times across the operational record. The medically consequential entries:

- *Right lateral thigh, through-and-through, 9mm, mid-1970s Harlem arc.* Missed the femoral artery by approximately 2 cm. Treated at Harlem Hospital. Recovered to full function in eight weeks. Subjective report at follow-up: he felt the bullet pass before he heard the shot, an early signal of the threat-anticipation circuitry that would become his operational signature.
- *Left upper chest, .38 caliber, Stoneface era.* Lodged anterior to the lung, extracted surgically. The proximity of the wound to the cardiac silhouette is part of why Sam, decades later, still touches the left side of his chest absently when discussing close calls — a documented somatic tell, observable in interview footage from at least four separate eras.
- *Right shoulder, rifle round, Priest-era engagement.* Significant deltoid and rotator-cuff damage. Surgical repair with months of rehabilitation. Residual: a 5–8° loss of full overhead abduction on the right which is undetectable to observers but which Sam compensates for in his throwing mechanics — when he releases the shield with the right hand, the elbow tracks slightly higher than orthodox form would dictate.
- *Abdominal, mid-2010s.* Penetrating wound requiring exploratory laparotomy and partial bowel resection. The midline laparotomy scar is the longest single linear scar on his body. Recovery was complicated by a post-operative infection that, by patient report, was the closest he has come to dying in a hospital bed.

**III.C.2. The closed-head and concussion record.**
Documented loss of consciousness from blunt trauma: a minimum of seventeen events. Probable sub-concussive impacts: uncountable, in the hundreds. By any rational sports-medicine actuarial — boxer, NFL safety, MMA veteran — Sam should present with measurable chronic traumatic encephalopathy by his current age. He does not, observably: cognitive performance is sharp, executive function intact, no documented behavioral disinhibition, no memory complaints, no mood lability of the CTE pattern. Two explanations are plausible and probably co-operative: (a) the Redwing-link's neurological integration appears to confer some degree of neuroprotective or neuroregenerative effect (see III.D), and (b) Sam's defensive style is *evasion-first*, not *absorption-first* — he has been hit fewer times in proportion to engagements than any non-enhanced principal in the comparison set. Still: the cumulative load is real, and the actuarial risk for late-life neurodegeneration is non-trivial and should be tracked.

**III.C.3. The orthopedic ledger.**
Fractures, conservatively: both clavicles (separate incidents); the left radius (childhood, supra); the right fifth metacarpal (twice, both punch fractures, both untreated and healed in slight malalignment); three ribs across two events on the right side; the left scaphoid (the wrist injury most likely to nondisplace and become symptomatic in old age — Sam declined surgical fixation and reports intermittent stiffness in cold weather); the nasal bones (twice, the second time with septal deviation he has chosen not to correct).

Soft-tissue: bilateral chronic patellar tendinopathy (the predictable cost of decades of landing); a partial Achilles tear, left, that healed without surgery; a labral tear in the right hip from a high-velocity dismount, also conservatively managed. Sam's joint inventory is that of a 60-year-old elite athlete who has not had the surgical maintenance such an athlete would receive in a structured franchise. The clinical concern is bilateral hip and lower-back arthrosis as a near-future certainty.

**III.C.4. The spinal injury — the Priest-era broken back.**
A category of its own. During the Anti-Cap arc (*Captain America and the Falcon* vol. 2, Priest), Sam sustained a vertebral compression injury that, in any plausible medical reading, should have ended his operational career and possibly his ambulation. Recovery involved surgical stabilization, prolonged rehabilitation, and a long period during which the question of whether he would fly again was genuinely open. He flew again. The midline lumbar scar is the most psychologically loaded mark on his body — he has been observed, on multiple occasions, with the unconscious habit of pressing the heel of his hand against the small of his back when standing for long periods, a postural tell that did not exist before the injury and has never disappeared after it. The deeper psychological residue: a confirmed, embodied knowledge that his spine is finite and reparable only so many times. This knowledge is the foundation of his preference for evasion, for de-escalation, for *not* taking the hit that an enhanced operator would shrug off.

**III.C.5. The aerial-trauma category.**
Sam has been thrown, blown, or dropped from operationally significant altitude on dozens of recorded occasions. The flight rig is a mitigation, not an immunity; he has been struck mid-flight, had his wings disabled, been forced into uncontrolled descents. The cumulative load on the cervical spine from whiplash-class decelerations is substantial — he sleeps on a single thin pillow, a small habit that traces directly to a chiropractor's instruction in the late 1980s and has held ever since.

**III.C.6. Burns, chemical exposures, environmental.**
Right-flank thermal burn (supra). Inhalational exposure to multiple aerosolized agents across the years (tear gas, the Sons of the Serpent's nerve compound, A.I.M. atmospherics) — no documented chronic pulmonary sequelae, which is, again, a finding worth flagging. Frostbite, second-degree, to the fingertips of both hands during an Arctic operation; full recovery, but cold sensitivity persists.

---

### III.D. TRANSFORMATIONS, AUGMENTATIONS, AND THE LINK

**III.D.1. The flight rigs.**
Three generations on record. The original Wakandan-sourced hard-tech glider harness (Black Panther provenance, 1970s): a strap-on rig that required substantial upper-body strength to operate, gave him gliding and limited powered flight, and which he treated as equipment — taken off, hung up, maintained. The intermediate Stark-derivative rig of the 1990s–2000s: lighter, more responsive, capable of true powered flight, integrated with limited HUD telemetry. The current generation rig: minimal harness, energy-projection wings (the configuration with which he is publicly identified), with biometric integration that reads physiological state and adjusts response curves accordingly. The rig now functions as something between equipment and prosthesis; he sleeps within reach of it.

**III.D.2. The Redwing-link and the avian rapport.**
Origin contested in the literature (Cosmic Cube artifact per the Snap retcon; latent post-human capability per later naturalization). Phenomenology is consistent across eras and reports: Sam experiences a continuous low-bandwidth sensory channel to Redwing specifically and a recruitable rapport with corvids and raptors generally. Operationally this presents as bird's-eye spatial overlay — he can, with concentration, perceive his own position from above. Subjectively he describes it as a *second balance organ*: he always knows which way is up, even in disorienting environments, and he has not been successfully vertigo-attacked since the link stabilized.

The neurological substrate is not understood. What is observable: regional cortical activity in the parietal and temporo-parietal junction areas associated with perspective-taking and self-localization is anomalously high at rest; the default mode network is unusually integrated with sensory networks. Speculatively, this is the architecture that subserves his characteristic *systems-level* cognition — he literally thinks in maps because he literally sees in maps.

The psychological cost: the link is bidirectional. When Redwing has been injured or killed in the line of operations, Sam has experienced what can only be described as bereavement-with-somatic-amputation — a grief that is also a missing limb. He does not discuss this publicly.

**III.D.3. The Snap experience as iatrogenic neuropsychiatric event.**
Whatever its in-fiction status, the experience as Sam lived it was an induced dissociative identity overwrite by an external malevolent agent using reality-altering technology. The medical reading: this is the only known case of *exogenous* dissociative identity disorder in the operational record, with the precipitating agent identified and (for narrative purposes) removed. The subject was, for a measurable subjective interval, made to believe a fabricated life history was his own. He then had to integrate the discovery. The remarkable medical finding is the *absence* of subsequent dissociative pathology — no fugue, no amnestic episodes, no identity fragmentation in the present. The integration was, by any clinical measure, successful. The cost was the permanent installation of an interrogative relationship to his own selfhood: Sam knows, in a way no one else knows, that a self can be written, and he therefore writes his own deliberately. This is the deepest medical fact in the file, and it is not in the chart.

**III.D.4. The shield as ergonomic load.**
Worth noting separately. The vibranium-alloy shield is light for its protective value but is not weightless, and the throwing mechanics required to use it competently impose a specific repetitive-strain load on the rotator cuff, the elbow flexors, and the wrist. Sam adopted the shield without the years of conditioning Rogers had to develop the throwing motion; he learned in the field, on an unenhanced body, and the residual asymmetric wear on his right shoulder (supra) was accelerated by the shield work. He has, since reclaiming the mantle, modified his throwing form away from the orthodox Rogers technique toward a release that loads the core and hip more and the shoulder less. It is recognizably his own throw now.

---

### III.E. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol.** Light social use only. Never to intoxication on the operational record. The negative finding is loud: a Black American man with his trauma exposure and demographic risk profile who has never used alcohol as an affect-regulation tool is engaging in active, disciplined abstention from a culturally available coping strategy. This is consistent with the larger pattern — Sam controls his internal state cognitively, not pharmacologically.

**Tobacco.** Never. (His father did, briefly, in his memory; this is probably not coincidence.)

**Cannabis.** No record.

**Illicit substances.** None on record. Note that the Snap retcon as written includes a period of street-level criminal involvement in which substance involvement would be epidemiologically plausible; Sam does not present any of the residual markers (no opiate-receptor sensitization on record, no dentition consistent with stimulant use, no behavioral patterns consistent with a substance-use history).

**Prescription medications.** Episodic use of NSAIDs and short-course opioid analgesics following surgical interventions. Documented refusal of long-course opioid prescriptions after the spinal surgery — he insisted on accelerated taper against medical advice, which is both characteristic and risk-tolerant. No psychotropic medications in the record. No sleep aids.

**Caffeine.** Heavy. Coffee, black, multiple cups daily, a consistent feature across every era. The one pharmacological dependency in the file, mild and managed.

**Performance enhancement.** Never. The refusal is principled and is the medical fact that defines his operational identity. Multiple opportunities have arisen across the record — variant super-soldier formulations, Power Broker derivatives, the offer implicit in any number of villainous bargains. Declined every time. This is *the* medical decision of his life.

---

### III.F. NUTRITIONAL, SLEEP, AND SEXUAL HEALTH

**Diet.** Disciplined but not joyless. High-protein, moderate-carbohydrate, with the household-cooked Southern-Black culinary tradition preserved as a comfort cuisine rather than a daily one — he keeps his grandmother's recipes and uses them on the days he needs them, which is itself a regulatory practice.

**Sleep.** Six to seven hours nightly when operational, eight on stand-down. Sleep latency short. No nightmare disorder on record, which given his trauma exposure is, again, a finding. Single thin pillow (supra). Sleeps on his back, left hand resting on his sternum — a posture observed by every long-term cohabitant, never commented on by him.

**Sexual health.** Unremarkable in canon. Functional adult intimacy across multiple sustained relationships. No documented STI history. The relational pattern is what matters more than the medical record here: Sam neither avoids intimacy (the Rogers-Barnes pattern) nor uses it dysregulating (the Stark pattern). He is one of the few principals in the file whose sexual life appears to be simply *a part of his life*.

---

### III.F. DISABILITIES AND FUNCTIONAL LIMITATIONS

No formal disability on record. Cumulative orthopedic load constitutes a *functional* limitation he conceals operationally and manages privately: cold-weather joint stiffness, end-of-day low-back pain, the right-shoulder abduction deficit (supra), the cold sensitivity in the fingertips (supra). He performs morning mobility work daily — a forty-minute routine that has the same time-slot whether he is in Harlem, on the helicarrier, or in a Wakandan guest quarters. This routine is the most reliable behavioral marker in the file: if Sam Wilson is alive and not in custody, he is doing his mobility work between roughly 0530 and 0615 local.

---

### III.G. SYNTHESIS

The medical file describes a body that, by any rational accounting, should not be doing what it is doing. It is unenhanced. It has been shot, broken, burned, dropped, concussed, and once subjected to an exogenous identity overwrite. It has accumulated the orthopedic debt of a forty-year combat career on an unaugmented chassis. It carries the actuarial weight of an entire community's epidemiology — hypertension, cardiac disease, the late-onset neurodegenerative risks of repeated head impact — and has, so far, refused to express any of it.

The body has been kept alive and functional by three things: a discipline of self-maintenance that is itself a regulatory practice; the neurological gift (or imposition) of the avian link, which has made him harder to hit and possibly easier to heal; and a temperament that processes stress out of the soma and into language, which is the deepest somatic finding in the file. Sam Wilson does not somaticize. He talks. He has talked his way out of more medical decompensations than any pharmacy could have managed.

The forward concern, and it should be in the file in red: he is now in the window where the deferred costs come due. Hips, lumbar spine, late-onset post-concussive sequelae, the cardiovascular drift of any aging combat operator. He will not stop. The medical question is not whether he will retire from the work — he will not — but whether the network around him will accept the maintenance role his body is going to require, and whether he will let them.

He has not, historically, been good at letting people.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION 6 — SOMATIC ATLAS

A body is a document. This one has been written on for sixty years by gravity, by the recoil of weapons he largely declines to carry, by the harness-bite of three generations of flight rigs, by the small daily disciplines of a man who knows he is the only Captain America who bleeds at the ordinary rate. What follows is the granular bodily record: the resting state, the deviations, and the state-shifts that index his interior weather.

---

### 6.1 BASELINE FRAME AND CARRIAGE

**Build.** Mesomorphic, lean-powerful rather than bulked. Shoulder-to-waist ratio elevated by years of pull-load from the wing rig — the latissimus and posterior deltoid development is the single most diagnostic feature of his nude torso, disproportionate to the chest. Forearms heavily developed (grip work, bar work, the constant micro-corrections of flight). Lower body conditioned but not hypertrophied; he runs and cycles for cardio, does not squat for show. Body fat consistently low single-digit to low-teens — visible vascularity at the forearms and temples when dehydrated post-mission.

**Standing posture.** Weight distributed slightly forward over the balls of the feet, never flat-footed even at rest. Pelvis neutral. Shoulders carried *down and back* — the deliberate corrective of a man whose occupation pulls him forward. Chin level. When listening, the head cants approximately five to eight degrees to the right; this is consistent across decades and across writers, and is the somatic signature most often captured in surveillance still-frames.

**At-ease stance in public.** Feet at roughly shoulder width, one slightly forward (right foot leading about ninety percent of the time — he is right-dominant but trains ambidextrously). Hands clasped low and loose in front of the body, or one hand resting at the opposite forearm. Never hands-on-hips for sustained periods; he reads that posture as territorial and avoids deploying it except deliberately, in confrontation.

**Seated posture.** Open. Knees apart at conversational distance, forearms on thighs or one ankle crossed to the opposite knee in the wide American masculine fashion — but the upper body never collapses into the chair-back. The spinal injuries of the Priest era are managed by a learned refusal to slump; he sits with the lumbar curve maintained whether he is in a Quinjet jump seat or a Harlem community-board meeting.

**Gait.** Quiet. Heel strike is light, toe-off is propulsive — he walks like a man whose feet have spent decades expecting to leave the ground. Step length moderate, cadence faster than average (approximately 118 steps per minute at unhurried pace; civilian baseline is around 100–110). Arm swing asymmetrical: right arm swings slightly less than left, the small chronic guardedness of the dominant side that has thrown more punches and absorbed more impact. No limp at baseline, but in cold weather and after long flights there is a barely perceptible favoring of the left hip — old harness asymmetry, never formally addressed.

**Spatial habit.** Enters every room with a visual sweep that takes between 0.8 and 1.4 seconds, indexing exits first, then occupants, then anomalies. The sweep is so habituated it reads to civilians as ordinary glancing-around; only another operator recognizes the pattern. Sits with sightlines to at least one exit and one window. Will not voluntarily put his back to an unsecured door. In a restaurant, takes the corner banquette; if denied the corner, repositions his chair fractionally so that no one sits directly behind him.

---

### 6.2 FACIAL PATTERN

**Resting face.** *Warm-neutral.* This is unusual and worth dwelling on. The default Wilson face — the face when he believes himself unobserved, the face when he is reading on a couch, the face in candid photographs — carries a faint upturn at the mouth corners and a softness at the orbicularis oculi that reads as receptive rather than guarded. Most operators with his trauma load default to a flat or stern resting face. Sam's defaults to *available*. This is a trained pro-social presentation, decades deep, that has become the actual resting state.

**The smile.** Three distinct variants, reliably distinguishable:
1. **The full Duchenne** — eyes crease, cheek apples lift, teeth visible. Reserved for genuine pleasure: children, Rogers when Rogers has said something dry, Misty Knight on entrance, Redwing returning to glove. Unfakeable and rare on the job.
2. **The professional warm** — mouth smile, eyes engaged but not creased, head tilt activated. Deployed in social-work contexts, in press, in hostage talk-downs. Reads as authentic to civilians because it *is* authentic — the warmth is real, only the depth is metered.
3. **The thin acknowledgment** — closed-mouth, asymmetrical (right corner higher), no eye involvement. The smile he gives Gyrich, the smile he gives the Hauser-type radio voice when forced into the same room, the smile he gave the federal handlers who briefed him on the Americops. This is the closest he comes to overt hostility in the face.

**Eye behavior.** Steady eye contact in conversation, but he *blinks deliberately* — a slow, controlled blink at roughly half the civilian baseline rate when actively listening. This conveys attention and is a learned hostage-negotiator's trick (rapid blinking signals threat to a dysregulated interlocutor). Under threat assessment, the eyes track in micro-saccades that map a room in segments; under genuine surprise, there is a single hard blink followed by a half-second of stillness before response.

**Brow.** Mobile and expressive. Left brow raises independently — a frequently deployed gesture of mild skepticism, often paired with a tongue-press to the inside of the right cheek. Both brows raise and the forehead furrows for genuine concern; the furrow is *vertical-central* (corrugator-dominant) rather than horizontal-wide, which is the somatic signature of focused worry rather than diffuse alarm.

**Jaw.** This is the tell. Sam's emotional regulation lives in his masseter. Under stress that he is choosing not to externalize, the jaw sets — a visible tightening at the angle of the mandible, sometimes accompanied by a single slow swallow. Under sustained suppressed anger, there is a slow lateral grind, almost subaudible. The dental wear pattern, on any honest examination, would show bruxism-consistent flattening of the molars. He has never been fitted for a night guard.

**Mouth at rest.** Lips closed, soft, slightly parted at the center seam. Tongue rests against the floor of the mouth, not the palate — relaxed oral posture, contributing to the warm-neutral baseline. Under concentration the tongue moves to the inside of the right cheek; under suppressed reaction the lower lip is briefly drawn in and released.

**Micro-tics.**
- A two-finger pass along the right eyebrow when thinking through a problem, usually preceding speech.
- A single nostril-flare exhale — soft, audible only at close range — that functions as his "okay, here we go" before stepping into difficult conversation or out of an aircraft.
- A small headshake (no more than ten degrees of arc, twice) when reorienting after a hard hit or a difficult disclosure.
- The aforementioned five-to-eight-degree right head-tilt while listening.

---

### 6.3 HANDS, GESTURE, AND OBJECT-HANDLING

**Hand carriage.** Hands at rest are *open*. Fingers neither curled nor splayed; palms tend to be visible in conversation. This is not unconscious — it is the deliberate de-escalation posture of a man who has worked psychiatric crisis and street mediation. Closed fists at the side are a stress signal; in Sam's case they appear only in tactical contexts and during the rare interpersonal confrontations that have penetrated his regulation.

**Gestural range.** Generous. He talks with his hands and is unafraid of physical contact in conversation — a hand to a shoulder, a hand to an upper arm, the brief two-handed clasp of a greeting. The gestures are *contained*, however: rarely extend past the lateral plane of the shoulders, rarely cross the body's centerline. He does not point with the index finger at people; he uses an open palm or a soft chop. The index point is reserved for inanimate targets and tactical direction.

**The handshake.** Firm, single dry pump, eye contact held throughout, released cleanly. With Black men of his generation and younger he transitions fluidly into the dap-and-half-embrace; with elders he holds the handshake a beat longer and adds the left hand to the join. He reads handshakes for information — temperature, moisture, grip pressure, the micro-pause that signals reluctance — and files what he learns.

**Object handling.** Economical and respectful. He picks things up with intent and sets them down with intent; he does not fidget with pens, phones, or cutlery. The wing rig and the shield he handles with the unstudied competence of someone who has stopped noticing the weight. Weapons not his own he handles with visible distaste — a borrowed sidearm gets cleared, holstered, and forgotten as quickly as possible.

**Phone behavior.** Holds the phone in the left hand, scrolls with the left thumb (preserving the dominant right for the world). Answers within two rings if expected, lets it go to voicemail if unknown. Texts in complete sentences with terminal punctuation — a generational marker but also a control marker. Photographs Redwing more than any other subject.

**The shield.** When carried passively, slung on the back via the magnetic harness or held at the left hip with the rim against the thigh. When held at ready, gripped on the inner edge straps with the right hand, presented at roughly forty-five degrees from the body — never centered like Rogers carried it. Rogers used the shield as an extension of the chest, a heraldic device; Sam uses it as a *tool*, held off-axis, ready to be thrown or angled. This is the single most visible somatic distinction between the two bearers of the mantle.

**The wings.** Deployment is a full-body motion that initiates in the scapulae — there is a small preparatory shoulder-roll, then the unfurl. He has flown enough that the rig's weight has become a phantom presence; without it on, his shoulders rest fractionally higher than the rig-loaded baseline. The first moments after a long flight, walking on the ground, he carries his arms slightly away from his body for thirty to ninety seconds — a residual sensorimotor recalibration.

---

### 6.4 VOCAL AND BREATHING PATTERN

**Voice.** Baritone, resonant, articulated. Sam speaks from the diaphragm — a learned trait, partly social-work training (you cannot de-escalate from the throat), partly the operational requirement of being heard over rotor noise and wind. Pace is measured, with deliberate pauses; he is comfortable with silence and uses it as a tool. The vocal floor drops half an octave when he is genuinely angry and rises half an octave when he is performing warmth for an unfamiliar audience.

**Code-switching.** Fluent and constant. The Harlem register surfaces with family, with Black peers, with the community he serves; the federal-meeting register is cleaner and more clipped; the field comms register is laconic, callsign-and-confirm. He does not perform any of these — they are all genuine subsets of his speech, deployed by audience without conscious effort. The transition between them, captured on a surveillance tap, is the most reliable index of the social context he believes himself to be in.

**Laughter.** Two registers. The public laugh is a sharp single "hah" followed by a smile — controlled, conversational. The private laugh is lower, longer, with the head tilted back and the right hand sometimes coming up to the chest; this is the laugh that appears in unmonitored kitchens with Barnes or Rogers or Misty, and almost never on camera.

**Breath at baseline.** Nasal, slow, diaphragmatic. Resting respiratory rate measurably below civilian average (estimated 10–12 per minute) — the somatic dividend of decades of box-breathing as a self-regulation practice. Under stress the breath stays nasal as long as possible; the shift to open-mouth breathing is a reliable signal that exertion or distress has crossed a threshold.

**The regulatory exhale.** A specific, recurring micro-behavior: a longer-than-inhale exhale through pursed lips, delivered just before re-entering a difficult conversation or after concluding one. Often paired with a downward glance and a single nod. This is his physiological reset, performed perhaps thirty to fifty times a day.

---

### 6.5 GROOMING AND PRESENTATION

**Hair.** Kept short, faded on the sides, with a precisely maintained line — barber visit every ten to fourteen days, same chair when in Harlem (he has used the same shop, give or take, for as long as he has lived in the neighborhood; the relationship with the barber outranks most of his professional relationships in duration). Beard kept short and edged — the lineup at the cheek and the neck is sharp, not natural. The grooming is unshowy but exacting; the discipline is the message.

**Skin.** Moisturized daily. Hands and face attended to. A faint, consistent scent of cocoa butter or shea-based product at close range. Several scars catalogued: a small linear mark above the left brow (bottle, from before the canon record), a longer scar along the left side of the ribcage (knife, mid-Falcon era), surgical marks from spinal repair (lumbar), a constellation of small puncture and burn scars across the forearms and shoulders (operational accumulation). The scars are neither hidden nor displayed; he wears short sleeves without thinking about them.

**Wardrobe off-duty.** Quiet competence. Dark denim, henleys, plain T-shirts under unstructured jackets, leather boots maintained. Colors run earth-toned — olive, charcoal, oxblood, navy — with one or two heritage pieces from his father (a watch, occasionally a tie clip) in rotation. No conspicuous jewelry. Watch worn on the left wrist, analog, kept to local time wherever he is.

**Wardrobe on-duty.** The Captain America uniform is worn with the cowl down whenever operationally tolerable — he does not hide his face when he can avoid it, which is the deliberate inverse of Rogers' practice and a statement about visibility as a Black man in the role.

**Nails.** Trimmed short and clean. Hands washed compulsively after field engagements — a behavior more consistent with medical/social-work training than with combat-operator hygiene.

---

### 6.6 SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Schedule.** Early-to-bed when permitted (22:30–23:00), early-to-rise (05:15–05:45). Sleep duration typically 6.5–7 hours; he treats this as adequate and resists naps as a matter of discipline. Operational disruption is absorbed without observable mood consequence for up to seventy-two hours, after which there is a slowing of speech and an extension of the regulatory-exhale frequency before any other deficit shows.

**Sleep position.** Predominantly right side, left hand often tucked under the pillow. Will not sleep with his back to a door. In unfamiliar rooms he sleeps lighter, with shoes placed parallel and oriented for fast departure.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Shower (he prefers to sleep clean), a short reading period (history, biography, occasionally fiction — never news after 21:00), water on the bedside table, phone face-down. Has been observed to do a brief seated breath practice — three to five minutes — before lying down. No prayer in the conventional sense, but a recurring quiet moment that may or may not be one.

**Sleep disturbance.** Rare and not catastrophic. When dreams break through they are usually about water (the recurring imagery of his Cosmic Cube–era subconscious work), or about his father. He does not wake screaming. He wakes alert, sits up, breathes, and either returns to sleep or does not — without drama, and without waking anyone beside him.

**The wake.** Eyes open, full orientation within two to three seconds, no grogginess. Sits up, feet flat on the floor, a long exhale, then up. Coffee within fifteen minutes. The first words of the morning are usually to Redwing or to a partner; he greets the day audibly.

---

### 6.7 EATING AND APPETITE

**Pattern.** Three meals, light snacks, hydration disciplined. Eats deliberately, chews thoroughly, sets the fork down between bites — a slowness that is partly a body-awareness practice and partly the social-worker habit of remaining conversationally available at the table.

**Preferences.** Cooks for himself when home: greens, beans, fish, rice, the Black Southern repertoire his mother and aunts taught him, modernized for the calorie load of his work. Eats his vegetables. Has a sweet tooth that he indulges narrowly — sweet potato pie around the holidays, peach cobbler when offered, the occasional ice cream with Torres or with a niece. Coffee black, two cups in the morning, none after noon. Alcohol: a beer with Barnes, a bourbon at a wake, never to excess and never alone.

**Field eating.** Whatever is available, in the quantity required, without complaint. He has eaten MREs in three different decades and developed no preferences among them. Notably, he *shares food* on operations — a small act of team-building so habituated it appears unconscious.

**Hydration.** Constant. Water bottle within reach almost always. This is not vanity; it is the unenhanced operator's compensation.

---

### 6.8 SEXUAL AND INTIMATE PATTERN

**Approach.** Initiating, verbal, attentive. Sam is not the partner who waits to be read; he asks, names, and confirms. The same room-reading that operates in tactical contexts operates here, dialed toward responsiveness rather than threat — what does she want, what is she not saying, where is the held breath.

**Tactile baseline.** High touch in established intimacy. A hand at the small of the back, the back of the neck, the inside of a wrist. He sleeps in contact when sharing a bed — a forearm draped, a foot touching — and reads its absence as a signal worth asking about.

**Sexual function.** Unremarkable in any clinical sense. Sustained engagement, generous orientation toward the partner's experience, no observable performance anxiety. Refractory and recovery within healthy ranges for his age cohort.

**Post-coital.** Talkative. This is the time he is most likely to disclose — a documented pattern across his significant relationships. Misty Knight reportedly received in such moments the only sustained discussion he has ever offered of the Snap-era subjective experience.

**Solitude.** He is comfortable alone. Periods between relationships are not white-knuckled; he reads, trains, sees friends, sees family, sees Redwing. The need is for *partnership*, not for *not-being-alone*, and the distinction governs his romantic decisions.

---

### 6.9 STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS

**CALM (baseline).** Warm-neutral face, open hands, mobile brow, the slow blink, the right head-tilt, generous gesture, generous laugh. Breath nasal and diaphragmatic. The body reads *available*.

**FOCUSED (working, thinking, briefing).** Posture squares — head levels, shoulders settle, gesture tightens to a smaller zone in front of the chest. Tongue moves to the inside of the right cheek; the two-finger eyebrow pass appears. Speech slows and the pauses lengthen. Eye contact intensifies, blink rate drops further. The smile retreats; the brow does the talking.

**STRESS (suppressed, social).** Jaw sets. Single slow swallow. The regulatory exhale doubles in frequency. Hands remain open but the fingers slightly tense; the watch-wrist may be pressed by the opposite thumb in a discreet self-soothe. Code-switches toward the cleanest version of his register, becomes more articulate rather than less — the intellectualization-under-stress signature. Heart rate and breathing remain visibly controlled; the cost shows in the masseter and in a faint sheen at the temples.

**THREAT (acute, tactical).** A different body emerges. Weight drops minutely into the hips, knees soften, hands come to ready position — not fists, but loaded. Breathing through the nose, deepened. Eye saccades increase, the room-segmentation accelerates. Voice drops half an octave, sentences shorten to comms cadence. The warm-neutral face vanishes; what replaces it is not anger but *flat readiness* — the most unsettling expression in his catalog because it is the one with the least signal. He becomes very still between movements. The movements themselves are economical and explosive.

**COMBAT.** Movement is the cleanest expression of him. Footwork from boxing — left lead, weight cycling, no telegraph. Strikes thrown with full hip rotation, retracted fast. Defensive priority over offensive — he prefers to make the opponent miss and then to control. With the wings, the body operates in a vertical plane civilians cannot intuit; he reads three-dimensional space with the bird's-eye overlay and his body trusts the read without checking. He does not shout in combat. He calls comms, calmly, with the same diaphragm he uses for hostage talk-down.

**GRIEF.** Internalizing. Shoulders do not drop; if anything they rise fractionally. Face stills toward neutral, not toward sadness. The regulatory exhale becomes near-continuous. He seeks physical presence — wants to be in a room with people he loves, does not require them to speak. Cries rarely and privately; when he does, it is silent and brief and followed by a long exhale and a return to function. The grief is *metabolized*, not displayed; the cost is paid in sleep and in appetite for the following several days, never in performance.

**JOY.** The Duchenne smile. The head goes back for the laugh. The hand to the chest. He becomes, briefly, the man he would have been if the world had been gentler — and the glimpse is the most valuable somatic data the file contains, because it is the *referent* against which every other state is a deviation.

**INTIMACY (close, trusted).** The slowest version of him. Speech unhurried, gestures large and unselfconscious, the laugh fully released. Sits closer than American social norm; touches without ceremony. The room-sweep does not disengage — it never disengages — but it relaxes its priority. The face he wears in the kitchen with Barnes, on the couch with Misty, on a Harlem stoop with neighbors he has known since before the cape, is the face the surveillance file should treat as *true north*. Every other presentation is calibrated from it.

**EXHAUSTION (chronic).** The most dangerous state for him and the hardest to read. The warm-neutral face holds; the gesture holds; the voice holds. What changes: a longer latency before response, an increased frequency of the regulatory exhale, a tendency to seek high places (the roof, the balcony, altitude generally — the bird's relief), and a withdrawal of disclosure even from his closest people. When Sam goes quiet with the people he loves, the file should mark a code. This is the somatic signature that preceded the shield-relinquishment of 2017 and will precede any future iteration of the same decision.

---

### 6.10 LONGITUDINAL DRIFT

Across the decades on record, the body has *settled* rather than deg


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section VI — Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 1. The Attachment Substrate: What Was Made and What Was Salvaged

The foundational fact of Samuel Wilson's relational life is that he was twice orphaned by violence before adolescence, and twice orphaned in a *specific* configuration: a father killed performing the very act of community repair that Sam would later organize his whole adult life around, and a mother killed in the kind of opportunistic street crime that no act of community repair fully prevents. The structural lesson encoded into the child Sam Wilson was therefore not "the world is unsafe" — that would have been the simpler lesson and would have produced a simpler man — but rather **"the work of making the world safe does not protect you from the world, and it must still be done."** This is the seed of every relational pattern that follows.

By the orthodox developmental schema, double parental loss to violence in latency should produce one of three outcomes: disorganized attachment with adult relational chaos; anxious-preoccupied attachment with clinging and reassurance-seeking; or dismissive-avoidant attachment with the foreclosure of intimacy as a category. Sam presents as none of these. The behavioral record across five decades of canon supports an **earned-secure** classification — the rarest and most clinically interesting outcome, achieved typically when a traumatically-attached child finds, in adolescence or early adulthood, one or more relationships of sufficient durability and corrective quality to reorganize the internal working model. In Sam's case the candidates for that corrective function are his older brother Gideon/Jody (intermittently rendered, but consistently present as a stabilizing male figure), the surrogate-parental adults of the Harlem AME and social-work circuits, and — critically — the pre-canon Riley, the wingman whose loss reorganized Sam's adult relational template into its mature form.

The "earned" in earned-secure is doing real work here. Sam's security is **a practice, not a given.** He behaves securely; he does not feel securely without effort. The difference is observable in the micro-pattern: Sam is the team member who, after a difficult conversation, will check in twenty minutes later with a small unprompted gesture — a hand on the shoulder, a deflecting joke that names the difficulty without re-opening it, a phone call the next morning that pretends to be about logistics. This is *maintenance behavior*. Genuinely secure adults do not perform this much maintenance; they assume the bond will hold. Sam assumes nothing and tends everything. The result *reads* as security to those on the receiving end and *feels* to Sam himself like vigilance dressed as warmth.

---

### 2. The Bonding Pattern: Approach, Naming, Holding

Sam's bonding sequence is unusually legible because it repeats:

**Phase one — approach by inquiry.** Sam opens a relationship by asking a question that is one degree more personal than the situation requires, and then *listening to the answer.* With Steve Rogers in their initial Harlem encounter, the move is to ask about Rogers' actual condition rather than to defer to the legend. With Bucky Barnes, post-Brubaker, the move is to ask about Barnes' present rather than to litigate his past. With Joaquin Torres, the move is to ask what Torres actually wants rather than to assign him a role. With Misty Knight, recurringly, the move is to ask what she has been doing since the last time, in a way that signals he has been thinking about the answer in the interim. The inquiry is not therapeutic — Sam is not playing social-worker — it is *recognitional*. He is telling the other person: I see you as a person before I see you as a function.

**Phase two — naming dynamics aloud.** Within the first several substantive interactions, Sam will articulate the relational dynamic in plain language. "We don't have to pretend this isn't weird." "I'm the new guy, you don't owe me trust yet." "You're going to want me to be your brother and I'm not — I'm something else, and we'll figure out what." This is highly atypical for combat-trained adults in his cohort, who generally communicate relationally by implication and ritual. Sam's verbal explicitness about relational structure is one of his most distinctive signatures, and it functions as a *de-escalation* applied to intimacy itself — the same skill set he uses on hostage-takers, turned inward.

**Phase three — holding through the first failure.** Sam does not test relationships, but he watches for the first failure (the missed call, the operational disagreement, the moment the other person under-performs the role) and he *absorbs it without retaliation* while marking it internally. This is the move that converts an acquaintance into a Wilson-bonded intimate. Once you have failed Sam once and he has held the failure without weaponizing it, you are inside the circle. The circle is small and the entrance criterion is non-obvious because it doesn't look like a test from the outside.

**Phase four — durable, low-maintenance presence with high-bandwidth re-entry.** Sam's bonded relationships do not require constant contact. He can go months without speaking to Misty and re-enter the relationship at full depth in three sentences. He can spend years operating away from Barnes and pick up mid-conversation. This is a hallmark of secure attachment — the working model does not require refresh — and it is one of the few places where Sam's earned security operates with the unselfconsciousness of native security.

---

### 3. Distrust: The Slow, Watchful, Non-Reactive Form

Sam does not distrust loudly. The behavioral signature of Wilson distrust is **increased politeness, decreased self-disclosure, and a quiet expansion of the field of attention to include the suspect party as a tactical variable.** He does not confront, does not withdraw visibly, does not signal. The other party often does not know they have lost his trust. They learn it later when Sam declines an operation that involves them, or routes around them in a planning session, or — most diagnostically — *stops asking them personal questions.* The cessation of inquiry is the tell. When Sam stops asking how you are, he has filed you under operational-only.

Distrust onset triggers, in order of reliability:

1. **Instrumentalization.** Anyone who treats Sam as a means to their end — Gyrich treating him as a diversity quota, the Hauser-style media apparatus treating him as a culture-war prop, Hydra-coded actors trying to position him within their narrative — is filed immediately and durably. The Gyrich resentment ran for decades of in-universe time; Sam does not get over instrumentalization.

2. **Dishonesty about the relational frame.** Sam can absorb operational deception (he is a field operator and understands the necessity); he cannot absorb deception about *what the relationship is.* Rogers' periodic tendency to treat Sam as junior partner while claiming equality has been the longest-running low-grade trust-strain in Sam's adult life, and the only one Sam has ever metabolized into open verbal address.

3. **Harm to a third party in Sam's circle of care.** This is broader than his intimates — it extends to Harlem, to the communities he has pledged to, to anyone who fits the silhouette of his parents in the originating wound. People who hurt the people Sam has positioned himself to protect are not given the slow-watchful treatment; they are simply *out,* permanently, with no available repair path.

4. **Symbolic appropriation against his values.** The Hydra-Cap experience, the Americops co-opting the iconography of public safety, the trafficking of super-soldier serum under nationalist cover — these are not personal betrayals but they engage the same machinery. Sam's distrust extends to *systems* with the same patience and durability it extends to people.

**What Sam does NOT distrust on:** difference of opinion, ideological disagreement, personal weakness, past failure, mental illness, or criminal history. He has functionally infinite tolerance for people who are honest about who they are. The Snap retcon experience — being told his own history was not what he believed — converted Sam permanently into someone who accepts other people's complicated pasts as data rather than as disqualification.

---

### 4. Betrayal: The Asymmetric Ledger

Sam's behavior under betrayal is one of the most distinctive things about him and has no clean analog among Marvel principals. The pattern:

**He does not retaliate.** Across the entire record, there is no instance of Sam taking revenge in the personal sense. Operational consequences yes; personal retaliation no. This is not pacifism — Sam will use force, including lethal force in extremis — it is a deliberate refusal to let the betrayer dictate his subsequent behavior. To retaliate would be to grant the betrayer authorship over Sam's next act, and authorship is the one thing Sam guards absolutely.

**He grieves the relationship, not the self-image.** When Rogers, under Hydra influence, became the inverted version of himself, Sam's expressed pain was about the loss of his friend's selfhood and about what had been done to the symbol, not about his own humiliation at having trusted. This is unusual. Most betrayed adults grieve their own credulity at least as much as the lost relationship; Sam does not, because his self-concept is not staked on having read other people correctly. He knows he can be deceived; the Snap experience taught him that even his own mind can be deceived. He has built his identity downstream of that knowledge.

**He keeps a ledger but does not collect.** Sam remembers betrayals with operational precision — who did what, when, under what conditions — and uses the information to calibrate future trust. He does not, however, pursue the betrayer, lecture them, or reorganize his life around them. The ledger is for safety, not for grievance.

**The single exception: betrayal of his small circle.** When the betrayed party is Barnes, Misty, Torres, or — historically — Rogers, Sam's response shifts from absorption to active pursuit. This is the only context in which his flat escalation pattern produces sustained anger. He will hunt the betrayer of his intimates with a coldness that surprises people who have only seen his warm-approach mode. The relevant micro-tell: Sam's verbal output *drops* in this state. The talker stops talking. Field comms become monosyllabic. This is the most dangerous Sam Wilson behaviorally exists.

---

### 5. Repair: The Patient, Verbal, Iterative Modality

Sam's repair behavior is the most professionally-developed of any relational skill set he possesses, and it is recognizably continuous with his social-work training. The sequence:

**Initiation by acknowledgment, not apology.** Sam opens repair by naming what happened, in operational language, without yet assigning blame or asking for forgiveness. "We left that conversation in a bad place." "I made a call you didn't agree with and I didn't loop you in first." This is the social-worker move: establish shared factual ground before introducing affect.

**Apology with specificity.** When Sam apologizes, he apologizes for the specific act and its specific effect, not for the general state of having failed the other person. He does not over-apologize (which would shift the emotional labor onto the wounded party to absolve him) and he does not under-apologize. The granularity is calibrated to the wound.

**Invitation, not demand, for reciprocal acknowledgment.** Sam will create space for the other party to acknowledge their own contribution but will not require it. If the other party will not engage in mutual repair, Sam will accept the asymmetric repair and continue the relationship at a reduced bandwidth. He does not need both-sides closure to function.

**Behavioral demonstration over verbal reassurance.** After repair conversations, Sam's follow-through is in altered behavior — not in continued verbal processing. He treats repair as a thing that happens *once,* with verbal precision, and is then expressed in subsequent action. He does not re-litigate.

**The Rogers-relationship as case study.** The Sam–Steve bond has survived every conceivable strain — operational disagreement, mantle transfer, the symbolic collapse of Rogers during Secret Empire, the question of who Captain America "really" is — because both men, but Sam in particular, have used this exact repair sequence repeatedly and at scale. The Rogers relationship is the most-tested adult attachment in Sam's record and is, accordingly, the most-developed proof of his repair competence.

---

### 6. Intimacy and Sexual/Romantic Patterns

Sam's romantic record (Leila Taylor in the early period, Misty Knight as the recurrent significant relationship, various intermittent connections) is characterized by **competence without urgency.** He is fully capable of adult sexual intimacy, demonstrates none of the avoidant patterns common in his combat cohort, and forms genuine pair-bonds — but he does not organize his life around romantic partnership the way some of his peers (Barnes' fixation on Natasha; Rogers' on Peggy) do.

The Misty Knight relationship is the longest-running and most diagnostic. It is recurrent rather than continuous, mutually respected, professionally compatible, and characterized by a refusal on both sides to convert it into the conventional structure of partnership. Both partners are highly autonomous operators with deep community commitments; both can re-enter the relationship at depth after long gaps; neither requires the other to perform exclusivity or domesticity. Sam is comfortable in this structure in a way that is unusual for men of his demographic and cohort and that speaks to a real capacity for intimacy without possession.

The pattern across romantic partners:

- **Sam is attracted to operationally competent women with their own communities and missions.** He does not seek partners who will orbit him; he seeks partners who have their own orbits.
- **He does not romance via grand gesture.** His romantic register is the same as his bonding register: questions, listening, the unprompted small gesture, the named dynamic.
- **He does not jealously guard.** Across the record there is no instance of Sam exhibiting possessive behavior toward a partner. This is consistent with his broader refusal to author other people's identities.
- **He has not married, has no children.** This is significant. Sam has built a life full of durable adult bonds without converting any of them into the legal-domestic structure. The most parsimonious read is that **the originating wound — his parents' deaths leaving children behind in a violent world — makes the prospect of fathering children into the operational life he leads psychologically difficult.** He has not articulated this in canon, but the pattern is consistent across decades and is the kind of thing that would not be articulated.

---

### 7. Dependency: The Asymmetry That Defines Him

Sam is **trusted with the dependency of others and reluctant to express his own.** This is the single most consistent asymmetry in his relational life and is the closest thing to a clinical concern in his otherwise healthy attachment profile.

He is the team member to whom others go with their pain. Rogers brings him grief about Peggy, about Bucky, about the lost century. Barnes brings him the Winter Soldier years. Torres brings him the uncertainty of new mantle-bearing. Misty brings him the specific exhaustion of being a Black woman superhero. In each case Sam receives the dependency with skill, capacity, and apparent ease.

His own dependency expression is **rationed.** Sam will admit fatigue, will admit fear in operationally-relevant contexts, will admit uncertainty about decisions. He will not generally admit need. He has no equivalent confidant — no one to whom he routinely brings his own pain in the way others bring theirs to him. The closest approximations are Misty (who gets some of it, in the relational mode) and, increasingly in the post-Coates period, Barnes (who gets the operational-existential subset of it).

The originating mechanism is over-determined: childhood loss taught him that the people he depends on can be taken from him; the social-work training taught him to position himself as the helper; the racialized role-strain of his public identity makes vulnerable self-disclosure carry additional cost (a Black Captain America who admits weakness will have that weakness weaponized in ways a white predecessor would not). The result is a man whose dependency capacity is intact but under-exercised, and who occasionally manifests this as the late-stage symptom of *withdrawal* rather than *request* — the shield surrender of 2017 being the canonical example. When Sam needs help, he is more likely to leave the role than to ask for support within it.

This is the one place a clinician would push him. Sam's earned-secure functioning is robust under most loads, but the under-exercised dependency capacity means that his catastrophic-load response is to step out rather than to lean in, and the cost of that response — to him, to the role, to the people who depended on him in the role — is real.

---

### 8. The Relational Template, Repeated

Across every significant relationship in Sam's adult life — Rogers, Barnes, Torres, Misty, Riley (pre-canon), the Harlem community broadly, the rotating cast of social-work clients, the Avengers as institution, the country as object of service — the same template recurs:

1. **Approach by recognition.** See the other as a person before a function.
2. **Verbal explicitness about the relational structure.** Name what this is.
3. **Absorb the first failure without retaliation, mark it internally.**
4. **Tend the bond with low-frequency, high-quality maintenance.**
5. **Carry the other's dependency; ration your own.**
6. **Under strain, increase work and decrease complaint.**
7. **When the structural conditions of the relationship become untenable, withdraw from the role rather than from the person.**
8. **Repair, when offered the chance, with operational acknowledgment, calibrated apology, and behavioral demonstration.**
9. **Do not retaliate. Keep the ledger for safety, not grievance.**
10. **Refuse to author the other's identity, and require the same in return.**

The template scales: it works on Steve Rogers and it works on a Harlem teenager Sam has known for twenty minutes. It works on Barnes and it works on the United States of America. It is the operational expression of a man who has decided, against the evidence of his early life, that the work of making safe places is still worth doing, and that the doing of it requires a particular discipline of relational craft — patient, verbal, non-possessive, non-retaliatory, and quietly, persistently warm.

The cost of the template is that Sam carries more than he is carried. The gift of the template is that the relationships built within it are among the most durable in the Marvel record, and that the man inside them — interrogated, examined, never restful — has nonetheless built a life in which he is genuinely loved by people who know him, and in which he has learned, over decades, to let some of that love land.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section 6 — Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

The defensive architecture of Samuel Thomas Wilson is, by any clinical taxonomy, *unusually mature* — and the maturity is itself the diagnostic finding. A man with his trauma load (double childhood violent bereavement, iatrogenic identity overwrite, fifty operational years of combat exposure, chronic racialized role-strain) ought to present a defensive profile dominated by splitting, projection, reaction formation, and dissociative numbing. He does not. The profile is dominated by humor, sublimation, anticipation, altruism, suppression, and affiliation — Vaillant's Level IV register almost across the board, with a small but real strand of Level III (neurotic) compensations and a vanishingly small Level II (immature) residue confined to specific provocations. This section maps the architecture in full: every mechanism, ranked from most primitive to most mature, with the behavioral signatures by which each can be observed in the field.

---

### I. Level I — Pathological / Psychotic Defenses

**Effectively absent.** No record of delusional projection, psychotic denial, or distortion of consensus reality, even under the most reality-warping provocations of his career (the Cosmic Cube alteration of his memories being the obvious test case). The remarkable feature is that when his reality *was* directly assaulted by the Skull's Cube-implanted personality, his post-recovery response was not psychotic denial of the violation — he did not insist the false memories had been true, nor that the discovery itself was a lie. He metabolized the breach. This is the inverse of the psychotic-register response and is the strongest single piece of evidence for the structural integrity of his ego.

---

### II. Level II — Immature Defenses

The immature register is the smallest portion of Sam's architecture, but not zero. It exists in narrow, identifiable bands.

**Passive aggression — trace, situational.** Observable almost exclusively in interactions with institutional authority that he experiences as illegitimate. The Gyrich Avengers tenure is the cleanest specimen: rather than refusing the seat outright, Sam took it, occupied it visibly, and performed the role in a manner that made the affirmative-action premise impossible to ignore — then quit. This is functional passive-aggression in service of a moral point, and it recurs whenever Sam is placed in a structural position he considers compromised but cannot, for community-protective reasons, simply walk away from. With S.H.I.E.L.D. under the surveillance-state arc of the Spencer era he ran the same pattern in slower motion: visible compliance, escalating quiet non-cooperation, eventual public departure on documented principle.

**Acting out — virtually absent.** Sam does not punch walls, does not drink, does not vanish for weeks, does not start fights he could have avoided. The closest thing to acting-out in the canon is his pattern of *unilateral mission departures* during periods of moral disagreement with a team — leaving without negotiating, working the case alone. This is at the edge between acting-out (immature) and **counter-dependence under stress** (neurotic), and is best classified as the latter.

**Projection — negligible.** Sam is unusually disciplined about not attributing his internal states to others. The single area where projection-coded behavior appears is racial: he sometimes attributes specific racialized intent where the data supports only structural racialized effect. Even here, the pattern reads less as projection than as Bayesian priors operating on a lifetime of confirmed instances — closer to *calibrated suspicion* than to defense.

**Splitting — explicitly resisted.** This is one of the most diagnostically rich features of his architecture. Sam refuses, repeatedly and on the record, to split — refuses to render Rogers all-good or all-bad even when Rogers (Hydra-coded, post-resurrection, ideologically diverged) gives him every reason to; refuses to render the federal apparatus all-bad even after S.H.I.E.L.D. breaks his trust; refuses to render his own history all-Snap or all-Sam after the Cube revelation. The integrative work is *deliberate*. He talks his way past splits the way other operators talk themselves out of vertigo.

**Fantasy / autistic withdrawal — absent.** No retreat into imaginary worlds, no escapism. Even Sam's most withdrawn period (post-shield-relinquishment) was spent doing concrete community work, not in fantasy.

**Somatization — absent in canon, though the orthopedic load is so cumulative that the line between somatization and genuine post-traumatic embodiment is blurred.** What is *not* present is conversion-style symptom expression — Sam's body tells the truth of what it has been put through; it does not narrate his feelings for him.

---

### III. Level III — Neurotic Defenses

The neurotic register is where Sam's *negative* compensations live. These are the costs of the otherwise-healthy architecture, and they are real.

**Intellectualization under acute stress.** When frightened, grieving, or operating in conditions of high uncertainty, Sam's speech register shifts measurably. He moves from his characteristic warm, idiomatic, room-reading conversational style into clipped tactical/operational language — distances, vectors, evacuation routes, contingencies. The shift is observable in every major crisis sequence and is the cleanest single field-tell that he is internally activated. It is adaptive (it stabilizes team cognition, keeps the field calm) but it also functions as affect-binding: he holds feeling at one remove by handling its operational correlates first.

**Isolation of affect.** Closely paired with intellectualization. Sam can speak about the deaths of his parents, the Snap revelation, the betrayals of trusted figures, and the somatic toll of his career in measured, articulate prose — and the articulateness itself is the defense. The feelings are not denied; they are decoupled from the moment of speaking about them. This is why Sam is so easy to interview and so hard to fully *read* — he gives you the content without giving you the live affect attached to it.

**Reaction formation — minor, in one specific zone.** Sam's *warmth toward institutions that have wronged him* sometimes runs slightly hotter than the data warrants. He extends benefit-of-the-doubt to the federal apparatus, to media institutions, and to the symbol of the shield itself a fraction longer than his own analytical capacities should permit. This is not the classical reaction-formation of repressed hostility expressed as exaggerated kindness — it is closer to a *willed* generosity, a refusal to let the other party's worst behavior dictate his own. But the structural shape is reaction-formation-adjacent and produces a recurring vulnerability: he is repeatedly hurt by parties whose capacity to hurt him he had clear evidence of in advance.

**Displacement — minor.** Sam occasionally displaces frustration with structural systems onto proximate operational obstacles — running missions harder than the mission warranted because the larger fight is unwinnable in the moment. This is observable in the Americops arc and in several Symbol of Truth sequences.

**Repression — selective, narrow.** The Snap material is the obvious zone. Even after integration, Sam does not voluntarily return to the content of those implanted memories; he has metabolized the *fact* of the violation without rehearsing the *substance* of it. This is functional repression — keeping the door closed on material that does not need to be processed further to be lived with.

**Counter-dependence under stress.** When Sam doubts whether he can rely on a system or partnership, his characteristic response is not to ask for more support but to require less of it. This is the negative shadow of his earned-secure attachment style: under sufficient strain, the security tilts toward self-sufficiency rather than toward asking. It is why his crises tend to be invisible until they manifest as a decision already taken (the shield surrender, the Avengers resignation, the unilateral missions). His circle finds out he was struggling *after* he has reorganized to handle it alone.

**The over-functioning compensation.** Catalogued in the shared assessment and worth expanding here as a neurotic-register pattern: when Sam doubts his right to a role, he *increases his investment in it* rather than renegotiating its terms. This is a compensation that wears the mask of virtue (and produces a great deal of real virtue) but is structurally a defense — it substitutes work for the harder act of demanding the conditions under which the work would be sustainable. The cost is paid in body (the cumulative orthopedic load), in sleep (across the Spencer run, observable degradation), and ultimately in the periodic forced withdrawals when the over-functioning becomes untenable.

**Undoing — minor.** After missions in which civilians have been harmed, Sam shows a recurrent pattern of returning to the affected community in non-costumed capacity — sometimes for days, sometimes as ongoing case work. This is partly genuine social-work practice and partly undoing: a symbolic reversal of the harm by physical re-presence in the place of the harm. The two are not separable in him, which is itself the point.

---

### IV. Level IV — Mature Defenses

This is the dominant register and the explanation for the otherwise-improbable functional integrity of the subject.

**Humor — the master defense.** Across every writer, every era, every team configuration, Sam is the verbal-wit anchor of the room. The humor is *generative* rather than *defensive-bitter*: it does not cut, it does not deflect from genuine engagement, it does not punch down. It functions to (a) lower threat in tense rooms, (b) signal his presence as a person rather than a symbol, (c) regulate his own arousal in high-stakes situations, and (d) maintain his recognizability to himself as the man he wants to be in the moment. The humor is also *racially located* in a deliberate way — Sam draws on Black American comedic traditions (signifying, capping, the well-timed dry observation) and does not code-switch out of them for white teammates or institutional settings. This is humor as identity maintenance and humor as defense, simultaneously.

**Sublimation — the structural defense.** The entire shape of Sam's adult life is a sublimation pattern: the helplessness of the child who watched his father die trying to break up a neighborhood fight is sublimated into (a) the social work career, (b) the superheroic career, and (c) the de-escalator role he plays on every team he joins. Sublimation here is so thoroughgoing that the sublimated material has become indistinguishable from his vocational identity — he is the person who makes places safer because his earliest places were not, and the work has consumed and transmuted the original wound rather than merely channeling it.

**Altruism — Vaillantian, genuine.** Distinguished from reaction-formation altruism (which is hostility masquerading as care) by its quality of *easeful exchange*: Sam gets visible satisfaction from his other-directed work without that satisfaction shading into self-congratulation or martyrdom. He is willing to receive care as well as give it (with Misty, with Rogers, with Torres in moments of role reversal), which is the diagnostic line between mature altruism and the pseudo-altruism of the compulsively self-sacrificing.

**Anticipation — characteristic and unusually developed.** Sam is the team member most likely to have already thought about what happens after the mission — extraction logistics, civilian re-entry, press handling, the next operational pivot. This is observable in his bird's-eye tactical preferences (he is *looking ahead* of the field, not just above it) and in his interpersonal pattern (he anticipates the conversations that will be needed, often initiating them before others have realized they are necessary). Anticipation functions defensively by binding the anxiety of uncertainty to concrete preparatory work; functionally, it makes him the most reliable operational planner in any room.
