**Suppression — the most underrated of his defenses.** Sam can *choose to set something aside until later*, and the setting-aside is genuine and reversible rather than repressive. He can park the Snap material, the racial fatigue, the body's accumulated complaints, and the question of his right to the shield, work the mission in front of him, and come back to the parked material in conditions of safety. This is the defense most responsible for his combat composure: he does not need to *not feel* the threat in order to function; he can feel it, hold it, and set it down for the duration of the operation.

**Affiliation — the relational defense.** Under stress Sam moves *toward* his small circle rather than away from it (this is the inverse of his counter-dependence pattern, which obtains only when he doubts the circle's capacity to bear the weight). Affiliation here means: actively seeking the company of Rogers, Barnes, Misty, Torres in periods of strain; using shared work as a regulatory mechanism; processing aloud rather than alone where possible. The affiliation defense is what protects against the counter-dependence pattern in most ordinary stress conditions.

**Self-observation.** Sam is consistently and accurately self-aware — able to name his own patterns, motives, and reactions in real time and in retrospect. This is rare at his operational level (most career operators show measurable degradation of self-observational capacity over time) and is one of the protective factors against the over-functioning pattern: he can see himself doing it, which gives him at least the option of stopping.

---

### V. Compensatory Architecture — Positive

**The vocational double.** Social work and superheroism are not separate careers; they are the same compensation expressed at two scales. The social work grounds the superheroism in concrete community and prevents the costumed work from becoming purely symbolic; the superheroism gives the social work a wider operational radius. Each protects against the failure modes of the other (the social worker's burnout; the hero's grandiosity).

**The dyad preference.** Sam's best functioning is in pairs — with Rogers, with Barnes, with Misty, with Torres. The dyad is a compensatory structure: it gives him the partnership that his early life lost (parents, then for years no one), it externalizes the self-observation function (a partner who can name what he is doing), and it provides the affiliation channel that his suppression and over-functioning would otherwise close off. When forced into structural solitude — lone Black Avenger, lone Black Captain America — the compensation fails and the costs surface.

**Verbal articulation as regulation.** Sam *talks*. He names dynamics out loud, he says the thing others are circling, he closes field comms with explicit reassurance. The articulation is regulatory: language binds affect, and Sam's facility with language is one of his strongest affect-regulation tools. This is why his crises take the form of *measured withdrawal statements* rather than ruptures — he can put the crisis into words before it has to put itself into action.

**The bird's-eye cognitive style as defense.** The avian sensory channel and the gestalt tactical preference it correlates with serve a defensive function as well as an operational one: seeing the whole board reduces the anxiety of partial information, contextualizes immediate threats within larger systems, and supports the de-escalation preference that keeps him out of the rage-state pathway entirely. The flight rig is, among other things, a regulatory device.

**Community as external ego.** Harlem, and more broadly Black America, function as an external reference structure against which Sam can check his self-concept. When the larger institutional apparatus tries to tell him who he is, he has a community-located self-concept to check the claim against. This is one of the protective factors against the identity-overwrite vulnerability that the Snap experience exposed.

---

### VI. Compensatory Architecture — Negative

**Over-functioning as identity insurance.** Already described above; the dominant negative compensation. It produces virtue at the cost of sustainability and is the single mechanism most likely to engineer the next forced withdrawal.

**Absorption of structural disrespect.** Sam absorbs and processes internally the slights, micro-aggressions, and structural disrespects of his racialized public role rather than expressing them outward or negotiating them at the source. This is partly suppression (mature), partly intellectualization (neurotic), and partly a compensation for the historical absence of safe channels for that expression. The cost is cumulative — the racial battle fatigue that ended his first Captain America tenure is the metabolic byproduct.

**Conditional service as the only available "no."** Because Sam over-functions rather than renegotiates, his only structural lever for refusal is *to leave the role entirely*. He cannot say "I will stay if you change these conditions"; he can only say "I am leaving because the conditions are these." This is a binary that costs him roles he would otherwise want to keep and produces the resignation-shaped crisis pattern.

**The pre-emptive solitude.** When Sam doubts the circle can bear the weight of a particular stressor, he reorganizes alone *before* asking — and the asking, once foreclosed, is rarely re-opened. This costs him support he could have had, and it costs the circle the chance to know him at the depth he is capable of being known at. Misty Knight has named this pattern; Rogers has named it; Sam himself has named it. The naming has not eliminated it.

**The body as the line of last resort.** Sam compensates for being unenhanced by training harder, planning better, and accepting more risk per fight than an enhanced operator would need to. The compensation is operationally effective and somatically catastrophic. The body is paying the bill for the rest of the defensive architecture.

---

### VII. The Architecture as a Whole

The synthesis: Sam Wilson's defensive system is built on a Level IV foundation (humor, sublimation, altruism, anticipation, suppression, affiliation, self-observation), reinforced by a Level III neurotic register (intellectualization, isolation of affect, over-functioning, counter-dependence under stress, mild reaction-formation toward wounding institutions), and almost entirely free of Level II and Level I material. The dominant negative compensation — over-functioning as identity insurance — is the price paid for the integrity of the rest of the system, and it expresses itself in the periodic forced withdrawals that punctuate his career.

The architecture's distinctive feature is its *deliberateness*. Most subjects with comparable defensive maturity arrived there through favorable developmental conditions; Sam arrived there through what reads as a sustained, conscious practice of choosing the mature defense over the available primitive one — choosing humor over bitterness, sublimation over acting-out, integration over splitting, articulation over withdrawal, again and again, in conditions that would have justified the worse choice each time. The defensive system is, in this sense, not a structure he inherited but a structure he *built*, and continues to maintain, and occasionally has to rebuild after sections of it collapse under load.

This is why the system fails the way it does — not by decomposition but by exhaustion. The defenses do not break; the man running them gets tired. And when he gets tired, he sets the work down, goes home to the community that grounds him, and begins, with characteristic patience, the slow process of picking it back up.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section 6 — Longitudinal Psychological Profile

A decade-by-decade clinical reconstruction. The frame is integrative: attachment theory (Bowlby/Main/Hesse, with Mikulincer & Shaver's adult extensions), Vaillant's defense maturation hierarchy, Linehan's affect-regulation dimensions, Marcia's identity-status model (with McAdams' narrative-identity extension for adult re-authorship), and — where racialized role-strain becomes load-bearing — the racial-battle-fatigue and John Henryism literatures (Smith; Sherman James). The intent is not to retro-fit pathology but to track the *trajectory* of a psyche that has, against the actuarial odds, ended up more integrated than it began.

---

### 6.1 Childhood and Pre-Operational Adolescence (pre-1969 baseline, reconstructed)

The two foundational events are non-negotiable across every continuity: Paul Wilson killed trying to intervene in a neighborhood fight; Darlene Wilson murdered in a mugging roughly two years later. Sam is, by every available timeline, school-aged for the first loss and pre-adolescent for the second. This is the textbook substrate for **disorganized attachment** in Main & Solomon's sense — caregiver-as-source-of-safety and caregiver-as-source-of-terror collapsed into the same memory architecture — and the actuarial prediction would be a constellation of externalizing behavior, identity diffusion, and a high probability of either substance recruitment or street-system recruitment by mid-adolescence.

The "Snap" retcon, taken at face value, is precisely that actuarial outcome: the boy who *should* have come out of those losses became a street operator. Whether one accepts the retcon or treats it as later-walked-back, it functions as the **counterfactual self** Sam has carried internally for his entire adult life — the version of him that the losses *would have* produced absent some intervening factor. Clinically, this is significant regardless of metaphysical status: Sam has organized his adult identity in opposition to a person he believes he could have been.

The intervening factor in the canonical (non-Snap) telling is **sibling and community holding** — Sarah, the older brother figure, the residue of the church Paul Wilson served — which provides Bowlby's "secondary attachment figures" and explains the eventual emergence of an earned-secure baseline. The cognitive style observable already in late adolescence is *vigilant-relational*: Sam reads rooms because rooms have hurt him.

Affect-regulation in this period is best inferred from its later sequelae. The adult Sam's near-total absence of explosive aggression suggests that the childhood adaptation was **internalizing rather than externalizing** — the loss was processed as sadness organized into responsibility, not as rage organized into retaliation. This is unusual and prognostically favorable; it likely reflects the modeling of Paul Wilson (a minister who died *de-escalating*, not retaliating) as the introjected paternal object.

Self-concept at entry to adulthood: **identity foreclosure under traumatic pressure**, in Marcia's terms — a committed identity (helper, protector, community-anchored) adopted without the moratorium phase, because moratorium is a luxury the doubly-bereaved cannot afford. This is the seed of the later interrogation: the identity was *taken on* before it was *examined*, and the examination would have to happen across decades.

---

### 6.2 The Long Falcon Decade (1969–c. 1979): Sublimation Under Construction

The Lee/Colan introduction shows Sam in mid-twenties as a working social worker partnered with Rogers. The affective signature of this period — across Lee, Englehart, Gerber — is **bright, verbally generative, warm-approach**, with humor used as social lubricant rather than as armor. This is the *constructed* Sam: pre-Snap-reveal, pre-Gyrich, the version that believes its own self-presentation without yet having had it interrogated.

Defenses are predominantly **mature but underexercised**. Sublimation is the dominant mechanism: the social work career and the costumed work are continuous rather than compensatory — Sam is doing the same job in two registers. Humor is present but not yet load-bearing; it has not been forced into the defensive role it will occupy in later decades. Altruism is genuine and somewhat naive — Sam in this period believes that doing the work is sufficient, that recognition and integration will follow effort.

Cognitive style is already gestalt and field-dependent, but its tactical sophistication is still developing. The Redwing-mediated spatial sense is operative but not yet fully integrated into a strategic worldview; Sam in 1971 uses the bird's-eye to find people, not yet to *understand* situations.

Self-concept is foreclosed-stable: Sam knows who he is, has not yet been forced to defend it. The first cracks appear in the early-to-mid '70s as Englehart and Gerber begin to write the racial subtext of the partnership explicitly — Sam noticing, in print, that the press treats him as ornament. The affect shifts subtly: a base rate of low-level **chronic role-strain** enters the record, manifest as a flattening of the early-period brightness into something more wry.

**The 1975 rupture (the Snap reveal):** clinically, this is the defining iatrogenic event of Sam's adult life. The subjective experience as written — being told that one's entire personality is the product of malevolent telepathic engineering — should produce, by any standard nosology, an acute dissociative episode or psychotic-spectrum response. What Sam exhibits instead is *interrogative stabilization*: he absorbs the information, tests it against his lived experience, refuses both full acceptance and full denial, and continues to function. This is the first observable instance of the adaptive pattern that will define him — **examination as homeostasis**. The Snap reveal does not break him because it activates a defense (cognitive examination of self) that turns out to be his strongest one.

---

### 6.3 The Avengers Stint and Late-'70s Reconfiguration (c. 1979–1985): First Encounter with Structural Disrespect

The Gyrich affirmative-action placement (*Avengers* #183–184) is the second formative role-strain event after the Snap reveal, and the first in which the strain is *structural* rather than *personal*. Sam's behavioral response — completing the assignment competently, articulating the indignity privately, and quitting on his own terms — is a clinical demonstration of what will become his canonical escalation pattern: **flat affect under provocation, decisive withdrawal at the threshold**.

This period marks the maturation of humor into a **load-bearing defense**. Pre-Gyrich, Sam's humor was social; post-Gyrich, it acquires the secondary function of *naming the absurd in real time*, which is the verbal-defense profile of long-term Black professionals in white-dominated institutional spaces. The shift is small in any single panel but unmistakable across the decade.

Self-concept enters its first genuine **moratorium** phase — Marcia's term for active examination of a previously foreclosed identity. Sam is now consciously asking what he is doing, for whom, and at what cost. The Priest run a quarter-century later will retrospectively read this period as the origin of Sam's adult skepticism toward institutional symbolism.

Affect regulation in this period is *consolidating*. The Linehan-frame analysis: Sam's distress tolerance is high, his emotional regulation is intact, his interpersonal effectiveness is excellent, and his mindfulness (in the technical sense of present-moment, non-judgmental awareness) is *increasing* — a function, likely, of years of social-work practice combined with the bird's-eye cognitive overlay.

---

### 6.4 The Long Plateau (c. 1985–2004): Integrated Functioning, Quiet Costs

This is the least dramatized period of Sam's life and clinically the most informative *as baseline*. Across the Gruenwald/late-Bronze/early-modern runs, Sam operates at sustained high function: Harlem-based casework, intermittent Avengers and team-up work, the long arc of his relationship with Leila Taylor, the rotating but durable partnership with Rogers. There is no decompensation, no major depressive episode, no withdrawal from role.

The psychological signature of the plateau is **adaptive over-functioning**. Sam carries more than he is asked to, processes more than he discloses, and metabolizes the chronic racial and operational strain through an increasingly disciplined private practice: physical conditioning, the Redwing link, and what appears in scattered panels to be a reflective/contemplative practice that is never fully named but is consistent with the inheritance of his father's ministerial training (the introjected Paul Wilson again).

Cognitively, the bird's-eye is now fully integrated. Sam in this period is reliably the *first* team member to identify civilian endangerment, the first to call for evacuation, and the first to articulate the second-order consequences of a tactical choice. This is not just augmented sense; it is **trained perception** — twenty years of seeing high places from above has trained a cortical pattern of contextual prioritization that is observable even when the wings are off.

Self-concept settles into a stable but *examined* form. The Snap question is not resolved; it is **shelved**. This is itself a clinical achievement — Sam has learned to operate without requiring metaphysical certainty about his own authorship. McAdams' narrative-identity frame is the right tool: Sam has constructed a personal myth in which the Snap is an *episode* rather than the *theme*, which keeps it from organizing the rest of the story.

The quiet cost, visible only in retrospect: the plateau is sustained at the price of **never fully asking the question the Spencer run will eventually force**. Sam in 1992 has decided not to ask whether the work is *worth* what it costs him. He is still operating in the foreclosure that examination had begun to crack in 1979.

---

### 6.5 The Priest Run and the Articulation Era (c. 2004–2010): Naming the Wound

Priest's *Captain America and the Falcon* vol. 2 is the period in which Sam's racialized role-strain is for the first time given *first-person articulation* on the page. Clinically, this corresponds to a profound shift: the chronic load that had been carried as background noise for thirty years becomes available to conscious processing.

This is the second moratorium phase and the more productive one. Sam in the Priest period does not destabilize despite explicitly examining material that had been shelved for decades — a finding consistent with the earned-secure attachment read and with the maturation of his defense profile. The capacity to look directly at one's own structural position without decompensating is the marker of high integration.

Affect in this period is at its most *layered*. Sam is simultaneously warmer in close dyads and more astringent in public, which is the affective signature of someone who has stopped pretending the public reception is what he wants it to be. The broken-back arc and the cumulative operational trauma begin to be visible in body — a slight increase in the deliberation of movement, a more conservative engagement style — but never in mood.

Cognitive style sharpens into its mature form: **systemic, longitudinal, suspicious of the discrete event**. Sam in this period is the team member who asks who benefits from a crisis, not just how to end it. This is the cognitive infrastructure that will later make him incompatible with S.H.I.E.L.D.'s threat-response paradigm.

---

### 6.6 Brubaker / Remender Transition (c. 2005–2014): Loss, Stewardship, Succession

The Rogers "death" in *Civil War* and its aftermath place Sam in a sustained role as **steward of an absent center**. Clinically, this is the period in which his attachment system is most directly stressed at the peer level — the loss of the primary adult attachment figure of his adult life — and the response is, again, *non-decompensating*: grief is metabolized, the work continues, the relationship with Barnes is constructed rather than refused.

This is one of the most prognostically important data points in the file. The standard finding in adult bereavement research is that the loss of a primary peer attachment in midlife is the single highest predictor of depressive onset in previously-asymptomatic adults. Sam does not decompensate. The mechanism appears to be the **distributed attachment portfolio** he has built over the plateau decades — Misty, Sarah and surviving family, the Harlem network, the broader Avengers — which functions as the protective factor Bowlby and later Mikulincer & Shaver identify as the chief buffer against complicated grief.

The Remender transition to the shield (2014) is a clinical event of a different kind: the **assignment of symbolic weight to a previously distributed identity**. Sam takes the shield from a position of consent but not eagerness. This consent-without-eagerness is the signature of his entire post-2014 trajectory and is the precondition for the Spencer-era crisis.

---

### 6.7 The Spencer Era (2015–2017): The First Authentic Decompensation, and Its Form

This is the period that finally tests the limits of the system, and the result is clinically definitive: when Sam's regulation finally breaks, the symptom is **withdrawal from role, not aggression, not depression, not dissociation**.

The clinical picture across the Spencer run:

- **Hypervigilance** to racialized criticism reaches operational ceiling. Sam is now monitoring three simultaneous threat streams (operational, political, reputational) and the cognitive load is observable in his increasingly terse field comms.
- **Sleep and appetite**: not depicted as compromised, which is itself diagnostic — full racial battle fatigue syndromes usually show somatic break-through by this load. Sam's somatic regulation holds, which speaks to extraordinary baseline robustness.
- **Mood**: not depressed in the clinical sense. There is no anhedonia, no hopelessness, no psychomotor slowing. There is *moral exhaustion*, which is a different phenomenon and is best captured by the **moral injury** literature (Litz et al.): the experience of being required to act in ways that violate one's moral framework, in this case the framework being that a Captain America must be allowed to be Captain America by the country he serves.
- **Cognitive function**: intact and, if anything, sharper. Sam in late Spencer is making correct second-order assessments under conditions that would degrade most operators' decision quality.
- **The decision to relinquish**: not impulsive, not depressive, not retaliatory. It is the **considered withdrawal of consent** from a role whose conditions have become incompatible with the actor's integrity. This is the most psychiatrically health-indicative response possible to moral-injury saturation.

The Spencer crisis is the moment at which Sam's lifelong pattern of *examination as homeostasis* meets a condition it cannot examine away. The response — putting the symbol down — is the same pattern he showed in 1979 with Gyrich, scaled up to the highest-stakes role he has ever held. Continuity is total.

---

### 6.8 Coates and the Re-Acceptance (2018–2021): Earned Re-Authorship

The Coates period is, clinically, the **post-traumatic growth** phase in the technical sense (Tedeschi & Calhoun). The hallmarks are all present: revised priorities, deepened interpersonal relationships, increased sense of personal strength specifically grounded in having survived the prior crisis, and — most importantly — a *changed relationship to the meaning of the role* rather than a return to the prior relationship.

Sam in this period re-takes the Captain America identity with full awareness that the role will continue to cost what it cost before. The change is not in the role; it is in the **internal contract** with the role. McAdams' narrative-identity frame again: Sam has re-authored the personal myth so that the role is now an *expression* of his identity rather than a *test* of it. This is the difference between identity *foreclosure* (1971), identity *moratorium* (1979, 2004, 2016), and identity *achievement* in Marcia's full sense — a committed identity arrived at through genuine examination.

Affect in this period is *settled*. The brightness of the early Falcon years and the astringency of the Priest years coexist now without contradiction. Humor is at its most generative — load-bearing without being defensive.

Cognitive style is at its mature ceiling. The gestalt/bird's-eye/systems-thinking pattern that has been developing for forty in-universe years is now reflexive.

Self-concept: **examined, durable, and — for the first time — restful in a non-defensive way**. Sam in this period can sit inside the role without having to constantly defend his right to sit there, because he has done the defending and is no longer asking the question for someone else's benefit.

---

### 6.9 The Onyebuchi / Symbol of Truth Period (2022–): Mentoring, Internationalization, Eldership

The current-record Sam is in early eldership — the developmental phase Erikson frames as *generativity vs. stagnation*, and Sam is unambiguously on the generative side. The Torres mentorship is the clinical center: Sam is now the figure Rogers was for him, and the mentoring style — patient, developmental, willing to let Torres fail safely — is the inverse of the role-strain Sam himself experienced under Gyrich. This is **reparative parenting in the workplace**, in the object-relations sense: Sam is providing for Torres the institutional holding he was denied.

The internationalization of the role — Wakanda, the global super-soldier trade — corresponds to a final widening of the cognitive aperture. Sam is now consistently thinking at the scale of *systems of harm* rather than *instances of harm*, which is the cognitive end-state of a forty-year trajectory from social-work casework through Harlem-bounded operations through national symbol-bearing.

Affect regulation in this period is best characterized as **post-decompensation equilibrium**: a man who has been to his own breaking point, has named what broke him, has set down what he needed to set down, has picked back up what he chose to pick back up, and is now operating with the unusual freedom of someone who knows the conditions under which he will stop.

The remaining vulnerabilities are clear and bounded: community legitimacy (criticism from Harlem still lands hardest), partnership integrity (betrayal in the small circle remains the genuine anger trigger), and the body (he is still the Captain America who can die, and the cumulative orthopedic load is a real long-horizon risk). None of these are pathological; all are the realistic load lines of a non-augmented man in a decades-long high-violence operational role.

---

### 6.10 Trajectory Synthesis

The decade-by-decade arc is, structurally, a **slow movement from foreclosed identity to achieved identity, mediated by repeated cycles of moratorium that each previous decade's adaptation had partially prepared him for**. The Snap reveal would have broken a less-prepared psyche; it didn't, because the social-work years had built the examination muscle. The Gyrich strain would have produced cynicism in a less-anchored psyche; it didn't, because the Harlem and Rogers attachments held. The Rogers loss would have produced complicated grief in a less-distributed attachment portfolio; it didn't, because the plateau decades had built the network. The Spencer moral injury *did* produce decompensation — but the decompensation took the form of considered withdrawal because forty years of internalizing-not-externalizing affect regulation had built no other pathway. The Coates re-acceptance was possible because the Spencer withdrawal had been clean.

Each decade's adaptation was the precondition for surviving the next decade's stressor. The cumulative effect, observable in the current-record Sam, is the rarest finding in this kind of file: a subject whose **trajectory is monotonically toward integration**, in a population (combat-trauma-exposed, childhood-bereaved, chronically racially-strained adults) where the modal trajectory is the reverse.

The clinical bottom line is the one the Shared Assessment opens with and the longitudinal record only deepens: Sam Wilson's psychological health is not a baseline. It is an *achievement*, sustained decade by decade by a discipline of self-examination that has, against the actuarial odds, produced a man more whole at sixty-plus published years than he was at twenty-five.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION 6 — PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

---

### 6.1 Framing the Question

The psychiatric question this file must answer is not "what is wrong with Samuel Wilson" but "what *should* be wrong, given the etiological load, and why isn't it." A subject with this exposure profile — double parental homicide before adolescence, decades of high-lethality combat, induced dissociative trauma at the hands of a malign telepathic operator, chronic minority-status role-strain in nationally visible institutional spaces — should, on actuarial grounds, present with at minimum a chronic PTSD picture, probable comorbid depressive disorder, elevated substance-use risk, and a non-trivial probability of personality-level pathology in the cluster B or C range. The behavioral record across approximately five decades of canonical observation supports *none* of those diagnoses at threshold.

The clinically interesting findings are therefore (a) the **sub-threshold** trauma signature, (b) the **specific shape** of his stress-related cognitive load, and (c) the **mechanisms of compensation** that hold the picture together. This section maps each in turn, then runs a long differential against the diagnoses he most resembles but does not meet.

---

### 6.2 Etiology — The Load on the System

**Developmental layer (childhood, ages ~9–11).** Father Paul Wilson killed intervening in street violence; mother Darlene murdered in a mugging approximately two years later. The clinically significant features of this exposure are not only the events but their *configuration*: (1) both parents lost to community violence, in the community itself; (2) the father's death encodes the lesson that *protective intervention is fatal*; (3) the mother's death encodes the lesson that *protective intervention may also be insufficient — the world keeps killing afterward*; (4) the temporal spacing (two years) prevented integration of the first loss before the second arrived, producing what the developmental-trauma literature terms a *complicated* rather than *complex* bereavement substrate. Adverse Childhood Experiences (ACE) analog score: minimum 4, plausibly 6 once economic disruption and serial caregiving instability are counted.

**Adolescent/early-adult layer.** The Snap retcon, regardless of one's authorial position on its canonical status, must be assessed in the file as *something Sam subjectively lived through* — a period of street activity in Harlem and Los Angeles operating as an enforcer/hustler, followed by the imposed-personality interval, followed by recovery of original memory. From a phenomenological-psychiatric standpoint this is functionally equivalent to a long dissociative fugue terminated by abrupt re-integration with full retrospective awareness. The iatrogenic insult — a hostile actor weaponizing a Cosmic Cube to author a false self — is, in psychiatric history, without close analog; the nearest comparators are severe cult-deprogramming cases and certain prolonged-captivity scenarios (Herman's *complex trauma* framing).

**Adult operational layer (1969–present in-universe).** Decades of high-acuity combat at non-augmented baseline against routinely augmented opposition. Documented combat morbidity includes vertebral fracture, multiple penetrating GSWs, repeated high-altitude blunt-force events, exposure to chemical/biological agents during S.H.I.E.L.D.-coordinated operations, and the cognitive load of repeated proximity to mass-casualty events (the Civil War period, *Secret Empire*, the Hydra occupation). On a sports-medicine analog this would predict measurable post-concussive cognitive sequelae; none are evident.

**Chronic social layer.** Continuous exposure to racialized public scrutiny across every public role (Falcon, Avenger-by-quota, Captain America). The literature on **racial battle fatigue** (Smith, 2003; Franklin et al., 2014) and **minority stress** (Meyer, 1995, adapted for race) is the correct analog frame.

**Acute identity-political layer.** The Spencer-era media siege — sustained, named, personalized public attack from a polarized media apparatus — constitutes a discrete chronic stressor distinct from operational combat trauma. Its symptom signature is different and is the closest Sam has come to clinical decompensation.

---

### 6.3 Symptom Presentation in Behavior

Working from the behavioral record outward to the diagnostic register:

**Hyperarousal cluster.** Mild and adaptive. Sam is observably scan-positive in any new environment — he checks sightlines, exits, elevations, and crowd composition before settling — but the scanning is *quiet*, embedded in his ordinary movement, and does not produce startle responses, sleep disruption, or autonomic dysregulation visible on the record. This is the **trained-vigilance** signature, not the **traumatized-vigilance** signature; the difference is whether the scan terminates with a return to baseline (trained) or maintains a chronic low-grade activation (traumatized). Sam's terminates.

**Intrusion cluster.** Largely absent. No documented nightmares, flashbacks, or intrusive imagery specifically tied to parental loss or to the Snap interval. The closest approach in the record is reflective rumination — Sam *thinks about* the Snap period in considered, articulate paragraphs — which is the opposite signature from intrusion (deliberate, ego-syntonic recall vs. involuntary, ego-dystonic eruption).

**Avoidance cluster.** Partial and selective. Sam does not avoid Harlem (he returns repeatedly and centers his civilian practice there); he does not avoid talk of his parents (he names them in conversation, including with mentees); he does not avoid the Snap material when asked. He *does* show what might be called **role-avoidance** under specific conditions — the 2017 shield surrender is the textbook instance — but this is values-driven withdrawal from a corrupted role, not phobic avoidance of trauma-linked stimuli.

**Negative alterations in cognition and mood.** Notably absent. No persistent negative self-attribution (he does *not* believe he is bad, broken, or unworthy), no foreshortened future, no pervasive negative emotional state. The one consistent negative cognition — *I cannot take my own goodness for granted* — is **examined and adaptive**, not depressive; it produces increased ethical scrutiny, not withdrawal or self-loathing.

**Somatic register.** No documented chronic pain syndrome despite injury history, no GI complaints, no sleep architecture disruption on record, no documented use of analgesics beyond acute injury. The somatic *silence* in his file is itself a finding — most operatives with his exposure carry some somatic signature, and Sam's absence of one suggests either exceptionally effective downregulation or systematic under-reporting (a known minority-male pattern that should be flagged for any clinician working with him; see §6.7).

**Affective range.** Wide, modulated, accurate-to-context. Humor is *generative* (creates connection, lowers threat) rather than *defensive-bitter* (deflects intimacy, conceals affect). Anger is *rare, situational, and articulated* — when Sam is angry, he names it and names its object, which is the marker of integrated rather than dissociated aggression. Grief is *processed serially* — he metabolizes losses (Riley, the various Rogers death/return cycles, civilian casualties on his watch) in real time rather than encysting them.

---

### 6.4 Working Diagnostic Formulation

Using DSM-5-TR analog categories with the explicit caveat that no category fits cleanly:

**Primary (sub-threshold) finding:** *Other Specified Trauma- and Stressor-Related Disorder*, with features of **complex post-traumatic stress** (ICD-11 6B41 analog) in **partial remission with post-traumatic growth predominant.** The qualifying features that are present: (a) exposure to extreme, prolonged, and repeated traumatic events; (b) historical disturbances in self-organization (the Snap interval); (c) chronic affect-regulation demand met by mature defenses rather than symptomatic dysregulation. The qualifying features that are *not* present at threshold: persistent re-experiencing, persistent avoidance, persistent sense of threat, clinically significant impairment in functioning.

**Secondary finding:** *Chronic racialized role-strain*, no formal DSM analog, best captured by the racial battle fatigue construct. Symptom signature: intermittent exhaustion (not anhedonia), intermittent role-disengagement (not depressive withdrawal), elevated cognitive load in identity-coded public contexts, and a *specifically located* fatigue point — the Captain America mantle as constituted under public/political adjudication. The 2017 shield surrender is the discrete clinical event of this finding.

**Historical finding (in remission):** *Dissociative experience, induced, non-recurrent.* The Snap interval meets phenomenological criteria for an induced dissociative fugue with identity alteration. It has not recurred. There is no present-day evidence of dissociative symptomatology — no time-loss, no identity fragmentation, no depersonalization/derealization episodes, no fugue states. This is an *historical* diagnostic entry that should be carried in the chart for context but is not an active condition.

**Adaptive findings (assets, not pathology):** earned secure attachment; mature defense profile (humor, sublimation, altruism, anticipation); high mentalization capacity; intact reality testing; robust working alliance capacity (i.e., he would be an excellent patient if he ever sat in a chair, which he has not).

---

### 6.5 Comorbidity Assessment

**Substance use disorders:** *Absent.* No record of alcohol abuse, prescription misuse, or illicit substance use across the canonical span. This is the single most actuarially surprising finding in the file — the population base rate for trauma-exposed Black urban males in his cohort would predict at minimum elevated alcohol use, and his combat-exposure profile would predict either alcohol or opioid risk. The abstention is consistent with a high-control internal-state-management style and probably also with the Harlem-pastor's-son value structure inherited from Paul Wilson.

**Mood disorders:** *Absent at threshold.* No major depressive episodes on record. No hypomania, no bipolar signature, no cyclothymic pattern. The 2017 withdrawal period had no neurovegetative depressive features (sleep, appetite, energy, libido all intact per available indicators) — it was a *values-decision episode*, not a *mood episode*, and the distinction is dispositive.

**Anxiety disorders:** *Absent at threshold.* No panic, no generalized anxiety pattern, no specific phobia, no OCD signature. Worry is task-bound and instrumental.

**Personality-level pathology:** *Absent.* No cluster A (no paranoid ideation beyond reality-appropriate institutional skepticism, no schizoid withdrawal, no schizotypal disorganization); no cluster B (the narcissism rule-out is the most important — see §6.6); no cluster C (not dependent, not avoidant, not obsessive-compulsive at personality level — disciplined, yes, but flexibly so, with no rigidity in moral or interpersonal frame).

**Neurocognitive:** No documented evidence of CTE-pattern cognitive decline despite repeated head-impact exposure. This is either a genuine absence (favorable somatic constitution, the Redwing/avian-link telemetry possibly carrying an unmeasured neuroprotective effect), an under-detection artifact (no neuropsych testing exists in canon), or both. **Flag for longitudinal monitoring.**

**Sleep-wake:** No documented insomnia, hypersomnia, parasomnia, or circadian disorder. Operational sleep is short and segmented (as expected) but baseline sleep when off-mission appears consolidated.

**Sexual and relational function:** Intact. Sustained relationships (Leila Taylor, the long Misty Knight arc) without the avoidant signature characteristic of his closest peers.

---

### 6.6 Rigorous Differential — What Sam Wilson Is *Not*, and Why

This is the analytically substantive part of the assessment. Each diagnosis below is one that a less careful reader might assign; each rule-out below is anchored in specific behavioral evidence.

**Major Depressive Disorder, recurrent.** *Ruled out.* The candidate episode is the 2016–17 pre-surrender period. Required features absent: pervasive low mood (he remained interpersonally warm), anhedonia (he continued to engage civilian hotline work with apparent satisfaction), neurovegetative changes (none documented), worthlessness/guilt at delusional intensity (his guilt was reality-tested and proportionate), and suicidality (entirely absent). What looked like depression was a *protracted moral injury response* terminating in a values-consistent role exit — phenomenologically distinct from depression even when the surface presentation (withdrawal, fatigue, reduced public engagement) overlaps.

**Persistent Depressive Disorder (dysthymia).** *Ruled out.* The chronicity is wrong direction — Sam's baseline affect is positive-warm, not chronically low. The "examined" quality of his self-concept is sometimes misread as dysthymic but is in fact ego-syntonic and energizing rather than ego-dystonic and depleting.

**PTSD, full criteria.** *Ruled out at present, historical sub-threshold.* The intrusion and avoidance clusters are not met. The negative-cognition cluster is not met. The hyperarousal cluster is met only at trained-professional baseline, indistinguishable from non-traumatized operators with equivalent training. The duration criterion is moot since the symptom thresholds are not met. This is the most important rule-out because the *presumption* of PTSD in any decorated combat operator is so strong that absence of diagnosis must be defended; the defense here is that Sam's symptom signature is *qualitatively* different from PTSD — reflective rather than intrusive, deliberate rather than avoidant, regulated rather than aroused.

**Complex PTSD (ICD-11).** *Sub-threshold; partial features present.* The three additional CPTSD criteria — affect dysregulation, negative self-concept, interpersonal difficulties — are present in *historical* form but not at current threshold. Affect dysregulation: historical (the Snap period), not current. Negative self-concept: present as *interrogated* self-concept, which is a categorically different cognitive structure (active examination vs. passive negative belief). Interpersonal difficulties: absent — his relational record is the *opposite* of CPTSD-typical. The CPTSD framework illuminates the etiology and the historical trajectory but does not fit the current presentation.

**Dissociative Identity Disorder.** *Ruled out.* This is a critical rule-out given the Snap material. DID requires recurrent identity-state switching with associated amnestic barriers and clinically significant distress/impairment. The Snap experience was a *single, externally-induced, terminated* dissociative episode, not a developmental DID picture. There is no evidence of switching, no amnestic gaps, no internal-system phenomenology. The Snap is to DID what a single drug-induced psychotic break is to schizophrenia: phenomenologically adjacent, etiologically and prognostically distinct.

**Other Specified Dissociative Disorder.** *Historical only.* The Snap interval would code here historically. No current dissociative phenomenology.

**Adjustment Disorder.** *Considered for the Spencer-era surrender period; rejected on duration and stressor-type grounds.* The stressor was not discrete and the response was not in excess of what the stressor warranted — it was, in fact, a *proportionate* response. Adjustment Disorder requires a maladaptive response; Sam's response was adaptive (extraction from a corrupted role).

**Bereavement-related disorders (prolonged grief / persistent complex bereavement).** *Ruled out for the parental losses.* Despite the configuration risk factors, his grief over Paul and Darlene Wilson has been integrated — referenced, named, used as motivational structure, but not encysted, not intrusive, not impairing. The integration is itself remarkable and probably reflects the protective effect of his vocational sublimation (social work as a way of *continuing the father's work safely*).

**Narcissistic Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out, definitively.* The dispositive evidence is the 2017 shield surrender. NPD does not voluntarily relinquish symbolic capital under public criticism — the structure of NPD requires the symbol to defend the self. Sam relinquished the symbol *because the symbol had become incompatible with the self*, which is the inverse structural logic. Additional rule-outs: he tolerates being out-shone (his entire Falcon career), he mentors successors developmentally (Torres), he loves Rogers without rivalry, he accepts criticism from community sources, he laughs at himself reliably. The NPD differential is worth running formally because Captain America roles attract NPD presentations; Sam's profile is the *photo-negative* of NPD.

**Antisocial Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out.* The Snap-era biography, if accepted, includes pre-15 conduct that might raise the question. The adult presentation rules it out completely — empathic, prosocial, rule-bound by internal values rather than external sanction, capable of sustained intimate relationships, no exploitative pattern, no callousness.

**Borderline Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out.* Stable self-concept (interrogated ≠ unstable), stable relationships, no impulsivity, no self-harm, no affective lability, no abandonment-frantic pattern. The closest BPD-resembling feature is his sensitivity to identity-attribution by others, but this is *cognitively processed* rather than *affectively reactive* — the opposite signature.

**Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out.* He is disciplined but not rigid, principled but not moralistic, organized but not perfectionistic, capable of delegation, capable of play. The Rogers personality presents this differential more strongly; Sam does not.

**Avoidant Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out.* Approach-oriented in all relational contexts.

**Dependent Personality Disorder.** *Ruled out.* Capable of solo decision-making at the highest stakes (shield surrender, S.H.I.E.L.D. break) against the wishes of his closest figures.

**Schizotypal/Schizoid spectrum.** *Ruled out.* Robust social engagement, normative reality testing, no perceptual anomalies (the Redwing link is an exogenous capability, not endogenous perceptual disturbance).

**ADHD.** *Ruled out.* Sustained-attention performance is elite; executive function is intact and probably above average; no hyperactivity, no impulsivity.

**Substance-induced disorders.** Not applicable — no substance use.

**Malingering / factitious presentations.** Not applicable; rather, the relevant clinical concern is the inverse — **stoic under-reporting**, particularly of pain and of distress, which is the documented pattern in Black male patients in U.S. medical systems and which should be assumed in any clinical encounter with this subject.

---

### 6.7 Course Over Time — Longitudinal Trajectory

**Phase I (childhood through pre-superheroic adulthood, c. age 9 through onset of operational career).** Acute traumatic loss followed by reconstitution through (a) extended family/community scaffolding, (b) the Snap interval as either a literal dissociative episode or — under the softening readings — as a contested narrative the subject had to integrate, and (c) early vocational identification with social work. The phase ends with a young adult who has *already* done substantial integrative work on his trauma history, which is why his operational debut presents as already-stabilized.

**Phase II (early operational, 1969–c. 1980).** The Falcon era proper. Symptom profile: stable. Stressor profile: rising (combat exposure begins to accumulate; the Gyrich Avengers experience adds racialized institutional strain). Adaptive response: increased reliance on the Rogers dyad as regulatory anchor, expansion of Harlem civilian practice as values anchor.

**Phase III (mid-career, c. 1980–2005).** Symptom profile: stable with occasional acute decompensation around discrete traumas (back injury, specific operational losses). Stressor profile: chronic, manageable. Adaptive response: deepening of partnership pattern, expansion of relational network, continued integration.

**Phase IV (high-tempo operational, 2005–2014).** Brubaker/Remender era. Symptom profile: stable under high load. The Rogers-death interval of *Civil War* is the most stress-tested period of his life to that point; symptom signature remained sub-threshold. Notable: the *absence* of decompensation during a period in which his closest peer was apparently dead and the political environment was hostile is itself diagnostic of robust regulatory capacity.

**Phase V (Captain America I, 2014–2017).** The role-strain phase. Symptom signature shifts for the first time on the record — *not* toward intrusion/avoidance/arousal but toward **role exhaustion** with values-conflict features. This is the discrete clinical event of the file. Resolution: the surrender, which is best read as a successful self-treatment intervention.

**Phase VI (Falcon-redux and reintegration, 2018–2022).** Recovery and re-authorship phase. Symptom profile: returns to baseline. Cognitive work: the explicit articulation of conditions under which the mantle is sustainable.

**Phase VII (Captain America II, 2022–present).** Mature state. Symptom profile: stable, with the difference that the role is now held *on examined terms*. The mantle is no longer a source of identity strain because the relationship to the mantle has been renegotiated. This is post-traumatic growth in its mature form — the stressor has been metabolized into a structural feature of the self rather than a destabilizing force.

**Prognosis.** Excellent for continued psychological stability under operational conditions. The two non-trivial risk vectors going forward are (1) **cumulative somatic burden** — the unenhanced body in enhanced combat is the actuarial pressure point, and a serious injury could open a depressive vulnerability that operational identity has so far masked; and (2) **loss within the small circle** — Rogers, Barnes, Misty Knight, Torres. Sam's regulation depends on partnership integrity; loss of multiple anchor figures in close succession would be the scenario in which a previously well-compensated CPTSD picture could become unmasked.

---

### 6.8 Clinical Notes for Any Future Treating Clinician

For the use of any future provider who might receive this file:

1. He will not present for treatment voluntarily. If he is in your office, someone close to him brought him or an injury required it.
2. Assume under-reporting of pain, somatic complaint, and internal distress. Verify rather than accept reassurance.
3. Do not lead with the Snap material. He has metabolized it; pressing on it without warrant would be iatrogenic.
4. Do not pathologize the shield surrender. It was the healthy act in his history, not the sick one.
5. The therapeutic alliance will form quickly and durably. He is an unusually high-functioning patient and will be a pleasure to work with, which is itself a countertransference risk — clinicians will be tempted to under-treat because he presents


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION 6 — BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

A surveillance-grade catalog of the Subject's observable conduct, sorted by state. Patterns are derived longitudinally across his Falcon period, his first Captain America tenure, his withdrawal, and his current mature-state operations. Granularity is the point: the same man under different loads produces different micro-signatures, and the cross-state map is what permits prediction.

---

## 6.1 BASELINE / CALM STATE

**Posture and stance.** Subject defaults to an open carriage — shoulders rolled back and slightly down, weight distributed evenly on both feet rather than cocked on one hip. Hands are almost never in pockets; they rest at the sides, on a counter, on the back of a chair, or holding something (coffee, phone, comm earpiece). The hands-visible default is consistent enough to be diagnostic: he learned, somewhere, that a Black man with visible hands is read as less threatening, and the learning has become musculature. He does not appear to notice he does it.

**Eyes.** Long visual sweeps on entering any room — a single arc across the space taking in exits, elevations, and persons, completed in roughly two seconds, then a return to whoever is talking. He makes eye contact early in a conversation, breaks it deliberately when he is thinking, and re-engages it when he is about to say the operative sentence. He looks *up and slightly off* when accessing memory; he looks *down* when accessing feeling. The down-look precedes his most honest sentences.

**Voice.** Mid-register baritone, paced slightly slower than the room. He uses the slowness as a leveling tool — interlocutors involuntarily match it. Vocal warmth is genuine, not performed; the laugh is from the diaphragm and brief, never social-extended. He says people's names early in a conversation and again at the close, a social-work habit retained from his Harlem casework.

**Verbal tics and signatures.**
- "Alright" as a sentence-opener when transitioning from listening to acting.
- "Talk to me" as a directive in field comms — never "report" or "status," always the conversational form.
- "We're gonna figure this out" — said to civilians under threat, said to teammates mid-mission, said to himself audibly when alone with a problem.
- The phrase "say what you mean" surfaces when he is being lied to and wants the other party to know he knows.
- He drops the "g" on participles when at ease ("workin' it," "gettin' there"); he pronounces them fully when on record, in court, or addressing federal personnel — a code-switch he executes without strain and without comment.

**Micro-gestures.** A flat-palm gesture toward the ground when asking someone to slow down or stay put — used identically with frightened civilians, agitated cops, and Steve Rogers when Rogers is about to escalate. A single nod, slow, when he has decided something internally. A two-finger tap on his own sternum when acknowledging fault. A back-of-the-knuckles brush against his jaw when he is amused but does not want to show it.

**Daily rhythm.** Early riser, pre-dawn by preference. The first hour is solitary: coffee (black, no sugar, in a heavy mug he holds with both hands), a window or rooftop, and what reads as either prayer or a structured meditative scan — eyes closed, breathing slow, lips occasionally moving. He has never publicly described this as prayer. The minister's son in him has not gone anywhere. After this, a physical training block that is brutally consistent: calisthenics, mobility, weighted carries, sparring three times a week, flight-rig drills two. He does not skip. The body is the only ally that has never lied to him, and he treats it accordingly.

**Eating.** Eats slowly. Always finishes. Cleans his own dish immediately, even in other people's kitchens. Cooks competently — soul-food repertoire from his mother's side, supplemented by whatever the current safehouse pantry contains. Feeds other people before himself when feeding a group, and notices who has not eaten.

**Phone and screen behavior.** Phone face-down on tables. Reads news in the morning and does not return to it during the day. Texts in complete sentences with punctuation. Does not use emoji except a single thumbs-up as a mission-acknowledged signal. Does not post to social media in any persona. Listens to voicemails fully before responding; will call back rather than text back when the message was emotional.

**Sleep.** Sleeps on his back, light. Wakes fully at the first anomalous sound and is operational within two seconds. Returns to sleep within ten minutes if the anomaly resolves. Does not nap.

---

## 6.2 LOW-LEVEL STRESS / WORKING PROBLEM

**Speech.** Sentences shorten. The conversational rhythm tightens into clauses. He begins narrating his own thought process aloud — "okay, so what we've got is —" — which has the dual function of organizing his cognition and inviting others into it. This is the social-worker case-conference habit operating in tactical conditions.

**Body.** He starts to *move while thinking*. Pacing in a tight rectangle, never circular. If pacing is impossible, he will rotate a small object in his hand — a pen, a coin, the edge of a folded map. Redwing, when present, will shift on its perch in sync; the link runs both directions and Sam's low-grade agitation transmits.

**Eye behavior.** More frequent sweeps of the room. He begins counting exits a second time. He looks at the ceiling when working a spatial problem — running the bird's-eye overlay.

**Decision habit.** Sam does not make decisions under low stress; he *frames* them. He will lay out two or three options aloud, attach a cost to each, and then defer the choice for as long as the situation permits. The deferral is not indecision — it is a deliberate practice of letting more information arrive. When forced, he chooses the option that preserves the most future options. He is constitutionally a *containment* thinker, not a *resolution* thinker.

**Interpersonal.** Becomes more solicitous, not less. Checks on people he would not normally check on. Asks the junior person in the room what they think. This is partly leadership doctrine and partly the displacement of his own anxiety into the management of others' — but the others benefit, so the defense is mature.

---

## 6.3 ACUTE THREAT / COMBAT

**The transition.** There is no visible adrenaline tell. No jaw clench, no fist clench, no widening of the eyes. The shift is *downward* — voice drops half an octave, sentences become imperatives, the body settles rather than tightens. Observers consistently report that Sam looks *calmer* in a firefight than in a meeting.

**Verbal under fire.**
- Comms discipline is excellent. Call signs, compass directions, ranges in meters, casualty counts as numbers not adjectives.
- He talks to civilians continuously: "I've got you, stay with me, we're moving in three." The talk is itself a tool — it prevents shock spirals and gives him a read on the civilian's coherence.
- He talks to opponents when the tactical situation allows it. The talk is genuine de-escalation, not stalling: he is actually trying to give the other party an exit. He will name what he sees ("you don't want to be doing this, I can see it"). He will offer terms. He means them.

**Movement.** Economical. Sam does not throw a punch he does not need. His combat style integrates aerial and ground transitions seamlessly — he uses the wings to *reposition*, not to dominate, and he prefers the angle of approach that takes the opponent's weapon out of play rather than the angle that maximizes his own offense. Against enhanced opponents (which is most of them) he fights *defensively-offensively*: absorb, redirect, create the opening, exploit once, disengage. He does not trade blows. He cannot afford to.

**Use of the shield (Captain America periods).** Different from Rogers'. Rogers uses the shield as an extension of the body, a striking and blocking surface. Sam uses it as a *third object* — thrown more often, used as a barrier between civilians and threat more often, used as a fulcrum for the wings' aerial work. He is more likely to *give* the shield to someone (place it in front of a downed teammate, hand it to a civilian behind cover) than Rogers ever was. The shield, for Sam, is a tool he is responsible for, not a relic he is fused with.

**Killing threshold.** High. Sam has lethal capability and demonstrably will not use it as a first resort, second resort, or third. He will use it. He has used it. He does not pretend otherwise and does not moralize about it after. The aftermath signature: longer silences for forty-eight hours, an extra hour at the dawn window, a phone call to someone (often Misty Knight, sometimes Barnes) that consists mostly of listening.

**Pain response.** Suppresses visible expression in the moment, addresses it tactically ("right shoulder's done, switching"), processes it physically after. Does not refuse medical care but minimizes its disruption to others — will drive himself to a safe-house medic rather than call for evac if the injury is sub-critical.

**Fear.** Present, managed, never denied. The tell is a single slow exhale through the nose before a committed action. If you see the exhale, he is about to do something he is afraid of and has decided to do anyway.

---

## 6.4 LEADERSHIP / TEAM COMMAND

**Briefing style.** Stands rather than sits. Uses physical objects to model the situation (coins, salt shakers, drone-cam stills) — kinesthetic and visual, rarely text-heavy. Assigns roles by *name*, then by *function*, then asks each named person whether they have questions. The order matters: the personal address comes first.

**Disagreement protocol.** Sam invites dissent explicitly and early. "Tell me why I'm wrong about this" is a documented recurring phrase. He absorbs the dissent without defensiveness, restates it back to the dissenter to confirm comprehension, and then either adjusts or explains why he is holding the original line. He does not punish dissent. He remembers who dissented and consults them earlier next time.

**Praise and correction.** Praise is specific and immediate ("that was good work on the south corridor — you saw the angle before I did"). Correction is private, delayed to a moment of low ambient stress, and framed developmentally rather than punitively. He does not raise his voice to subordinates. He has not been recorded doing so in any era.

**Distribution of credit.** Reliably gives credit to others in public and absorbs blame to himself. This is consistent enough to be a vulnerability — he has accepted institutional blame for failures that were not his (the Americops affair, the Hauser-era media cycles) rather than redirect it to the actual responsible parties, because redirection feels to him like the betrayal of subordinates.

**Mentorship signature (Torres and others).** Sam teaches by *asking questions he already knows the answer to* and waiting through the silence. He will not rescue the mentee from the silence. When the mentee answers, he expands the answer rather than corrects it. He is willing to let a mentee fail in low-stakes conditions in order to learn — this is unusual among Marvel principals, most of whom are over-controlling with proteges.

---

## 6.5 INTIMACY / CLOSE RELATIONSHIPS

**Approach.** Initiates physical contact warmly but briefly — a hand on a shoulder, a forearm clasp, a one-armed embrace on greeting. Holds the contact a beat longer with people he is worried about. With Rogers specifically: the contact is unselfconscious and frequent, a settled physicality between men who have carried each other off battlefields.

**Disclosure.** Discloses incrementally and reciprocally — will not unload, will not pry. The pattern is one observation about himself, then a question that opens the same territory for the other. He does not perform vulnerability. He does not weaponize it either.

**Romantic pattern (Leila Taylor, Misty Knight, others).** Slow openings, durable middles, clean endings. Sam does not ghost and does not relapse into dead relationships. With Misty in particular the pattern is *adult intermittent partnership* — two operationally independent people who return to each other across years without possessiveness. He remembers details (birthdays, anniversaries of losses, the names of the other person's nieces) and acts on them without announcement.

**Conflict in close relationships.** Names the conflict early. Refuses to fight about the surface issue when the actual issue is underneath. Will sit in a long silence rather than say something he will regret. Apologizes specifically — not "I'm sorry you felt that way" but "I'm sorry I said X, that was wrong, here's what I'll do differently." Forgives slowly but completely.

**Sexual register.** Not exhibited in detail in canon, consistent with the character's reticence rather than the medium's. Inference from the surrounding behavior: present, generous, communicative, non-compulsive.

---

## 6.6 GRIEF

**Acute grief response.** First hour: operational. Sam will complete whatever the situation requires before he allows himself to feel the loss. This is the social-worker discipline (the death notification training: deliver the news, then be present for the family, then go home and feel it).

**First 24–72 hours.** Withdrawal to a solitary space. The dawn window extends. He cooks for himself and eats methodically. He calls one person — usually Misty, sometimes Barnes, occasionally a Harlem contact from the social-work years who has nothing to do with the superhero life and therefore offers a baseline-reality anchor. The call is mostly listening on his end. He does not cry on the phone. He cries, when he cries, alone, briefly, and without ceremony, then washes his face and resumes.

**Days to weeks.** Sam *visits places*. Graves, scenes, neighborhoods the dead person loved. He stands in them. The somatic ritual is more important to him than verbal mourning. He will bring food and eat there.

**Long-term grief integration.** Sam does not curate shrines and does not over-commemorate, but he keeps small physical tokens — a folded photograph, a piece of fabric, a coin — in a single drawer or pocket. He references the dead in present-tense sentences ("my father says—") and catches himself, smiles, lets it stand. This is healthy grief, not unresolved grief: the dead are integrated into ongoing identity rather than maintained as open wounds.

**Anniversary behavior.** Quiet. He does not announce. The dawn window doubles. He may be unreachable for half a day. He returns without comment and expects none.

---

## 6.7 VICTORY

**In the moment.** Subdued. Sam does not celebrate at the scene of a win. He moves immediately to civilian welfare, debrief, evacuation. The first sentence after a victory is almost always a question about someone's safety. He will accept a teammate's offered hand or embrace and return it, but he does not initiate the celebration.

**Subsequent hours.** Genuine warmth surfaces. He will buy a meal for the team, sit through the recounting, laugh at the right places, contribute the self-deprecating story that makes the junior member feel like part of the group. The laugh is real but he is the first to leave.

**Suspicion of victory.** Sam treats wins as provisional. The verbal tell is "for now" appended to assessments — "we've got it contained, for now." This is not pessimism; it is the operational humility of someone who has been told for fifty years that the work is unfinished and believes it.

---

## 6.8 DEFEAT

**Tactical defeat (mission failure).** Cold focus. No outward expression of frustration, no recriminations, no second-guessing in the immediate debrief. Sam runs the after-action calmly, accepts the blame appropriate to his role, distributes none, and ends the meeting on the next operational step rather than on the failure itself.

**Private processing.** Substantial. Sam *replays* defeats — alone, methodically, at the dawn window, in physical training (he will run drills against the specific failure mode for weeks). He does not show this to the team. The cost is internal and the team sees only the corrected behavior in the next operation.

**Moral defeat (the deeper category).** When Sam has been *used*, *misrepresented*, or *betrayed by an institution* — the Hydra-Cap timeline, the Americops, the Gyrich Avengers seat, the Hauser media cycles — the response is qualitatively different. He gets *quiet*. The humor recedes. The dawn window extends to two hours. He consults his own conscience explicitly, often by talking to one of the small handful of people whose moral judgment he trusts without reservation. The eventual response, when it comes, is structural: he changes the conditions of his service. He gives the shield back. He resigns from the team. He moves operations. He does not stay in a role that has become incompatible with the person he has decided to be.

**The signature of moral defeat is not anger; it is withdrawal followed by reconstitution.** This is the single most important behavioral data point in the file.

---

## 6.9 INTERACTIONS WITH AUTHORITY

**Law enforcement (street-level).** Hands visible. Voice level. ID produced before requested. The code-switch into fully articulated participles. A small, fixed smile that is not friendly but is non-threatening. He has trained this behavior into reflex over a lifetime and it does not abate when he is in the Captain America uniform — he is aware that the uniform does not protect the body wearing it from the assumptions of the officer encountering it, and may in some cases intensify them.

**Federal and military.** Polite, brief, declarative. Does not volunteer information. Does not ingratiate. Does not antagonize. Treats rank as a fact about the institution rather than a fact about the person and adjusts his deference accordingly — he will defer to a competent senior officer and ignore an incompetent one with equal calm.

**Press.** Prepared. Speaks in completed paragraphs. Pivots from gotcha questions to substantive ones without visible defensiveness. Refuses to be drawn into characterizing other heroes negatively. Will name structural problems (surveillance overreach, militarization, the specific failures of specific agencies) on the record and without hedging when he has decided to do so. Does not give interviews he has not prepared for.

**Hostile authority (Gyrich, hostile federal investigators, hostile journalists).** Cools rather than heats. Becomes more formal, more concise, more difficult to maneuver. Will exit the room when the interaction has ceased to be productive and will do so without dramatics.

---

## 6.10 INTERACTIONS WITH CIVILIANS

**Children.** Crouches to eye level immediately. Speaks at adult vocabulary level, not down-talk. Asks the child's name and uses it. Lets the child touch the wings or the shield if the child wants to. Does not promise outcomes he cannot guarantee — will say "I'm going to try" rather than "you're going to be okay."

**The elderly, particularly Black elders.** Demonstrably respectful — yes ma'am, yes sir, hat off (metaphorically; he doesn't wear one). Will sit and listen to a long story when operational tempo permits. Accepts food when offered.

**The frightened.** Modulates everything down. Slower speech, smaller gestures, more space between himself and the person. Narrates his own next movement before he makes it ("I'm going to reach for the radio now").

**The hostile.** Names the hostility ("I can see you're angry, and you've got reasons") and then asks what they want. Does not argue identity politics on the street. Does not perform patience he does not have, but he generally has it.

---

## 6.11 SOLITUDE

The solitary Sam is the most stable Sam. He does not require company to regulate. He reads (history, political theory, biography — light on fiction, with exceptions for poetry); he listens to music (soul, jazz, gospel — the sonic vocabulary of his parents' Harlem); he cooks; he trains; he sits at windows. He is not lonely in solitude. The withdrawal periods after defeats and losses are not depressive episodes — they are *recalibrations*, and he emerges from them with the decision already made.

He talks to himself audibly when alone — working problems aloud, occasional one-sided exchanges with Redwing, occasional sentences directed at the dead ("you'd have laughed at that, Pop"). None of this is dissociative. All of it is the verbal generativity of a man whose primary cognitive instrument is language.

---

## 6.12 THE CROSS-STATE SIGNATURE

Across every state catalogued above, one pattern recurs and is the unifying behavioral fingerprint: **Sam Wilson decreases his own arousal as the ambient arousal increases.** Calmer rooms make him slightly more energetic; tenser rooms make him slower, lower, quieter. This counter-cyclical regulation is the deepest behavioral signature in the file, the thing that makes him the de-escalator on every team he has ever been on, and the thing that has kept an unenhanced human alive across five decades of operational service against enhanced opposition.

It is also, not coincidentally, the behavior of a man who learned very young that a Black child in a frightened room must become the calmest object in it, and who has built an entire adult identity — vocational, superheroic, symbolic — on the refinement of that childhood adaptation into a discipline.

The Atlas, in sum, does not describe a man performing composure. It describes a man whose composure is the residue of every decision he has ever made about what kind of person to be in a world that did not promise him the chance to choose.


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section 6 — Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

The file that follows reconstructs the granular texture of Subject's lived week — what a continuous-coverage surveillance package would actually log, hour by hour, across a representative non-crisis fortnight. The operating premise: Subject is one of the most *routinized* principals in the active-operator population. This is itself diagnostic — high-functioning trauma-adapted adults tend to externalize order into schedule, and Subject's schedule is the architecture his interior runs on. Disruptions to routine are therefore disproportionately informative; they correlate with mission-tempo escalation, family stress, or the rarer episodes when his self-interrogation enters an acute phase.

---

### 6.1 The Diurnal Frame

**Wake.** Reliably between 0510 and 0535, no alarm in the apartment most mornings — Subject's internal clock is calibrated and has been since his social-work years, when home-visit caseloads required dawn starts. On nights following operational engagement he allows himself an additional ninety minutes; this is a deliberate, scheduled concession, not slippage. Lights-on signature in the kitchen typically precedes lights-on in the main room by six to nine minutes. He does not check a phone first thing — phone remains face-down on the kitchen counter overnight, a habit consistent across surveillance windows in three different residences.

**First fifteen minutes.** Water (room temperature, glass not bottle, drawn from the tap and left out the night before), the small kitchen window opened regardless of weather, and a brief stillness at the window before any other activity. Lip movement observable from external optics on multiple occasions — short, under twenty seconds, no rosary or text. Assessment: a learned prayer or remembrance, almost certainly inherited from Paul Wilson's household. Not performed when houseguests are present; performed without fail when alone. This is the single most consistent ritual in the entire surveillance record and the one Subject would be most reluctant to discuss.

**Movement.** Forty to sixty minutes of physical practice before any food. Composition varies by day on a clearly cycled split — Mondays and Thursdays favor a calisthenic strength block (pull, push, single-leg work, weighted carries with whatever is in the apartment); Tuesdays and Fridays favor running, either rooftop circuits at altitude when local infrastructure permits or street miles at conversational pace through whichever neighborhood he is in; Wednesdays and Saturdays favor what an observer would parse as combatives — shadow work, evasion drills, recoveries from disadvantaged positions on the floor, all done quietly and without equipment. Sundays: mobility and breath work only, forty minutes, on a mat by the window. This split is *self-imposed and self-enforced*; no trainer, no app, no log visible to optics. Subject is the kind of athlete who keeps the program in his head and trusts himself to be honest about it.

The unenhanced body is the unspoken subtext of the entire training schedule. Subject trains like a man who knows that the margin between him and the people he fights is the margin he himself manufactures every morning. Volume is *high* by civilian standards and *low* by elite-operator standards — calibrated for longevity, not peak, because he intends to be doing this in his sixties.

**Breakfast.** Eggs almost daily — two, scrambled, with whatever vegetable is closest to going off in the fridge folded in. Toast. Coffee, black, brewed in a stovetop moka pot which he owns in duplicate (one travels). He cooks for himself even when there is a perfectly adequate building kitchen, a perfectly adequate room-service menu, or a perfectly adequate compound mess available. This is not asceticism; it is *control of inputs*, and it is also the social worker's residual housekeeping instinct — the dishes are washed before he leaves the kitchen, every time, including in hotels.

**Morning correspondence block.** 0700–0815, depending on the day. Subject reads at the kitchen table: a physical newspaper when available (he subscribes to at least one local paper in whichever city he is operating from, and to a Harlem community weekly that is mailed forward), a battered paperback or nonfiction title rotating on a roughly two-week cycle, and a tablet for email and the morning's intelligence read. He answers messages in a specific order: family first (Sarah, the nieces and nephews, anyone in the extended Casper line who has written), then the small circle (Barnes, Rogers, Torres, Misty when she initiates), then institutional traffic, then press requests (which he reads but rarely answers same-day). Family messages get long answers; institutional traffic gets short ones. This priority ordering is invariant and is itself a values statement.

---

### 6.2 The Working Day

Subject's "work" decomposes into three braided streams that he keeps deliberately separated in time and place:

**Stream A — Operational.** Intelligence reviews, mission planning, equipment maintenance, the wing rig (which he services himself — refuses to delegate this even to qualified armorers, a habit traceable to early experiences with provided equipment failing at altitude). Equipment maintenance happens in a dedicated workspace, never in the living areas, and follows the same sequence every time: visual inspection, articulation test, power cycle, edge/seam check, stow. The whole process takes between thirty-five and fifty minutes and he times it consistently; an unusually long maintenance session is a tell that something happened in the field he is not putting in the report.
