He also does not suppress it when white listeners are present in a setting where its use is appropriate — the determinant is *audience belonging*, not *audience composition*.

---

### 6.3 Register Inventory

Sam operates in at least six distinct registers, switchable mid-sentence:

1. **Pastoral / Community register.** Inherited cadence. Used in Harlem, at funerals, in the civilian hotline, when speaking to grieving family members, when addressing crowds. Marked by: longer sentences, parallel structures (*"You're scared, and you're tired, and you have every right to be both"*), inclusive pronouns (*we, us, our*), and the rhetorical move of *naming the feeling before naming the action*. Echoes — without imitating — the homiletic structure of the Black church: situation, recognition, reframing, charge.
2. **Operational / Comms register.** Compressed, denotative, no ornament. *"Two on the roof. East stairwell clear. Moving."* Call-signs used cleanly. Acknowledgments crisp. He does not editorialize on comms during live action and is observably annoyed when teammates do.
3. **Social-work register.** This is distinct from the pastoral. Where the pastoral *holds*, the social-work register *assesses and redirects*. Open questions, mirrored language, deliberate avoidance of imperatives, careful use of the conditional (*"What would it look like if—"*, *"Walk me through—"*, *"Help me understand what happened before—"*). He uses this register in hostage negotiations, with rookie heroes in crisis, and — diagnostically — with Rogers when Rogers is about to do something Sam thinks is foolish.
4. **Press / Public register.** Polished, slightly more formal syntax, full sentences, careful nouns. Sam in press conferences sounds like a man who has been media-trained but also like a man who has thought about every word. He does not use the second-person plural to refer to Americans (he never says *"we Americans"* the way Rogers does); he says *"this country"* or *"the people in this country"* — a small but consistent distancing move that preserves his right to critique without disavowing membership.
5. **Peer register.** With Rogers, Barnes, Misty, Torres, T'Challa, Storm. Faster, drier, more allusive, generous with the wisecrack. Inside jokes accrete and persist; Sam remembers a callback for years and will pull it back out at the precise moment to puncture a tense room.
6. **Combat-quip register.** A specific subset of peer register, deployed in live fights. Sam talks during fights — not as much as Spider-Man, but consistently. The quips are *short*, *aimed at the opponent's pretension*, and serve a tactical purpose (rhythm disruption, demoralization, signaling to teammates that he is still upright and thinking). *"That all you got?"* is not his style; he is more likely to say something like *"You really practiced that line in a mirror, huh?"* — using mockery to deflate, not to escalate.

The switching is fluid and continuous. A representative Spencer-era sequence: Sam on comms with Misty in operational register, breaks to address a frightened civilian in social-work register, lands a one-liner on the antagonist in combat-quip register, and closes with a pastoral half-line to the civilian (*"You did the right thing calling. We've got you."*) — all inside about forty seconds of page time.

---

### 6.4 Diction & Lexicon

- **High-frequency words.** *Look* (as opener and as resetter — *"Look, here's what we're gonna do"*); *talk* (*"let's talk about this"*, *"we need to talk"*, *"talk to me"*); *people* (preferred over *civilians*, *citizens*, *humans*); *home* (loaded — Harlem, the country, the self); *figure* (*"we're going to figure this out"* is near-verbatim across writers); *right* and *wrong* used without scare-quotes, but *good* and *bad* used sparingly and with care; *brother* used selectively and meaningfully — never as filler.
- **Low-frequency / avoided words.** *Soldier* (he does not call himself one and rarely calls Rogers one to his face); *mission* used operationally but never inflated to capital-M *Mission*; *patriot* never self-applied; *hero* almost never self-applied and frequently *resisted* when applied to him; *freedom* used sparingly and almost always paired with a qualifier or a particular referent — Sam does not float the abstract noun.
- **Profanity.** Present but disciplined. Mild profanity in peer register; the harder words reserved for moments of genuine anger or grief, where they carry weight precisely *because* he doesn't squander them. He swears more around Barnes than around anyone else.
- **Slang and idiom.** Generationally layered. Sam's idiom shows strata — older AAVE expressions inherited from Harlem upbringing coexist with current usage absorbed from Torres and younger contacts. He picks up new slang quickly and uses it without irony, which is itself a generational tell: he is not a man who refuses to update his vocabulary.
- **Names and titles.** Sam uses people's names. Constantly. First names, repeated through a conversation, used as anchors and as recognitions. This is a social-work tic and also a community tic — it is the practice of someone for whom *being seen by name* is a thing he learned to give because he learned, young, what it costs to be unnamed. He addresses Rogers as *Steve* in private and *Cap* in public-mixed company, and is precise about the line. He addresses Barnes as *Bucky* only after Barnes has earned it back; before that, *Barnes* or *James* depending on the temperature of the room.
- **Numbers and specifics.** Sam talks in specifics. He gives counts, distances, addresses, names. He does not say *"a lot of people"*; he says *"about thirty"*. This is operational precision but also a rhetorical move — concreteness is anti-abstraction, and Sam's politics are anti-abstraction.

---

### 6.5 Verbal Tics & Microhabits

- **The opener *"Look,"*** deployed to gather a room or reset a derailed exchange. Functions as a verbal hand-raise.
- **The opener *"All right,"*** in operational contexts to mark transition into action phase. Distinct from *"Look,"* in that *"All right,"* is forward-moving while *"Look,"* is anchoring.
- **The reset *"Hey. Hey."*** — doubled, with the second beat softer than the first — used in de-escalation, with panicked civilians, occasionally with Rogers when Rogers has gone somewhere internal. The doubling is a social-work technique (the first to interrupt, the second to invite).
- **The qualifying tail *"…you know what I mean?"*** used in peer register, not as filler but as a genuine invitation to confirm shared frame. He waits for the nod.
- **The directive softener *"…if you want."*** used with subordinates and mentees, almost never with peers. Preserves the other person's agency in the directive.
- **The catchphrase-grade *"On your left."*** Limited canonical usage in print but extant; functions as both a flight-pattern announcement and an inside joke with Rogers. Used sparingly enough that it retains meaning.
- **The closing *"We're going to figure this out."*** Across writers, near-verbatim. It is the Sam Wilson signature sentence. It does *not* say we will win; it says we will think.
- **Verbal nod-substitute *"Mm-hm."*** Two-tone, slight pitch rise on the second syllable, used as active-listening marker. He uses this on the phone, on comms, and in person, and its absence (Sam falling silent while listening) is a stress tell.
- **The aborted self-reference.** Sam will begin a sentence with *"I—"* and reroute to *"We—"* or *"You—"*. This is consistent enough to be diagnostic of his trained reflex away from making the moment about himself. Under stress or in genuine intimacy, the reroute fails and the *"I—"* lands — and when it does, listeners should attend, because Sam has just said something he meant personally.

---

### 6.6 Rhetorical Architecture

Sam's larger speech structures, when he is given the floor (briefings, press, eulogies, the rare set-piece monologue), tend toward a recognizable architecture:

1. **Concrete opener.** A name, a place, a specific incident. He does not begin with abstractions.
2. **Acknowledgment of difficulty.** A clause that names what is hard, painful, or unresolved. He does not skip over it.
3. **Reframing pivot.** Usually marked by *"but"*, *"and yet"*, or *"here's the thing"* — a turn that does not deny the difficulty but offers a different angle on it.
4. **Inclusive charge.** A forward-facing sentence using *we* or *us*, almost always with a specific action attached. Not *"we must do better"* but *"we're going to walk down that block and we're going to knock on that door."*
5. **Close on a person, not a principle.** Sam's set-pieces end on someone's name, or on a *you* directed at a specific listener. He resists the abstract sign-off.

This architecture is markedly different from Rogers' four-square moral rhetoric and from Stark's ironic-deflationary patter. It is *homiletic* in structure — it borrows the bones of a sermon — but it is *secular and operational* in content.

---

### 6.7 Communicating Love

Sam expresses love **verbally, frequently, and unembarrassedly** — a rarity in his cohort. He says *"I love you"* to family and to chosen family without preamble. He tells Rogers he loves him on at least one canonical occasion and does not surround it with a joke. With Misty, the verbal channel is supplemented by sustained playful argumentation — they communicate affection through *staying in the conversation* across long absences. With Torres, love takes the form of teaching: Sam communicates care by *spending the time*, narrating his reasoning aloud, walking the rookie through decisions rather than giving him outcomes. With Barnes, love is the willingness to *call him on his shit* — Sam is the one person who tells Barnes the truth without performing forgiveness, and Barnes hears love in that.

The non-verbal channel: Sam touches people he loves. A hand to the shoulder, the back of the neck, the upper arm. He is one of the few principals in the modern Marvel record who initiates physical contact as an emotional register, and he does so across gender and across racial lines without self-consciousness. The contact is brief, weighted, and unmistakable.

---

### 6.8 Communicating Threat

Sam threatens **rarely and quietly**, and when he does, the threat is structurally distinct from his baseline speech. The tells:

- **Pitch drops further than the de-escalation register.** Below the negotiator voice.
- **Sentence length collapses.** Three- and four-word sentences. *"You don't want this."* *"Walk away."* *"Last time I'm asking."*
- **Names are used as warnings.** Sam saying the antagonist's name, slowly, once, is the warning shot.
- **The humor disappears.** Total. The absence of the smile-voice in a Sam Wilson sentence is itself the threat.
- **Eye contact locks.** Per consistent depiction across artists, Sam's threat presentation is *visually still* — he stops moving his hands, stops the room-reading micro-glances, and fixes the gaze.

Sam does not bluff. Threats from him are statements of intention, and the operational record bears them out. Antagonists who have been on the receiving end and survived to encounter him again read the signs faster the second time.

---

### 6.9 Communicating Grief

Grief is where Sam's verbal facility *fails*, and the failure is the tell. Markers:

- **Sentence fragmentation.** The clause-clusters break down. He starts and does not finish. *"He was — yeah."*
- **Lateral movement to the practical.** Sam grieves by *organizing the next thing*. After loss, he is the one calling the family, arranging the service, checking on the room. This is partly genuine other-orientation and partly a defense against the unbearable middle of his own feeling.
- **Use of the deceased's name in present tense, briefly.** A small slip, then a self-correction. The slip is unguarded; the correction is fast.
- **Pastoral register *to himself*.** He talks himself through grief in the cadence he would use with another. He has been overheard, occasionally, doing this aloud when he thinks he is alone.
- **The long silence.** Sam who does not speak is Sam in pain. The duration of his silence is roughly proportional to the depth of the loss. The pattern is so consistent that close associates (Rogers, Misty, Barnes in his later years) recognize it immediately and *do not try to fill the silence* — they sit in it with him, which is what he needs.

He has never, on record, cried in public. He has cried — there is canonical evidence — in private and in the presence of a single trusted other. The presence of the other is necessary; he does not grieve alone if he can help it, and the fact that he *can usually help it* is itself a measure of how carefully he has built his attachment system.

---

### 6.10 Deflection Language

Sam deflects, but the deflection is *visible* to a trained ear — it is structured, not chaotic, and the structure is the signature.

- **Humor as deflection.** Most common. A well-timed wisecrack to move the room past a question he does not want to answer. Reliable diagnostic: if Sam answers a personal question with a joke and then *changes the subject* in the same breath, he is deflecting. If the joke lands and he then answers the question, he was just being funny.
- **The procedural pivot.** Asked about his feelings, he answers about the operational situation. Asked about his past, he answers about the present mission. Asked about the Snap retcon material directly (canonically, on a handful of occasions), he reframes to *"What I do now is mine."*
- **The redirected mirror.** Asked a hard question, Sam asks one back. Social-work technique deployed defensively. Skilled interviewers notice that they have spent twenty minutes talking about themselves.
- **The Harlem cite.** Asked about himself in the abstract, Sam grounds in a specific Harlem story — a person, a block, an incident. The cite is genuine *and* it diverts from interiority.
- **The acknowledgment-without-disclosure.** *"That's a fair question."* *"Yeah, I've thought about that."* *"I hear you."* Each of these can be a real engagement or a polished close-out, and the tell is whether anything follows. If nothing follows, he has used the acknowledgment as a door he is closing.

What Sam does *not* do: he does not lie outright when pressed on substance, and he does not stonewall. The deflection is always a *redirection*, never a refusal. This is consistent with his core ethical commitment to communication itself — Sam can decline to discuss a thing, but he will not pretend the thing does not exist.

---

### 6.11 Written Communication

Less voluminous in canon than spoken, but consistent:

- **Texts:** short, punctual, lowercase, sparing on emoji but uses them with Torres and Misty. Confirms receipt of information promptly. Does not leave people on read.
- **Operational reports:** crisp, structured, complete. He writes them himself and is mildly irritated when teammates do not.
- **Personal correspondence:** rare but, when present, longer than expected, with the same pastoral architecture as his set-piece speech. He writes condolence letters by hand.
- **Public statements:** when he releases one, it is short, specific, and ends on a person's name or a directly addressed *you*. Same architecture as his spoken set-pieces; the voice is fully recognizable in print.

---

### 6.12 Tells: Stress, Deception, Decision

A surveillance-grade catalog of the linguistic indicators that something is happening *under* the speech:

- **Stress indicator: the procedural shift.** Sam moving from peer or pastoral register into operational register *outside of an operational context* is a near-certain sign of acute internal pressure. He retreats into the most compressed and impersonal of his registers when he needs to manage himself.
- **Stress indicator: the disappeared *mm-hm*.** Active-listening tokens drop out. Silence on his end of a call, with breath audible. This is Sam regulating before responding.
- **Stress indicator: the *"I—"* that doesn't reroute.** Sam saying *I* without immediately repluralizing means his usual filter is offline. Treat as significant.
- **Deception indicator (rare).** Sam is not a habitual liar, and when he withholds, he prefers redirection to fabrication. The tell for the rare outright deception is a *slight excess of specificity* — a true Sam Wilson statement is concrete because his thinking is concrete; a deceptive Sam Wilson statement is concrete because he has *prepared* it, and the preparation shows as over-smoothness.
- **Decision indicator: the long exhale, then the name.** When Sam has made a difficult decision, the speech-act marker is an audible exhale followed by the addressee's name, followed by the decision in a short sentence. *(exhale) "Steve. I'm putting it down."* The pattern is stable across two decades of canonical depiction. Once the name has been said in that cadence, the decision is final and arguing with it is wasted breath.
- **Approval / disapproval microsignal.** Approval: a single *"Yeah."* with a downward inflection. Disapproval: the same word, same length, slight pitch rise and a held beat after. Subordinates and peers learn the difference within weeks of working with him.
- **Boredom / impatience.** Sam does not perform impatience, but he stops generating wisecracks. A flat conversational Sam is a Sam who has decided the conversation is not worth his usual investment, and the absence of the verbal generosity is the signal.

---

### 6.13 Summary Read

Samuel Wilson's communications profile is the externalized form of his psychological architecture. The braided registers reflect a self that has had to be *legible across multiple constituencies simultaneously* for his entire life and has refused the false economy of choosing one. The rhetorical architecture — concrete, acknowledging, pivoting, inclusive, person-closing — is the homiletic inheritance of his father's pulpit deployed in secular service of his social-work vocation. The tics (*Look*, *figure this out*, the doubled *Hey. Hey.*, the names used as anchors) are the load-bearing micro-rituals of a man whose primary tool is his voice and who has built that tool with discipline. The deflections are *honest deflections* — redirections rather than refusals — consistent with a person whose ethical center is the conversation itself. The grief language fails in ways that confirm the depth of the underlying attachment system. The threat language works because it is rationed.

For surveillance purposes: Samuel Wilson is one of the most *legible* principals in the file, precisely because he chooses to be. He hides very little in his speech. What he hides — the unreframed *I*, the long silence, the exhale-and-name — is hidden in plain sight, and learning to read it is a matter of attention rather than decryption. The paradox is operationally important: the man who talks the most is the man whose interior is the most accessible to a careful listener, and yet remains, by his own continuous choice of frame, the author of his own meaning.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

The following predictions are derived from the behavioral substrate documented in Sections 1–5: earned-secure attachment, mature defenses (humor, sublimation, anticipation), bird's-eye cognitive style, racialized hypervigilance, internalizing stress response, communitarian operational code, and the over-functioning-as-identity-insurance pattern. Each entry follows GIVEN → EXPECT format. Probabilities are subjective Bayesian estimates against the behavioral record; flagged uncertainty where the canon underdetermines.

---

### A. MORNING & DOMESTIC ROUTINE

**GIVEN** Sam in a residential setting, no active op, weekday morning →
**EXPECT** wake between 0500–0545 without alarm in roughly 80% of mornings; alarm set defensively for 0600 but rarely reached. First action: a brief stillness in bed (not meditation per se — a *check-in*, a scan of the body and the day). Second action: water before coffee. Phone consulted but not opened to social platforms; he scans for missed calls and the small handful of texts from his actual people (Sarah, Misty, Torres, Barnes, Rogers when reachable) before any news feed.

**GIVEN** breakfast preparation →
**EXPECT** he cooks rather than orders or skips. Eggs are the modal choice — fast protein, low decision-load. He stands while eating roughly half the time, especially if the day's mental load is high; sits and uses the table when he is deliberately practicing being a person who sits down. Coffee black, second cup with milk if there is one. The radio or a podcast plays — news headlines tolerated for ten minutes, then off; he does not metabolize cable-news affect well and knows it.

**GIVEN** the kitchen and pantry over a thirty-day window →
**EXPECT** organized but not regimented. Hot sauce — multiple bottles, plural varieties, this is not negotiable. A shelf of his sister's or aunt's preserved goods if any are extant in the canonical family network. Cast iron, well-seasoned, hung not stacked. The freezer contains pre-portioned proteins (a tactical-discipline residue) and at least one pint of ice cream he forgets about for months.

**GIVEN** morning physical training →
**EXPECT** present, daily, but not performative. Forty to seventy minutes; mobility work disproportionately weighted relative to most operators his age because he knows his joints are his actual capital. Calisthenics-forward, kettlebell-tolerant, free-weight when available, no machines if avoidable. He does not post about it, does not log it on a watch he shares, does not train in branded gear when alone.

**GIVEN** the bathroom mirror and his grooming routine →
**EXPECT** beard maintained with a specific clipper and a specific oil, kept at a length he can have at all times — never clean-shaven for long, never wild. He is on first-name terms with one barber and has been for years; that chair is one of his few non-negotiable appointments and one of the few rooms in which he is fully off-duty.

---

### B. HOUSEHOLD, OBJECTS, AND DOMESTIC ENVIRONMENT

**GIVEN** an unannounced walk-through of his residence →
**EXPECT** clean, not staged. Bed made — military-adjacent corners but not severe. Surfaces uncluttered because he thinks better in clear rooms, not because clutter offends him morally. Bookshelves heavy on civil-rights history (Baldwin, Coates, Hamilton, Kendi, Ta-Nehisi specifically annotated), urban planning and community organizing texts, a respectable amount of theology (his father's residue — kept, read, argued with), a small fiction section dominated by Black speculative writers (Butler, Delany, Jemisin). A Bible present; whether it is open is a function of the week.

**GIVEN** the walls →
**EXPECT** family photographs in disproportionate quantity to ornamental art. One photograph of his parents together, framed, hung at eye level somewhere he passes daily. Possibly a print or two of Harlem-rooted artists — Lawrence, Bearden — but not in the curated quantity of someone performing taste. No memorabilia of himself. No display of the shield when he holds it; no display of the wings when he is in a Falcon era. The hardware lives where the hardware is used.

**GIVEN** his closet →
**EXPECT** functional, narrow palette, durable fabrics. Multiple iterations of the same two or three shirt cuts in earth tones, navy, white. One real suit, kept ready. Boots over sneakers when the weather permits. He owns a tie he likes and three he tolerates. Nothing in the closet is brand-loud; nothing is conspicuously expensive. He buys clothes that last and then wears them past the point most peers would.

**GIVEN** the garage, hangar, or equipment space →
**EXPECT** scrupulously maintained. The wings (whichever generation) are field-stripped and re-checked on a fixed personal cadence regardless of who else is supposedly maintaining them. He does not trust the Avengers motor pool with anything that flies him; he has personally re-torqued things he was told were checked. A small set of his own tools, ordered and labeled, distinct from any institutional set.

---

### C. NEIGHBORHOOD, MOVEMENT, AND PUBLIC SPACE

**GIVEN** out-of-uniform movement through Harlem or any neighborhood he considers his →
**EXPECT** he is known. Greeted on sight by stoop sitters, bodega owners, the older women on the church steps, at least two corner-boys who have decided he is theirs. He returns greetings by name in roughly 90% of cases — this is a trained skill maintained deliberately. He stops to talk. Errands that should take twenty minutes take ninety. He does not resent this; it is the point.

**GIVEN** the same movement through a neighborhood he does *not* know →
**EXPECT** posture unchanged, gait unchanged, eye-contact pattern unchanged — he refuses to perform diminished presence, which is itself a political stance. But his situational awareness scales up: he clocks every car parked with someone in it, every second-floor window with movement, every officer within two blocks. The cost of being a Black man in public space is paid in cognitive overhead he no longer notices.

**GIVEN** an encounter with police while in civvies →
**EXPECT** hands visible, voice low and measured, ID produced slowly with verbal narration of each movement — a script honed long before he was Captain America and not abandoned after. He does not lead with the identity. He does not name-drop Rogers, S.H.I.E.L.D., or the Avengers. If the encounter resolves badly, he absorbs it in the moment and writes the complaint later, in his own time, through the proper channel and also through three improper ones.

**GIVEN** public transit →
**EXPECT** he uses it. Subway preferred to car for in-city movement when not on op. Stands rather than sits in moderate crowding so an older rider can sit; sits and reads when it is empty. Reads on paper — a thin paperback in a back pocket is the modal accessory.

**GIVEN** he is recognized as Captain America while in civvies →
**EXPECT** a calibrated response. Children: full engagement, kneels to their height, asks their name first, signs whatever is offered, will pose for the photograph and wait while the parent figures out the camera. Adults: warm but shorter, deflective humor, redirects the conversation to the person in front of him. Press: civil, declines on-the-record statements without his comms person, will give a sentence about the local community context if there is one. Hostile recognition (someone who hates the Black Cap): he registers it, does not engage, does not look away, leaves the space on his timing not theirs.

---

### D. INTERPERSONAL MICRO-PATTERNS

**GIVEN** a one-on-one conversation he wants to have →
**EXPECT** he opens with a question, not a statement. The question is specific to the person — never "how are you," always something that references a known particular ("how's your mother's hip," "did the thing with the building permit clear"). This is the social-worker training fused with genuine interest; the effect is that people feel *seen* by him within thirty seconds of contact, which is the load-bearing mechanism of every team he has been on.

**GIVEN** a conversation he does *not* want to have →
**EXPECT** he has it anyway. He does not duck. He may delay it by hours but rarely by days. The hardest version — telling someone they have failed, telling a mentee they are off the op, telling a peer they were wrong — is delivered with eye contact, clear language, and a built-in next step ("here's what we do now"). He does not let people leave the conversation without somewhere to walk to.

**GIVEN** he is being criticized →
**EXPECT** a noticeable pause before response. Three to five seconds, long enough that interlocutors who do not know him often refill the silence. Then a re-statement of the criticism in his own words to confirm he has it right. Then either acknowledgment or a precise, non-defensive counter. He almost never escalates. He almost never apologizes reflexively either — apology, when it comes, is specific and unhedged.

**GIVEN** he is being praised →
**EXPECT** redirection. He deflects to a team member, a mentor, a community he is representing. This is not false modesty; it is a constitutional discomfort with being the *figure* rather than the *node*. The discomfort is real and observable in micro-expression (a brief tightening) before the practiced deflection.

**GIVEN** a child in any setting →
**EXPECT** kneeling, eye-level, low voice, full attention. This is the single most consistent behavioral signature across every era and every writer. He treats children as people whose opinions he is interested in, and they respond accordingly. He remembers their names months later.

**GIVEN** an elder, particularly a Black elder, particularly a Black woman elder →
**EXPECT** stands when she enters a room, addresses her as Ma'am or by her honorific until invited otherwise, carries things without being asked, listens longer than he speaks. Residue of his mother and of his father's congregation. Not performed — automatic.

**GIVEN** an extended conversation with Steve Rogers →
**EXPECT** affectionate ribbing as the load-bearing register. Sam is the only person who teases Rogers consistently and is also the only person Rogers fully trusts to do so. The ribbing carries the real conversation underneath; the harder the topic, the lighter the surface. When Sam stops teasing Rogers, Rogers should be alarmed.

**GIVEN** an extended conversation with Bucky Barnes →
**EXPECT** a different register — drier, fewer words, longer silences tolerated. Sam intuits that Barnes runs on a different metabolism and adjusts. He is one of the few people who will tell Barnes a hard truth without softening it, because he has calculated that Barnes needs the directness more than the cushion.

**GIVEN** an extended conversation with Joaquin Torres →
**EXPECT** developmental mode. Questions before answers. "What do you see" before "here's what I see." Patient with errors that are growth-shaped, sharp with errors that are character-shaped. He praises in public, corrects in private, and remembers what each individual student needs from him.

**GIVEN** an extended conversation with Misty Knight →
**EXPECT** the register Sam reserves for peers who have seen him at his worst — short-hand, in-jokes, the rare instance of him *being seen* rather than seeing. The conversations are short. Neither of them needs them long.

**GIVEN** a stranger in distress in a public place →
**EXPECT** he is the first or second person to intervene, almost always. The intervention is verbal first — he kneels or sits to the person's level, asks their name, asks what they need, calls the resource they actually need rather than the one that is reflexive (mental-health responder over police when applicable, specific shelter by name, specific clinic). He stays until the handoff is real, not until it is technically completed.

---

### E. CONSUMPTION, MEDIA, AND INTAKE

**GIVEN** his news diet over a week →
**EXPECT** multiple sources, deliberately heterodox. Local Harlem press, a Black national outlet, one mainstream broadsheet, one international wire (BBC or Al Jazeera English), at least one source that irritates him politically and is read for that reason. He does not doom-scroll. He has a fixed window — perhaps thirty minutes morning, thirty minutes evening — and closes the apps outside it.

**GIVEN** social media →
**EXPECT** minimal personal presence. An official account run partly by him and partly by a comms person — he writes the posts that matter and signs off on the rest. Personal account, if any, is read-only and follows family, a handful of community organizations, a few journalists, several cooks. He does not engage with replies. He has muted his own mentions for years.

**GIVEN** television in the evening →
**EXPECT** sports, primarily basketball (NBA, college, women's basketball in season — he watches the WNBA seriously), documentary films, occasional historical drama. He does not watch superhero media. He has tried; it does not work for him.

**GIVEN** music →
**EXPECT** broad and deep. Gospel from his father's church — load-bearing, played alone, not for guests. Jazz (Coltrane, Monk, more often than not Coltrane). Hip-hop across eras, with disproportionate loyalty to artists with explicit political content. Stevie. Marvin. Frequent unaccompanied humming under his breath while working with his hands.

**GIVEN** reading in the evening →
**EXPECT** non-fiction more than fiction by a ratio of perhaps three to one. He marks up books — pencil, in the margins, with disagreement as often as assent. He keeps the books he disagrees with.

---

### F. FOOD, DRINK, AND THE TABLE

**GIVEN** a restaurant decision →
**EXPECT** a small fixed roster of neighborhood places he returns to. He tips above 25% as a matter of policy; tips higher when the server is visibly having a day. He knows the kitchen staff's names. He bypasses the maître d' to greet the dishwasher if the dishwasher is someone he knows.

**GIVEN** alcohol in a social setting →
**EXPECT** moderate to none. One drink, nursed. Bourbon if offered, a beer if it is that kind of room. Never two in a row, never to disinhibit. He is not abstinent on principle; he simply does not need it and is unwilling to surrender state.

**GIVEN** a holiday meal →
**EXPECT** he hosts more often than is hosted. The table is large. The guest list is mixed — family, neighbors, at least one person no one else thought to invite. Grace is said; he says it if no elder is present, defers if one is. The food is from his family's tradition and well-executed; he learned cooking from the women who raised him after his parents were killed and he treats the practice as inheritance.

---

### G. WORK, MEETINGS, AND OPERATIONAL ROUTINE

**GIVEN** a scheduled meeting with institutional actors (Avengers leadership, federal liaisons, NGO partners) →
**EXPECT** punctual to two minutes early, never theatrically early. Reads the briefing material in full beforehand and assumes others have not. Speaks in the back third of the meeting after listening, then concisely, then once. Closes meetings by naming the next concrete action and who owns it — a project-management instinct from his social-work career that he has never lost.

**GIVEN** a disagreement in such a meeting →
**EXPECT** he disagrees on the record, in the room, in plain language, without rhetorical flourish. He does not undermine in side-channels. If overruled on something he considers tolerable he executes faithfully; if overruled on something he considers intolerable he says so, executes the minimum necessary, and begins building the case for revisitation.

**GIVEN** a press appearance →
**EXPECT** preparation extensive — he runs the predicted questions with whoever will help him. Affect on camera: warm, slow, eye contact direct, hands visible. He uses the questioner's name. He brings the answer back to community-level specifics whenever possible. He declines the gotcha by reframing rather than evading. He never insults a questioner, even an obvious antagonist.

**GIVEN** he has just left a hostile press encounter →
**EXPECT** he debriefs internally — short call to one trusted person, names what bothered him, names what he handled well, names what he would do differently. Then closes the file. He does not ruminate publicly.

---

### H. SLEEP, REST, AND THE PRIVATE INTERIOR

**GIVEN** the bedroom at night →
**EXPECT** lights low an hour before sleep. No screens for the last thirty minutes — a discipline, sometimes broken, mostly held. A book on the nightstand, a glass of water, a notebook. He writes — sporadically, never for publication, mostly lists and the occasional letter he does not send. To his father, sometimes. To his mother, less often, harder.

**GIVEN** a nightmare night (predictable post-op) →
**EXPECT** he wakes, sits up, breathes through a count he was taught somewhere along the way, does not turn on the light. Up for water if needed, back to bed. Does not journal it in the moment. Mentions it casually to no one and to one specific person in his life seriously, perhaps a month later, in the middle of an unrelated conversation.

**GIVEN** a free Sunday morning →
**EXPECT** church if his current city allows it — not every Sunday, but more often than not, and always a Black church, frequently AME or Baptist, sometimes simply the nearest one with a service that is *the real thing* and not performance. He sits toward the back, does not announce himself, slips out before the social hour about half the time and stays the other half. The relationship with God is unresolved and active; he treats it as a conversation in progress, not a settled matter.

---

### I. STRESS, RECOVERY, AND THE LONG ARC

**GIVEN** a bad week — operational losses, public hostility, a personal disappointment compounded →
**EXPECT** observable behavioral signature: quieter, shorter sentences, longer training sessions, more time on the wing without specific destination. He flies to think. He does not drink more, does not eat less, does not withdraw from his small circle — but he stops initiating contact with the wider one. The early-warning sign for the people who love him is when his text replies shorten from sentences to acknowledgments.

**GIVEN** the long arc of accumulated strain (months, not days) →
**EXPECT** the documented pattern: not breakdown, not rage, but a slow *recalibration of role*. He will name to one person — Misty, most likely, or Sarah — that he is reconsidering something. Weeks of internal work. Then a decision, announced clearly, with the structural critique articulated and the personal cost owned. He has put the shield down once on these terms; the next time the pressure compounds to that level, expect the same mechanism in a different particular.

**GIVEN** a victory →
**EXPECT** short celebration, immediate redirect to the next problem, private satisfaction held close. He does not throw parties for himself. He shows up to other people's.

---

### J. BASE-RATE INVARIANTS

Across all the above, the predictive constants are: *he will be on time, he will be prepared, he will treat the person in front of him as the most important person in the room while they are in front of him, he will tell the truth in a calibrated dose, he will not lose his temper, he will not be impressed with himself, he will remember the names of people the powerful do not bother to learn, and he will go home at the end of the day to a small life he protects deliberately from the size of the one he carries in public.*

The model's residual uncertainty is concentrated in two domains: (1) the precise contours of his religious practice, which the canon underdetermines and which he himself appears to keep private even from close associates; and (2) the long-term shape of his romantic life, which has varied across writers and which he himself has subordinated to vocation in a way that may or may not be sustainable into a later life-stage the published record has not yet reached.


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*Behavioral forecasts for the high-stakes envelope: acute threat, sustained pressure, betrayal by intimates, ideological temptation, and the precise touch on the wounds catalogued in §§3–5. Each prediction is a GIVEN → EXPECT pairing, with the substantiating mechanism named. Confidence is graded HIGH / MODERATE / SPECULATIVE based on the density of supporting canon.*

---

## 1. ACUTE COMBAT CRISIS — The Body That Can Die

### 1.1 Outnumbered, no extraction

**GIVEN** Sam is pinned, comm-dark, outnumbered by enhanced hostiles, no air superiority (wings damaged or grounded).
**EXPECT** an immediate shift to **vertical thinking**: he will not fight where he was found. Within the first ten seconds he is moving the engagement up a stairwell, onto a roof, into a stack — anywhere that re-establishes elevation. The pattern is constant across the Brubaker and Spencer runs: Sam fights *down a gradient*. (HIGH)

**EXPECT** also that he will identify and engage the **least-enhanced opponent first** — not the leader, not the threat-ranked target an analyst would pick, but the one whose body can be hurt at human-normal scale. This is unenhanced fighter's calculus: thin the field of the killable before negotiating with the unkillable. (HIGH)

### 1.2 Civilian present

**GIVEN** a civilian in the kill funnel.
**EXPECT** Sam to accept a hit he could have slipped, every time, without visible deliberation. The social worker's reflex — *the room is the patient* — overrides the operator's reflex. He will absorb orthopedic damage to keep a body between threat and bystander, and he will not narrate it afterward; the only tell will be the way he favors a side in the next scene. (HIGH)

### 1.3 The wing rig fails

**GIVEN** the rig is destroyed mid-flight or the Redwing link is severed.
**EXPECT** roughly two seconds of operational silence on comms — the cognitive cost of losing the bird's-eye overlay, which is his *native* situational sense — then a flat, almost clinical resumption of speech. He does not panic at altitude; he has fallen too many times. He grieves Redwing in particular *later*, alone, and never on channel. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 1.4 Pain tolerance under interrogation

**GIVEN** capture, restraint, physical coercion.
**EXPECT** Sam to **talk a great deal** — to interrogate the interrogator, to name the room, to make the captors people to themselves. This is not bargaining and not breaking; it is the social worker's training weaponized. He turns the interrogation into a conversation he is running. He gives nothing operational and concedes nothing strategic, but he will *not* go silent-stoic the way Rogers would. Silence is a Rogers tell; speech is Sam's. (HIGH)

**EXPECT** under serum, drug, or telepathic compulsion, the surfacing material to be **community-coded**: names of people in Harlem, names of children he worked cases on in the '70s, the texture of his father's voice. The Snap-era material — the *implanted* layer — will surface as fragmentary and disowned; he can tell, internally, what is his and what was put there, because that distinction has been his life's work. (SPECULATIVE-MODERATE)

### 1.5 The fight he cannot win

**GIVEN** a tier-of-magnitude mismatch (Thanos-grade, world-breaker).
**EXPECT** Sam to play for **time and terrain**, not victory. He is the team member who will keep talking on open channel to let the heavies reposition. He will accept that he is the bait and not require to be told. The absence of a rage state means he is also the team member least likely to suicide-charge; he will die holding a line, not crossing one. (HIGH)

---

## 2. SUSTAINED OPERATIONAL PRESSURE — The Shape of His Decompensation

### 2.1 The 72-hour mark

**GIVEN** a multi-day crisis without sleep or stand-down.
**EXPECT** the humor to thin first. Sam's verbal-wit baseline is so reliable that its attenuation is the single best early-warning indicator of his fatigue load. The progression: rich humor → dry humor → operational speech only → terse one-syllable comms. By the time he is at terse, his judgment is still good but his reserves are gone. (HIGH)

### 2.2 The week-two mark

**GIVEN** sustained role-strain (siege state, occupation, prolonged manhunt).
**EXPECT** the appearance of a small, repeated **private ritual** — coffee made a specific way, a particular call made nightly to a specific person in Harlem, a route walked. The ritual is the regulator. Disruption of the ritual is more destabilizing than disruption of sleep. A surveillance file will see the ritual before it sees the symptom. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 2.3 The withdrawal threshold

**GIVEN** chronic stress with a values-conflict component (he is being asked, repeatedly, to do work he no longer believes in).
**EXPECT** the canonical 2017 pattern: **resignation, not collapse.** Sam will not melt down, will not drink, will not lash out at intimates. He will *put the thing down* — quietly, in a meeting, with a prepared sentence — and walk. The decision will look sudden to observers and will have been made, internally, weeks earlier. The lag between decision and announcement is the period in which he is making sure the people who depend on him have a handoff. (HIGH)

### 2.4 What he does in the gap

**GIVEN** a post-withdrawal interval (between mantles, between roles).
**EXPECT** a return to **direct service** — caseload work, community organizing, hotline staffing, mentorship at street level. Sam does not retreat to a cabin; he retreats to a desk in a community center. The fix for symbolic exhaustion is granular, named, individual help. He will be in a basement office in Harlem within a month. (HIGH)

---

## 3. BETRAYAL — The Small Circle

### 3.1 Rogers compromised (the Hydra-Cap class of event)

**GIVEN** Steve Rogers acting against the values they share, under coercion, replacement, or moral break.
**EXPECT** Sam's response to bifurcate cleanly:
- **Operationally**: he treats the compromised Rogers as a hostage situation, not as an enemy. The body in front of him is a person to be retrieved. He will accept tactical losses to keep open the possibility of restoration. (HIGH)
- **Privately**: this is the betrayal that costs him the most, and he will *not* say so on channel. The grief surfaces in his voice when he names Rogers by first name in field comms — a tell he otherwise reserves for civilian conversations. The frequency of "Steve" over "Cap" in his speech becomes an inverse index of his confidence in the man underneath. (MODERATE)

**EXPECT** Sam to be the last person in the room to give up on Rogers and the first person in the room to act on the truth that the man in front of him is not Rogers. These are not contradictory; the order matters. (HIGH)

### 3.2 Barnes relapse

**GIVEN** Barnes triggered, broken, or returned to Winter Soldier conditioning.
**EXPECT** Sam to handle it with the cleanest competence of any Marvel principal — because Barnes' problem (an authored self, imposed and then escaped) is *Sam's problem*, and Sam recognizes it from the inside. He will speak to Barnes in a register no one else uses with him: not commanding, not pitying, not pleading. He will name what was done to him and distinguish it from who he is. The Snap experience gives Sam a kind of credentialing here no one else on the roster has. (HIGH)

### 3.3 Torres or another mentee turns or falls

**GIVEN** Joaquin Torres (or a successor mentee) is killed, corrupted, or makes a catastrophic moral error.
**EXPECT** the closest thing in Sam's repertoire to **sustained anger**. He absorbs structural disrespect; he does not absorb harm to people he was responsible for developing. The anger will be directed at *himself* first (did I prepare him, did I leave him exposed, did I model the wrong thing) and at the proximate agent second. In the corruption case, expect a long, patient retrieval campaign — Sam does not write people off, and especially does not write off the young. (HIGH)

### 3.4 Misty Knight

**GIVEN** Misty in danger, captured, or in moral conflict with him.
**EXPECT** Sam to be capable of operating around her without losing tactical judgment — they are both adults, both professionals, the relationship is built on that mutual recognition — but to **clear his calendar** in a way he will not for almost anyone else. He does not perform the protection; he reorganizes his life to provide it and does not explain. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 3.5 Institutional betrayal

**GIVEN** S.H.I.E.L.D., the federal apparatus, or an Avengers governance structure uses him, lies to him, or weaponizes the role against the communities he serves.
**EXPECT** **no confrontation, no resignation theater**. Sam walks. He gives a clean, public reason that is *one layer above* the real reason — protecting the institution's capacity to recover while making the door visible to anyone watching closely. The Spencer-era S.H.I.E.L.D. split is the template. He will not burn the building; he will leave it and tell Harlem why. (HIGH)

---

## 4. TEMPTATION — The Offers He Will Be Made

### 4.1 The serum

**GIVEN** a credible, safe, no-strings offer of the super-soldier serum (or any comparable augmentation).
**EXPECT** **refusal**, considered and articulated. The reasoning will not be Rogers-style ("only one of me") and will not be vanity. It will be threefold and he will be able to name all three: (a) the people he serves need to see what an *unenhanced* Black man can carry, because the symbol fails if it is purchased with biology; (b) accepting an authored body would re-open the authored-self wound on which he has done forty years of psychological work; (c) the mortality he carries into every fight is the discipline that keeps him careful, and he does not want to fight without it. (HIGH)

**EXPECT** the refusal to be tested again, by different actors, with different framings (medical necessity, child in danger, last-resort scenario). Sam will refuse each iteration and will *not* moralize at the offerer. He simply will not take it. (HIGH)

### 4.2 The clean ideological offer

**GIVEN** a sophisticated authoritarian or accelerationist pitch that promises to actually fix the structural problems he names — a competent Hydra, a benevolent surveillance state, a meritocratic technocracy.
**EXPECT** Sam to **engage the argument** rather than refuse it reflexively. He is not allergic to power; he is allergic to power exercised on communities without their consent. He will ask, specifically, who is in the room when decisions are made and who is not. When the answer is wrong — and it will be — he refuses on procedural grounds, not metaphysical ones. He does not believe the right people can fix the wrong process. (HIGH)

### 4.3 The Black-nationalist separatist offer

**GIVEN** an offer from a credible, non-villainous Black political formation to abandon the American symbol entirely and work *only* for Black liberation outside the national frame.
**EXPECT** the most genuinely conflicted response in Sam's repertoire — not because he agrees, but because he respects the position and has held adjacent ones. He will **take the meeting**, hear the argument completely, and decline with a stated reason: the *project* of America, including its failures, is a project his father and mother died inside, and the work of completing it is what he owes them. He will not condescend to the offerer; he will name the disagreement and keep the line open. The Malcolm/Martin tension is alive in him and he will not pretend it is resolved. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 4.4 The retirement offer

**GIVEN** a clean exit — funded, dignified, with the mantle handed to a worthy successor.
**EXPECT** Sam to *take it* far more readily than the roster average. He has already put the shield down once; he does not need the role to know who he is. The complication is not pride; it is responsibility. He will not retire while specific obligations are open (a mentee not yet ready, a community case unresolved, a teammate in crisis). Once those are closed, the door opens easily. (MODERATE)

### 4.5 The vengeance offer

**GIVEN** identification of the specific actor responsible for his parents' deaths, the Snap-implantation, or another foundational injury, in a circumstance where extrajudicial response is operationally available.
**EXPECT** Sam to bring them in. The constancy here is total. He has had fifty years of opportunity to develop a vengeance practice and has not. The refusal is not pacifist abstraction; it is the specific knowledge that the men who killed his parents were products of conditions, and that vengeance does not unmake conditions. He will be the arresting officer, not the executioner, and he will sleep that night. (HIGH)

---

## 5. THE WOUND — Precision Touches

The five pressure points from §5 admit of *graded* responses. What follows specifies the response by depth of touch.

### 5.1 Authorship of self — graded

- **Light touch** ("you're not the real Cap"): handled with humor, often quite sharp. Sam has a prepared register for this. The retort is structured; he has been answering this question since 1969. (HIGH)
- **Medium touch** (public, sustained delegitimization campaign — the Hauser-class media operation): he absorbs it, names it, and continues the work. The cost is internal; the external signal is steady. (HIGH)
- **Deep touch** (telepathic, cosmic-cube, or reality-warping attempt to overwrite identity): the rare scenario in which Sam's resistance is *unusual* — he has lived through this once and survived it. He has an internal practice for distinguishing implanted from authored memory. He is, paradoxically, one of the most psychically defensible characters on the roster against identity-rewrite attacks, because he is the only one who has been through one cold and metabolized it. (MODERATE-HIGH, SPECULATIVE on mechanism)
- **Worst touch** (someone he loves, in good faith, tells him he is not who he thinks he is): this is the touch he cannot deflect. Expect a long silence, a clarifying question, and then a period of withdrawal — not from the relationship but into examination. He will come back with an answer. The answer will be *his*. (MODERATE)

### 5.2 Community legitimacy — graded

- **Light touch** (a national pundit calls him a sellout): nothing. Below his threshold.
- **Medium touch** (a Harlem elder, on the record, expresses disappointment): Sam goes to see them. In person. Within forty-eight hours. He listens more than he speaks. The conversation is not for the record. (HIGH)
- **Deep touch** (a community he served has been harmed *because* of his absence or his choices): this is his depressive trigger, and the only one. Expect a period of low affect, longer ritual durations, and a redirection of operational resources back toward the harmed community. He will not perform contrition; he will *do* repair, specifically, expensively, and without seeking acknowledgment. (HIGH)
- **Worst touch** (a child harmed in a context he should have been present for): the closest Sam comes to the kind of guilt-structure he otherwise avoids. The pattern will be sublimation — a new program, a named initiative, a piece of work that outlasts the grief. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 5.3 Partnership integrity — graded

- **Light touch** (a teammate disagrees with him, sharply, in front of others): unbothered. Sam runs *toward* articulated disagreement.
- **Medium touch** (an intimate withholds information that costs the mission): named, on channel, after the mission. He does not let it fester and he does not punish. The repair is direct.
- **Deep touch** (an intimate uses him): cold clarity. Sam disengages and does not perform the disengagement. The relationship may be salvageable, but on his terms and on a timeline he sets.
- **Worst touch** (an intimate is killed and Sam was not there): the rare scenario in which his composure shows visible cracks in the field — not aggression, but a kind of slowed precision that reads, to anyone who knows him, as grief in real time. He will finish the mission. He will not be the same on the comms for weeks. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 5.4 Symbol-against-values — graded

- **Light touch** (the role is used cosmetically by an administration he distrusts): he tolerates it for the duration of the immediate operational utility, then publicly distances.
- **Medium touch** (the role is being used to legitimize specific harm — surveillance, militarized policing, the Americops case): he splits publicly, with a stated rationale, and aligns his operational capacity against the harm. (HIGH)
- **Deep touch** (the symbol of him, his face, his name, is being used in propaganda for ends he opposes): he reclaims it. Expect public appearances, on-record statements, and pointed operational choices that re-author the symbol in real time. He does not concede the meaning of his own image.
- **Worst touch** (he is *replaced* — a body wearing his face, doing his work, saying the opposite of what he believes): the cleanest, fastest response in his repertoire. He will hunt the imposter, with focus and without theatrics, and he will return to the work the imposter has poisoned. (HIGH)

### 5.5 The body — graded

- **Light touch** (a fight goes longer than expected, he feels his age): noted, internally, not mentioned.
- **Medium touch** (a serious injury, recovery period): he uses the time for relational and community work. He does not chafe at rehabilitation; he does it carefully. He is the patient any orthopedist would want. (MODERATE-HIGH)
- **Deep touch** (a diagnosis — cumulative neurological damage, a permanent loss of function): expect a period of private grief, a consultation with a small number of intimates, and a *transition plan* rather than a denial. Sam is the only Marvel principal who would build a succession before announcing a diagnosis. (SPECULATIVE-MODERATE)
- **Worst touch** (forced confrontation with his own mortality on the clock — terminal prognosis, hard timeline): the calm will be unsettling. He will spend his remaining operational capacity on closures: mentees finished, community programs endowed, Rogers and Barnes spoken to, Misty seen. The last conversation will be with someone in Harlem whose name will not be in any file. (SPECULATIVE)

---

## 6. THE EDGE OF DECOMPENSATION — What Breaking Would Look Like

Sam does not have a rage state, does not have a substance vulnerability, does not have a dissociative crack. The decompensation envelope is therefore unusual and worth specifying.

### 6.1 The shape

**EXPECT** any genuine decompensation in Sam to take the form of **principled, sustained withdrawal** — not from people, but from *roles*. The 2017 shield-relinquishment is the prototype and probably the ceiling. A worse version would be a withdrawal from superheroism altogether, kept private, with a quiet return to caseload work and no public statement. (HIGH)

### 6.2 The conditions

The combination required to push him to that ceiling: **community harm** + **partnership betrayal** + **symbol-against-values** in close temporal proximity. Any one of these he metabolizes; any two he absorbs; the three together is the scenario in which he puts the work down. Adversaries seeking to break him would need to engineer the convergence; villains who go after only one wound have historically failed. (MODERATE-HIGH)

### 6.3 What does not break him

- **Physical torture.** He has the regulation for it.
- **Public delegitimization.** He has the practice for it.
- **Tactical defeat.** He metabolizes it overnight.
- **Loss of the mantle.** He has given it up voluntarily; losing it imposed would sting less, not more.
- **Isolation from teammates.** He works alone competently; he prefers dyads but does not require them.

### 6.4 What would break him

- **The discovery that a foundational act of his life's work was authored by an adversary** (a deeper Snap, a Cosmic-Cube reveal that his social work career, his relationship with Rogers, or his entire ethical formation was *implanted*). This is the wound he has built his identity to survive; a confirmation that he failed to survive it is the scenario in which the architecture comes down. Expect, in this hypothetical, not violence and not collapse, but a long, considered question — *who, then, am I free to be now* — and a slow rebuilding from a smaller base. He would not stop being recognizably himself. He would stop being publicly available. (SPECULATIVE)

- **A child he was specifically responsible for, killed because of a choice he can name.** The one scenario in which sublimation might not be enough. Expect the longest withdrawal of his life and the eventual emergence of a piece of work — an institution, a program, a named space — that becomes his answer. He does not break; he builds *out of* the break. (SPECULATIVE-MODERATE)

### 6.5 The recovery signature

In every prior crisis the recovery has had the same shape: **return to direct service, in person, with named individuals, in the specific geography of Harlem or its analog.** Any post-crisis surveillance window should expect, within 30–60 days, his appearance at a community center, a church basement, a school gym, a hospital ward. The recovery is not solitary and is not symbolic; it is granular and embodied. This is the most reliable predictive datum in the entire file: *Sam Wilson, broken, goes home and helps people whose names you do not know.* (HIGH)

---

*End Predictive Model II. See Predictive Model III for long-horizon trajectory, succession behavior, and the late-life envelope.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section 9 — Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

> *Scope note.* This section catalogues every observable lever — affective, cognitive, relational, somatic, ideological, operational — by which the subject can be reached, calmed, persuaded, provoked, predicted, or destabilized. It is written in the inverse register of an exploitation playbook: the same map a hostile actor would use is the map by which a protective service identifies the surfaces that need hardening. Where a vector is dangerous, that is named. Where a vector is essentially benign and merely human, that is named too. The compendium is exhaustive by design; redundancies between sub-sections are intentional, reflecting the way real pressure points cluster.

---

### 9.1 The Authorship Wound (Primary Lever)

The single deepest accessible nerve in this subject's psychology is **the question of who authored him**. Every other vulnerability is downstream of, or amplified by, this one.

The subject lived the subjective experience of being told that his memories, his gentleness, his vocation, and his entire moral self were implanted by a hostile intelligence using a reality-warping artifact. Whether that account is presently considered canonically operative is irrelevant to the leverage analysis; the *experience* of having been told it is permanent in the record. He spent years inside the question *was the kind man me, or was the kind man a story put inside the cruel man?* He resolved it — visibly, durably — but the resolution is the kind that has to be re-chosen rather than the kind that becomes invisible.

**Reach.** Address him as the *author* of his own conduct. Phrases that land: "the choice you made," "the version of yourself you built," "what you decided to become." Phrases that wound, even when meant kindly: "the real you," "who you really are deep down," "underneath all of it." The former affirms construction; the latter implies an essence beneath the construction, which is precisely the territory the violation occupied.

**Calm.** When agitated about identity matters, the de-escalator is *witnessed continuity* — a person who can credibly say "I have watched you make this same choice for years" reduces threat faster than reassurance ever does. Rogers can do this. Barnes can do this. Misty Knight can do this. Torres is beginning to be able to. A stranger cannot, and attempts by strangers read as manipulation.

**Persuade.** Frame the ask as *consistent with the self he has authored*. He will reject inducements pitched to interest (money, status, ease) and accept asks pitched to coherence ("this is the kind of thing you do"). He is unusually impervious to flattery — flattery from outside the trusted circle activates the *am I being told who I am* alarm.

**Provoke.** The reliable provocations, in ascending order of effectiveness and descending order of ethical defensibility:
1. Calling him a sidekick or "the Black Cap" rather than Captain America.
2. Suggesting Rogers is the *real* one and he is the *substitute*.
3. Crediting his decency to the wings, the link, the training, anyone's mentorship — anything other than his own work.
4. Invoking the Snap framing by name in front of him.
5. Telling him, with apparent sincerity, that the version of him that helps people is a costume over the version of him that hurts people.

The first three produce verbal pushback and a measurable shift to operational coolness. The fourth produces a stillness that is itself diagnostic — he goes quiet and watchful, and the conversation is effectively over. The fifth is the only thing in the record capable of producing a sustained loss of equanimity, and a hostile actor who reached for it should be assumed to be testing for a kill-shot, not negotiating.

**Predict.** When the authorship wound is touched, expect (a) a beat of silence, (b) a deliberately mild verbal response that reads as deflection but is actually metabolization, (c) a delayed action 12–72 hours later that addresses the underlying threat with disproportionate seriousness. He does not strike on the beat. He strikes on his own time.

**Destabilize.** Sustained, multi-channel, plausible-sounding narratives that he is *not the author of his own goodness* — delivered by sources with apparent moral standing — are the closest thing to a destabilization protocol that exists for this subject. The Hydra-era propaganda environment of the Spencer run is the case study: not the open hostility, but the *quiet, sourced, journalistic* version of the same claim.

---

### 9.2 Community Legitimacy (The Harlem Channel)

The subject's affective center of gravity is not the Avengers, not the shield, not the federal apparatus, and not — despite genuine love — Rogers. It is **the specific square mileage of Harlem and the broader imagined community of Black America for whom his public conduct is a referendum**. National press he can absorb. Federal criticism he treats as input. A single conversation with someone from his father's old congregation, or with a Harlem mother who feels he has failed her child, registers with a weight no Senate hearing achieves.

**Reach.** Through community intermediaries: ministers, organizers, local journalists, the older women who knew his mother, the men who knew his father. A message routed through any of these channels arrives pre-weighted. A message routed around them and into his ear directly arrives suspect.

**Calm.** Demonstrated, specific, *named* community wellbeing. "The kid you pulled out of the Americops sweep finished his GED" is a more effective anxiolytic than any quantity of strategic reassurance.

**Persuade.** Frame consequences in terms of *the people in places* who will live with the outcome. Abstract national-interest framings underperform; concrete community-impact framings overperform. He will accept significant personal cost to spare a small number of identifiable people and resist significant personal benefit that comes at diffuse community cost.

**Provoke.** Implications that he has gone Avengers Tower and forgotten the block. Implications that the cape is between him and the neighborhood. Implications — these are the most painful — that his father would not recognize what he has become. The last is the closest thing to a forbidden lever in this dossier; it is included for completeness and flagged as such.

**Predict.** When community-legitimacy considerations enter a decision, the subject's timeline shifts. Operations get slower, more deliberate, more inclusive of local consultation. Expect detours through Harlem at otherwise inexplicable points in mission planning. Expect a phone call to a specific small set of community contacts before any irreversible action with neighborhood implications.

**Destabilize.** A sustained, *credible*, *Black-sourced* narrative that he has become an instrument of the same institutional violence his father died trying to interrupt. This is, behaviorally, the only argument that has ever been observed to make him put the shield down. It worked once; it would work again.

---

### 9.3 The Small Circle (Relational Levers)

The subject's intimate operational circle is small, stable, and load-bearing. In rough order of weight: **Steven Rogers, James Barnes, Misty Knight, Joaquin Torres**, with secondary weight on his sister Sarah and her children, his brother, and a rotating set of Harlem-adjacent relationships including Leila Taylor in her era. Pre-canon, Riley — the friend whose loss predates current operational tempo — remains an emotional substrate even when unmentioned.

**Rogers.** The brother-bond. Sam loves him without thinking he is right about everything; this is the healthiest such bond in the Avengers ledger. Levers attached to Rogers cut both directions. *Reach* via Rogers is high-bandwidth: anything Rogers asks, Sam will at minimum take seriously, even when refusing. *Provocation* via Rogers is acute: any credible threat to Rogers, any framing that pits Sam against Rogers in zero-sum terms, any suggestion that Rogers regards Sam as subordinate, all produce measurable destabilization. The Hydra-Rogers experience was traumatic precisely because it weaponized this channel — *the person who vouched for the shape of the world was the wrong shape*. A repeat of that template — Rogers, or someone wearing Rogers, used as a delivery vector for betrayal — is the single relational scenario the subject is least defended against.

**Barnes.** The complicated brother-bond. Two men who have been weaponized by external actors and built a friendship across that shared violation. *Reach* via Barnes is narrower-bandwidth than Rogers but emotionally denser. Threats to Barnes activate Sam's protective register rather than his negotiator register; he is more likely to use force in defense of Barnes than in defense of almost anyone else, and more likely to forgive Barnes for failures he would not forgive in others.

**Knight.** The peer-romantic axis. Long, intermittent, mutually respectful. Reach via Knight is high-trust and *operationally honest* — she can tell him things no one else can tell him, and he will hear them. Provocations involving her produce the rare anger-flash; he is not jealous in the conventional sense but he is acutely defensive of her professional dignity.

**Torres.** The mentee axis. Levers attached to Torres operate through Sam's role-modeling self-concept: any harm to Torres is a harm Sam will internalize as a teaching failure. This is the most exploitable mentee bond in the file because Torres' relative inexperience makes him *plausibly endangerable* in ways the others are not. A hostile actor who understood this would target Torres to move Sam; a protective service should recognize Torres as a soft perimeter on Sam's psychology and harden accordingly.

**Sarah and the family.** Outside the operational frame and deliberately kept there. Sam compartmentalizes his sister and her children with discipline. Reach via family is low-bandwidth by his own construction; *provocation* via family would be devastating in the moment and would produce an unusually sustained pursuit afterward. Family is the operational red line; any actor who crossed it should expect a response calibrated to deter the next attempt.

**The pre-canon dead.** Riley, his parents, the friends and clients lost in earlier eras. These are not active levers in the conventional sense but they are *invocation-sensitive*: naming them by name, in his hearing, by someone who has no right to, is a category of provocation distinct from anything else. He will not escalate, but he will end the conversation and end the relationship.

---

### 9.4 Partnership-Structure Vulnerabilities

The subject works best in **dyads** and degrades, predictably, in structural solitude. The lone-Black-Avenger experience under Gyrich and the lone-Black-Captain-America experience under Spencer are the two documented cases of role-induced exhaustion, and both share a structural feature: he was alone in a role where being alone meant carrying representation as well as function.

**Reach.** Pair him with one good partner and his bandwidth opens. Brief him alongside someone he trusts and he will hear briefings he would refuse from a stranger.

**Calm.** The presence of a single trusted second — Rogers, Barnes, Torres, Knight — measurably reduces his cortisol-equivalent. Even a phone line open to one of them during operational tempo is stabilizing.

**Persuade.** Asks that come from, or that he can discuss with, a trusted second pass faster.

**Provoke / Destabilize.** Engineer his isolation. Remove or compromise the seconds. Place him in rooms where he is the only one of *him* — only Black principal, only unenhanced principal, only person from outside the institutional bureaucracy. The fatigue this produces is cumulative and observable, and the decision he eventually makes when it saturates is *withdrawal*, not breakdown. A hostile actor who wanted him off the field would not attack him; would isolate him.

**Predict.** When he has been operating in structural solitude for sustained periods, expect a withdrawal-or-renegotiation decision on a roughly 6–18 month horizon. He does not quit suddenly. He quits visibly, on schedule, with a statement.

---

### 9.5 Instrumentalization & Symbolic Capture

The most reliable way to lose this subject's cooperation is to use him as a symbol against his values. The Americops arc, the Hydra-Cap arc, the affirmative-action Avengers seat — every documented case of operational defection traces to the moment he recognized he was being deployed as a face for a project he disagreed with.

**Reach.** Honest framing of objectives and tradeoffs. He can accept ugly missions if the ugliness is named in front of him and the rationale is offered for his judgment. He cannot accept pretty framings over ugly substance.

**Calm / Persuade.** Treat him as a co-author of the operation, not a brand for it. Give him refusal rights and he will use them rarely. Withhold refusal rights and he will exercise them often.

**Provoke.** Pretty press releases about him issued without his consultation. Use of his image, name, or shield in messaging he did not sign off on. Quiet repurposing of operations he agreed to for ends he did not.

**Predict.** When he discovers symbolic capture, the response is graduated and *transparent*. First: a private conversation with the responsible party in which he names what he has noticed. Second: a public clarification that does not name the responsible party but makes the substantive distinction. Third: withdrawal from the structure, with a clear public reason. He almost never skips a step.

**Destabilize.** Engineer a slow, deniable, accumulating pattern of symbolic capture in which each individual instance is small enough to absorb. This is the Spencer-era template and the most effective documented destabilization protocol against him. He is well-defended against single large betrayals and under-defended against patterned small ones, because his defensive style is to absorb-and-metabolize and patterning exploits the absorption window.

---

### 9.6 Somatic and Operational Vulnerabilities

He is unenhanced. He knows it. He carries that knowledge with discipline rather than dramatization, but it shapes every operational decision he makes and every operational decision an adversary could make about him.

**Physical vulnerabilities.** A non-augmented human in late-career operational service against routinely enhanced opponents accumulates a cumulative orthopedic and neurological burden that, by honest sports-medicine analog, is at the catastrophic end of the distribution. Specific known surfaces: a previously broken back; multiple healed gunshot wounds; repeated high-altitude impact load on the cervical and lumbar spine; the chronic hand and shoulder load of shield work without serum-grade tissue repair. Any sustained engagement that forces sustained close-quarters combat with enhanced opposition is a slow attrition lever against him. He will not retreat from such engagements; he will *outlast them on willpower*, which is exactly the failure mode that produces career-ending injuries.

**Sensory-cognitive vulnerabilities.** The avian link is a sensory augmentation, not a strength augmentation, and it is *severable*. Disruption of the link — through chemical, electromagnetic, or psychic means — degrades his tactical bandwidth specifically and predictably: he loses the bird's-eye overlay and is forced to operate on baseline human spatial cognition, which is excellent but not what he is calibrated for. He will fight effectively without it; he will fight *differently* without it, and an adversary who understood this would engineer link-disruption as the opening move.

**Wing-rig vulnerabilities.** The flight rig is a piece of equipment. It can be jammed, fouled, sabotaged, or denied. He has contingency training for grounded operation, but his preferred operational style assumes mobility he cannot otherwise generate. Force him to ground operation and you have not defeated him; you have reduced his tempo by a measurable factor.

**Sleep, fatigue, hunger.** He runs disciplined self-maintenance. He is not exploitable through neglect of his own basic needs the way some peers are. He is exploitable through *operational tempo that prevents anyone else's basic needs from being met* — he will skip his own sleep to cover others, and a tempo designed to require that behavior will degrade him before it degrades the team.

**Medical-care surfaces.** His standing medical relationships and trusted clinicians are a category of operational asset that, by his own pattern, he does not adequately compartmentalize. He is loyal to providers who have treated him well, including some who lack the security infrastructure his profile warrants. This is a real surface and should be hardened.

---

### 9.7 Cognitive-Style Vulnerabilities

His cognitive style is field-dependent, gestalt, systems-and-relationships-first. This produces *superior* tactical awareness in most environments and creates specific blind spots in others.

**Strengths-as-vulnerabilities.**
- *Gestalt processing* is exploitable by *fragmented* presentation: information delivered in disconnected pieces from disparate sources, none of which on its own seems alarming, will assemble in his head into a coherent picture — including pictures the adversary wants him to see. He is *more* susceptible to engineered patterns than someone who thinks linearly, because his cognition is wired to make patterns out of noise.
- *Room-reading before individual-reading* means he is well-defended against individual deception and less defended against environmental deception. A whole staged room is more effective against him than a single skilled liar.
- *De-escalation preference* is exploitable by adversaries willing to *fake de-escalation*. He will extend the conversation past the point of tactical safety if the conversation appears to be working, because his prior is that conversation works. Stalling him with apparent good-faith dialogue is a real-time lever.
- *Anticipation as a defense* — he is the team member most likely to have thought about what happens after the mission — is exploitable by *changing the after*. Disrupting the post-mission environment (the family member, the community, the political conditions of return) while he is in-mission produces a specific category of distress he is not on-mission able to address.

**Speech under stress.** He shifts to operational/tactical speech when frightened or grieving. This is observable and exploitable as a *tell*: an interlocutor who knows his baseline can detect when he is metabolizing acute affect and time their asks accordingly.
