Asks pitched to him while he is in operational-speech mode pass; asks that require him to drop out of that mode fail.

---

### 9.8 The Withdrawal Pattern (Escalation Profile)

This subject has a **flat escalation curve**. He does not have a rage state. He does not have a breaking point that produces aggression. His functional analog of "breaking" is the *decision to step back*.

**Predict.** Watch for the following early indicators of impending withdrawal:
1. Increased verbal precision and decreased verbal warmth in team comms.
2. Lengthening intervals between voluntary social contact with the inner circle.
3. Quiet re-routing of personal time toward Harlem and family.
4. Operational hand-offs that look like normal delegation but are slightly more thorough than the situation requires.
5. A single, calm, on-the-record statement of position that the recipient party tends to underweight at the time and overweight in retrospect.

When all five appear, the withdrawal decision is already made; the announcement is 4–8 weeks out.

**Calm.** Genuine renegotiation of the conditions that produced the withdrawal pressure. Apology by the responsible parties without instrumental motive. Restoration of community-facing legitimacy. The Spencer-era withdrawal was reversed in Coates-era reacceptance precisely because the conditions of carrying the shield were *substantively renegotiated* — not by the institutions, but by him in relation to himself. External actors can support that renegotiation; they cannot perform it for him.

**Destabilize.** Engineer the conditions that produce withdrawal (see 9.4, 9.5) and then *block the exit* — refuse the resignation, public-pressure him back into the role, deny him the space to renegotiate. This produces the only psychological scenario in which his flat escalation curve has, in the record, shown signs of breaking. He is built to step back; deny him the step-back and you are testing the limits of his architecture.

---

### 9.9 The Race-Specific Load

The subject carries, across decades, the operational and psychic load of being the only Black person in a great many rooms — including, for years, the only Black Captain America in the country's imagination. The clinical analog is the literature on racial battle fatigue, and the operational analog is *any sustained role in which representation is a job function alongside the job function*.

**Reach.** He is reachable on race-specific matters with unusual directness *by people who share the load*. A conversation about it from someone who has not carried it lands as theory. A conversation from someone who has lands as data.

**Calm.** Material reduction of the load — not rhetorical reduction. Bringing in a second Black principal, distributing the representational weight, ensuring he is not the only one in the room on questions where the room's racial composition is operationally relevant.

**Persuade.** Honesty about the load itself is more persuasive than any offered compensation for it. He will accept a hard ask if the asker names the additional cost the ask imposes on him specifically. He will refuse a soft ask that pretends the cost does not exist.

**Provoke.** Denial of the load, in his hearing, by someone in a position to know better. The patronizing "we don't see race here" framing. The "you're being divisive" framing. The "you make this about race" framing. Each of these produces a specific, cool, articulate response and a quiet downgrade of the speaker in his operational trust ledger.

**Predict.** When the race-specific load is high, his withdrawal-pattern timeline shortens. The Spencer-era exhaustion is the case study.

**Destabilize.** Saturate the load. Make him the sole face of every Black-coded question while denying him the standing to speak about it. This is the documented destabilization protocol that worked once; it would work again, and a protective service should monitor for its emergence in the institutional environments around him.

---

### 9.10 What Does NOT Work

A complete leverage compendium must include the levers that *do not* exist, because hostile actors will try them and an honest threat model accounts for the wasted attempts.

- *Bribery, financial inducement, status offers.* His relationship to money and status is instrumental and modest. He cannot be bought, and attempts to buy him produce a measurable downgrade of the offerer.
- *Sexual entrapment.* No documented pattern of exploitable extra-relational behavior. Adult intimacy is functional, articulate, and not compartmentalized in ways that produce blackmail surface.
- *Substance compromise.* No documented use beyond unremarkable social baseline. Attempts to compromise him through substance would have to begin with creating the dependency, which is a long-cycle operation against a hypervigilantly self-aware subject.
- *Public humiliation.* He has absorbed an unusual quantity of public humiliation across his career and processed it without decompensation. Humiliation campaigns against him underperform against the planning that goes into them.
- *Threat of personal death.* He carries the knowledge of his own physical vulnerability with disciplined acceptance. Death threats register operationally rather than affectively; they produce planning, not panic.
- *Appeals to ego.* He does not have an exploitable ego in the conventional sense. The shield-relinquishment is dispositive: pathological self-importance does not voluntarily surrender symbolic capital under criticism.
- *Rage induction.* He cannot be made to lose composure in combat by taunting, by escalation, by personal insult. The provocations that work on him work *quietly* and on *delayed* timelines; the loud ones bounce.

The shape of what does not work, taken together, describes the shape of what does: this is a subject defended at the surface and accessible only at depth, defended against single insults and vulnerable to patterned ones, defended against his own ego and accessible through the people and places he loves.

---

### 9.11 Protective Synth


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION 6 — STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

A complete intelligence file is incomplete if it catalogues only vulnerabilities. The asset ledger on Wilson is unusually deep, unusually distributed across domains (somatic, cognitive, social, material, civic), and — most importantly — unusually *integrated*: his strengths do not sit beside each other as discrete capabilities, they reinforce each other in feedback loops. This is the architecture of the file's central finding, that Wilson's psychological intactness is the *primary* asset and the *generator* of the others.

---

### 6.1 SOMATIC & PHYSICAL ASSETS

**Conditioning floor.** Wilson maintains, at the operational baseline, what sports-medicine literature would classify as elite-tactical-athlete conditioning sustained into his fifth-plus decade of canonical activity. Resting heart rate is consistently in the high-40s/low-50s range inferable from his recovery curves in combat panels; VO₂ max and lactate-threshold metrics, while uncited, must be presumed at the 99th human percentile given his demonstrated capacity to sustain aerial maneuvering and ground combat in the same engagement without observable degradation. This is not gifted; it is *built*, daily, and the discipline of building it is itself an asset.

**The unenhanced advantage.** Counter-intuitive but real: Wilson's lack of serum is a strength as well as a vulnerability. He has never had the option of muscling through a problem, which has forced thirty-plus years of investment in *technique* — positioning, angle, leverage, momentum redirection, the use of environment as weapon. Enhanced operators (Rogers, Barnes, Walker) carry the implicit option of brute force, which atrophies refinement. Wilson cannot afford that atrophy and has not suffered it. In a contest of *applied* technique against equivalent opponents, the unenhanced operator who has spent his entire career compensating is, paradoxically, often the more technically proficient combatant.

**Aerial proficiency.** Wilson is the most experienced sustained-aerial close-combatant in the human-scale Marvel theater. This is a specific, narrow, deeply rare skill set — three-dimensional spatial reasoning at speed, threat-tracking across vertical axes, transition from glide to combat to glide without recovery time. Stark and Rhodes fly powered; Storm and Thor fly meteorologically; only Wilson and a handful of others *combat-fly* as their native operational mode. The proprioceptive map this builds in him is unique.

**The Redwing/avian link.** The empathic-sensory rapport with Redwing and broader avian populations is, in intelligence terms, a *persistent low-altitude ISR asset Wilson carries on his person*. He does not need to deploy a drone; he is networked into a sensor mesh that is everywhere birds are, which in any urban or rural environment is everywhere. The cognitive style this builds — *I am already seeing this from above* — is the deep structure of his tactical superiority.

**Injury tolerance and recovery profile.** The orthopedic load Wilson has absorbed is, as noted in §2, catastrophic by civilian standards. The fact that he is still in the field is itself an asset datum: it indicates pain tolerance, rehabilitation discipline, and somatic body-awareness sufficient to keep returning to operational capacity. He knows his body the way a long-haul aviator knows an airframe — every small noise, every changed feel, catalogued and watched.

---

### 6.2 COGNITIVE & TACTICAL ASSETS

**Gestalt processing.** Wilson reads situations in *fields*, not in chains. Where most operators sequence threats (this one, then this one, then this one), Wilson sees the room as a system and intervenes at the node that collapses the most variables. This is partly trained (social-work case-conceptualization, which is identical methodology), partly augmented (the bird's-eye habit), and partly temperament.

**De-escalation as primary skill.** This is genuinely rare and chronically undervalued in adversary assessments of him. Wilson can talk a hostage-taker down, a panicked civilian through evacuation, an enraged enhanced individual into compliance, and a fellow hero off a bad decision — using the same underlying skill stack: presence, named affect, low pitch, controlled pace, refusal to mirror escalation. In raw mission-outcome terms, de-escalation is *cheaper, faster, and lower-collateral* than combat resolution, and Wilson resolves more situations this way than any other Avengers-tier operator.

**Tactical patience.** Wilson will wait. He will hold a position, decline a tempting engagement, refuse to commit before he understands the field. This is the discipline that pairs with the gestalt — seeing the system is useless if you cannot tolerate the time it takes to see it.

**Operational planning.** Documented across the Brubaker and Spencer runs: when Wilson plans an operation, the after-action footprint is unusually clean. Few civilian casualties, few collateral structural losses, clear extraction paths, contingency branches pre-thought. This is a habit of mind — *anticipation* in the Vaillantian defense sense, weaponized into operational practice.

**Languages and cultural fluency.** Wilson moves through Harlem, federal Washington, international theaters (Symbol of Truth), and Wakandan diplomatic space with code-switching fluency. The asset is not just linguistic; it is the meta-skill of *registering the room's register* and adjusting without losing self.

**Verbal generativity.** Wilson is the team's verbal anchor. Under stress, language gets *more* available to him, not less — the opposite of most operators, in whom acute stress narrows expressive range to tactical clipping. Wilson can crack a joke that lowers a hostile crowd's temperature mid-engagement. This is a rare neurological gift and a daily-trained skill simultaneously.

---

### 6.3 PSYCHOLOGICAL RESILIENCE FACTORS

**Earned secure attachment.** Detailed in §3 — the foundation of everything else. Children of double violent parental loss are not supposed to arrive at adulthood capable of stable, articulate, durable bonds. Wilson did. The asset value of this cannot be overstated: it is the substrate on which his entire operational and civic life is built.

**Mature defense profile.** Humor, sublimation, altruism, anticipation, intellectualization-under-stress — these are the defenses the Vaillant literature associates with the highest-functioning quintile of long-term-followed cohorts. Wilson runs the full mature stack, *natively*, without therapy-acquired retrofit.

**Affect regulation.** Wilson has, across fifty in-universe years, never lost composure in combat. This is not affective flatness; it is *regulation*. The affect is there, it is felt, it is metabolized in real time without externalization. The operational implication is that adversaries cannot bait him into error — a profoundly rare asset in his weight class.

**Identity self-authorship.** Wilson has been told by a Cosmic-Cube-empowered fascist that he was a different person; by the federal apparatus that his Avengers seat was racial accounting; by half the national media that he could not be Captain America; by Hydra that he was the wrong man for the shield. He came through all of it with a coherent self. This is not luck. It is a *practiced* capability — the daily habit of choosing his own account of himself over the accounts pressed on him. As a resilience factor, it is nearly inexhaustible: every successful self-authorship event strengthens the next.

**Post-traumatic growth without dramatization.** Wilson has converted trauma into capability (social work, de-escalation, Black-community advocacy) without organizing his identity around the trauma. He does not perform his wounds. He does not require their acknowledgment as a condition of function. This makes him, in operational terms, *quietly* rather than *visibly* recovered — a much more stable state.

**Withdrawal as healthy regulation.** The 2017 shield surrender, often misread as a defeat, is structurally one of his greatest resilience demonstrations. Faced with an unsustainable role configuration, he down-regulated by stepping back rather than decompensating in place. This is the textbook adaptive response, and very few high-symbolic-load operators are capable of it.

---

### 6.4 RELATIONAL & SOCIAL ASSETS

**The small circle.** Wilson's intimate operational network is small, deep, and time-tested: Rogers (decades), Barnes (post-thaw, durable), Misty Knight (intermittent but foundational), Torres (mentee/protégé), Sarah and her sons (family core), Riley (pre-canon, formative). Each relationship is *worked* — phoned into, shown up for, repaired after rupture. This is not a network he assembled; it is a network he *maintains*.

**Mentor capacity.** Wilson's handling of Torres is the clearest evidence: patient, developmental, willing to let the protégé fail at survivable cost, generous with credit, clear about standards. He produces capable successors, which is among the rarest leadership outputs in the Avengers-tier population (Stark cannot do it, Rogers does it only by accident, Banner cannot do it). This means Wilson's strengths *propagate* — they are not extinguished with him.

**Community embedment in Harlem.** Wilson is not a hero who *visits* his community; he is *from* it and *of* it. The civilian network in Harlem — clergy, social workers, community organizers, neighborhood elders, formerly incarcerated men he has worked with, kids he has known since they were kids — is an intelligence, logistics, and moral-legitimacy asset of enormous depth. He can move through that geography with full cover, full information, and full moral authority. No federal agency could build this; he *is* it.

**Cross-class fluency.** Wilson is equally credible at a Harlem stoop conversation, a Wakandan diplomatic reception, a Senate hearing, and an Avengers strategy session. The asset is not just linguistic code-switching (see §6.2) but *moral* code-switching without moral *compromise* — he can adjust register without adjusting substance.

**Trust-magnet effect.** Civilians under threat default to trusting Wilson faster than most heroes. Part of this is the warm-approach interpersonal pattern; part is the verbal de-escalation skill; part is racial signaling (Black civilians, especially, do not have to wonder if he will see them); part is simply that he projects, accurately, that he is paying attention to the *person* in front of him and not to the optics around them.

**Loyalty without idealization.** Wilson loves Rogers without thinking Rogers is right about everything. He works with Barnes without absolving him of his history. He partners with institutions without serving them uncritically. This is the mature form of loyalty and it is operationally invaluable: he will not be blindsided by a partner's failure because he was never blind to it.

---

### 6.5 MATERIAL & TECHNICAL ASSETS

**The wing rig (current generation).** Wakandan-collaborative, vibranium-componented, integrated EXO-7 derivative — flight, glide, hard-point munitions, tactical sensor suite, encrypted comms. Highly maintained; Wilson is mechanically literate about his own kit and does not rely on external techs for field repair.

**The shield (when carried).** Vibranium alloy, the historical Rogers shield. Wilson's throwing technique is documented as *different* from Rogers' — less brute-line, more bank-angle, more use of curved returns and aerial deflection paths. He has retrofitted the shield's use to his flight pattern rather than the reverse.

**Wakandan relationships.** The T'Challa connection is the deepest non-Avengers institutional tie Wilson holds. It provides technology pipeline, intelligence cooperation, sanctuary if ever needed, and — critically — a non-US frame of reference for evaluating his own country's behavior. This is geostrategic ballast.

**Avengers infrastructure access.** Quinjets, medical, intelligence, comms, safehouse network. Wilson is on the standing-access tier and has been for decades.

**Civilian infrastructure.** Apartment(s), the Harlem operating footprint, the hotline operation from the Spencer era (whether currently active or dormant, the *capacity* to stand it up is preserved). The civilian footprint is unusually robust for a costumed operator and provides operational fallback in scenarios where superheroic infrastructure is compromised or unavailable.

**Reputational capital.** Wilson is one of a small number of costumed operators with net-positive standing across simultaneously: Black America, the broader civilian public (post-Spencer-era polarization having largely settled), the Avengers institutional memory, international partners, and the federal apparatus (cautiously). This convertible reputational capital is itself a working asset — doors open for him that do not open for Stark or Rogers.

---

### 6.6 MORAL & CIVIC ASSETS

**Operational code clarity.** Wilson knows what he believes and can articulate it without sloganizing. Pragmatic communitarianism — people in places, force as last resort, institutions held conditionally, country as project rather than idol. This is a *workable* code, robust to edge cases, transferrable to subordinates, defensible in public.

**Refusal of instrumentalization.** Wilson will not be used. The Gyrich seat, the Hydra co-option attempt, the various federal pressures — at each point he has either refused, withdrawn, or negotiated terms. This is the asset that makes him *trustworthy*: actors cannot acquire him cheaply.

**Conditional service.** Wilson serves until service compromises integrity, at which point he stops. This is the opposite of the Rogers model (serve through compromise, repair from inside) and operationally more sustainable. It means his service, when offered, is *uncompromised*.

**Voice as instrument.** Wilson can speak to a hostile public and shift its temperature, not always or fully, but reliably more than most. The 2017 shield surrender press conference, the various Symbol of Truth international scenes — he uses voice as a civic instrument, not just a tactical one.

---

### 6.7 META-ASSETS (assets that generate other assets)

**The discipline of choice.** Wilson's signature meta-capability is the *daily, repeated practice of choosing his self-account over those imposed on him*. Each iteration strengthens the next. This is what underwrites the identity-self-authorship resilience factor, the refusal of instrumentalization, the conditional-service principle, and the equanimity under adversarial pressure. It is the file's single most important asset entry because it is the *generator* of his stability rather than an expression of it.

**The integration of work and self.** Social work and superheroism are the same vocation for Wilson — the making-safe of unsafe places — expressed at different scales. This integration prevents the role-strain decompensation that has destroyed other operators (Stark, Banner, repeatedly Rogers). When the costumed role becomes unsustainable, the civilian role catches him; when the civilian role is insufficient, the costumed role extends his reach. He is never doing only one thing.

**Sustainability orientation.** Wilson plans for *next year* and *the next operator* in a population that mostly plans for the next fight. He builds infrastructure (the hotline), develops successors (Torres), maintains relationships (the small circle), conserves his own capacity (the withdrawals when needed). This long-time-horizon orientation means his assets *compound* rather than deplete.

**The absence of secret rot.** Most operators at Wilson's tier carry a hidden corrosive — Stark's addictive structure, Rogers' grief-buried rigidity, Barnes' dissociative substrate, Stark's narcissistic injury layer, Banner's split. Wilson, after fifty years of file-building, does not present a hidden corrosive. The Snap retcon was the candidate, and it was metabolized. This absence is itself the deepest asset: there is no time-bomb in the file.

---

### 6.8 SYNTHESIS

The asset profile reads, in summary, as a man whose strengths are unusually *coherent*: each capability is connected to and reinforced by the others, the somatic underwrites the tactical, the tactical underwrites the relational, the relational underwrites the psychological, the psychological underwrites the moral, and the moral feeds back into the somatic discipline that makes the whole structure run. There are very few weak links in this chain, and the ones that exist (somatic mortality, the body that can die) are *known to him* and *factored into his planning*, which converts them from vulnerabilities into managed variables.

The intelligence implication is direct: Wilson is not a subject who can be efficiently broken. He has been tested across every available axis — childhood loss, racial pressure, institutional betrayal, identity violation, public humiliation, near-death combat — and he has returned each time more coherently himself, not less. The asset ledger does not describe a man with capabilities; it describes a man *constituted as a capability*, whose continued function is the function. This is the rarest profile in the file system, and it is the basis on which UATU recommends that Samuel Thomas Wilson be regarded not as a useful operator but as a *load-bearing element* of the moral architecture of his era.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## SECTION 6 — FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

### 6.0 Orientation: What "Breaking" Looks Like in This Subject

The first analytical task is to correct an intuitive error. Most subjects in this dossier class break *outward*: rage, substance recurrence, dissociative episode, paranoid spiral, betrayal of a principal, abandonment of a post under fire. Wilson does none of these. His decompensation profile is **internalizing, deliberate, and articulate** — which makes it both harder to predict from surface telemetry and harder to interrupt once it begins, because by the time it is observable to handlers, he has already finished the cognitive work that produced it.

The operative paradox: Wilson does not crack under the loads that crack his peers. He has been beaten unconscious, dropped from altitude, told his personality was a Cosmic Cube fabrication, watched his closest partner die and return and turn fascist and return, been publicly denounced as a fraudulent Captain America by a coordinated media apparatus, and presented none of the standard collapse markers. What he *does* break under is structural — long-arc, role-strain, legitimacy-erosion conditions — and his break, when it comes, takes the form of **withdrawal of consent**. He stops playing the part. He sets the symbol down and walks out of the frame. Operationally this looks like resignation; clinically it is closer to a *negotiated dissociation from role*, conducted with full insight and minimal affective dysregulation.

This section maps the escalation path, the collapse signature, the things that have to be true for it to happen, and the things that — to date — have not been tested.

---

### 6.1 The Escalation Ladder (Acute Stressors)

Wilson's acute-stress ladder is shallow and well-regulated. The rungs are observable and have been consistent across writers from Englehart to Onyebuchi.

**Rung 1 — Baseline elevation.** Threat appears. Verbal output *increases* in density and decreases in playfulness; jokes do not stop but tighten, become drier, become tools rather than ornaments. Eye-line lifts: Wilson, even without Redwing aloft, begins scanning altitude as well as horizon. Sentence length shortens. The shoulders drop rather than rise — a fighter's tell of someone *settling* rather than *startling*.

**Rung 2 — Operational mode.** Tactical/imperative speech displaces conversational speech. Names are used as commands ("Buck — left." "Joaquin — up."). He breaks situations into evacuation/containment/engagement triage out loud. This is the somatic-cognitive mode in which he is most himself — paradoxically, **acute combat stress is regulating for Wilson, not dysregulating**. Handlers should note: when Wilson is in clear operational mode, he is *not* near collapse. He is in his competence.

**Rung 3 — Stretched competence.** Mission load exceeds capacity. Tells: he stops checking in with teammates by name, begins issuing instructions to Redwing in fragments, the bird's-eye narration in his interior monologue (per writer convention since the '70s) becomes choppy. He absorbs hits he would normally evade — not from incapacity but from triage, accepting body cost to preserve mission cost. *This is the most dangerous rung for his body and the least dangerous for his psyche.* He does not break here. He breaks *later*, in the after-action, when the calculus of what the absorption cost him becomes itemizable.

**Rung 4 — Acute moral-injury event.** Civilian death he could not prevent. A failure of de-escalation that he had argued for. Use of force against a target whose unenhanced humanity mirrors his own. The signature here is **stillness** — Wilson goes quiet, finishes the operational requirements, and *only then* allows himself to register what happened. Observable lag of fifteen minutes to several hours between the precipitating event and the affective response, during which he is functionally normal and tactically reliable.

**Rung 5 — Decompensation.** Discussed at length below. Acute-stress decompensation in Wilson is *rare* and almost never combat-induced. When it occurs it is the trailing edge of a long structural process, and the acute event is the trigger, not the cause.

---

### 6.2 The Long Stressor: Role-Strain Erosion

Wilson's true failure mode is not acute. It is *cumulative*, and it has a recognizable architecture, observed clearly twice (the Gyrich Avengers tenure, 1979; the first Captain America tenure, 2015–2017) and faintly visible in several lesser arcs (the Priest run frustrations; the Coates-era hesitations around re-accepting the shield).

The architecture has four stages:

**Stage I — Conditional acceptance.** Wilson takes a role under conditions he has interrogated and finds acceptable. He is clear-eyed about the imperfection of the conditions; he believes he can do enough good within them to justify the cost. *This stage can last years.*

**Stage II — Accumulating discrepancy.** The actual operating conditions diverge from the accepted conditions. He notices early — his room-reading is too good not to — and he *files* the discrepancies rather than confronting them. The filing is not denial; it is deliberate triage. He believes the work matters more than the friction, and he absorbs the friction as a cost of the work. *Observable telemetry: he begins talking less about the role in private settings, more about specific cases. He retreats from the abstract ("being Captain America") into the concrete ("this hostage situation, this kid, this neighborhood").*

**Stage III — Legitimacy crisis.** A threshold event reveals that the discrepancy is not friction but structure — that the role, as constituted, cannot be performed with integrity. Critically, this is *almost never a single dramatic moment*; it is a slow conclusion he reaches by aggregation. The Americops, the Hauser-analog broadcasts, the Hydra Captain America's appropriation of *his* symbol, the federal pressure to operate as an arm of the state rather than as a community-rooted figure — none of these alone would have moved him. Their aggregate did.

In Stage III, observable tells include: longer silences in team comms; increased time spent with Misty Knight, Sarah, or other figures outside the operational frame; a shift in his de-escalation language from "we can fix this" to "we can get through this"; and — diagnostic — a return to *the Falcon name in his own internal monologue*, even when wearing the shield. He retreats into the older, less-contested identity as a stabilizer.

**Stage IV — Withdrawal of consent.** He sets the role down. Publicly, deliberately, with a statement that is articulate, non-accusatory, and final. The Spencer-era shield surrender (*Captain America: Sam Wilson* #21, 2017) is the paradigm case. *He does not quit in anger; he resigns in clarity.* This is the most important behavioral signature in the file: **Wilson's collapse looks like a press conference, not a breakdown.**

---

### 6.3 The Decompensation Signature, Granular

When Stage IV occurs, the surface presentation is paradoxically calm. The internal state is not.

**Affective register.** Flat-to-warm. He continues to greet, to joke (more sparingly), to maintain eye contact, to ask after others. The warmth is intact; what is absent is *generativity* — he no longer produces new humor, new framings, new ideas for how the situation could be different. He converses inside the new fact rather than against it.

**Somatic markers.** Sleep tightens (shorter, earlier rising — not insomnia but reduction). Appetite unchanged. Training continues with mild compulsive intensification — the disciplined non-enhanced body is something he can still control when the role is not. The flight rig comes off in domestic settings more often; he is more willing to be *physically* the man without the wings than he was before.

**Verbal markers.** Drop in first-person plural usage. Where previously "we" was reflexive (the team, the country, the project), it becomes more deliberate and more bounded — "we" contracts to the small circle (Barnes, Torres, Misty, Sarah) and away from the institutional "we." Increase in agentive past tense when referring to the role: "what I was doing," "when I was carrying that." He grammatically separates himself from the symbol before he physically sets it down.

**Relational markers.** *Increased*, not decreased, contact with the inner circle. This is the single most reliable indicator that Wilson is decompensating into withdrawal rather than into depression: he draws *closer* to his attachments, not further. He calls Sarah more. He drops in on Misty without operational pretext. He spends evenings with Barnes that are not debriefs. The protective effect of stable adult attachments noted in Section 4 is here doing its observable work — the decompensation is being *held* by the relational network, which is why it never crosses into clinical pathology.

**Cognitive markers.** Sharpened, not blunted. Wilson in late Stage III through Stage IV is at his most analytically lucid. He is doing the work of articulating to himself why the role has become impossible to perform with integrity, and he does it with the same systems-thinking, bird's-eye discipline he brings to tactics. The collapse, again, looks like *clarity*.

---

### 6.4 What His Collapse Is Not

It is necessary to enumerate the absences, because they discipline the threat model.

- **No rage state.** No writer across fifty in-universe years has produced a credible Wilson-loses-it scene. The closest approximations (moments in the Priest run; the confrontations with the Hydra-coded Rogers in *Secret Empire*) are *cold* anger, fully articulate, never disinhibited. There is no berserker mode to plan for.
- **No substance recurrence.** No baseline use to recur to.
- **No paranoid spiral.** Even under the maximally paranoia-justifying conditions (the Snap retcon, Hydra's appropriation of national symbols, surveillance-state pressure from S.H.I.E.L.D.), Wilson's threat-assessments remained reality-tested. He distrusts specific institutions for specific reasons; he does not generalize to a paranoid worldview.
- **No principal-betrayal risk.** Wilson does not turn on Rogers, on Barnes, on Torres, on Misty, on Sarah, under any documented stressor. His loyalty is durable to the point of being a liability in the *opposite* direction (overstaying costly roles to preserve relationships).
- **No suicidal ideation, active or passive.** Notable given the trauma load. The drive to *make safe* appears to be self-extending: he is one of the people he is obligated to keep alive.
- **No dissociative episode in present tense.** Despite the historical Snap material, no behavioral evidence of fugue, amnesia, or identity-state switching has been credibly recorded. The Snap material is *integrated*, not active.
- **No abandonment of post under fire.** When Wilson withdraws, he withdraws *between* missions, after the present operation is concluded and the field is safe. He has never set the shield down with a hostage still in play.

---

### 6.5 The Conditions That Produce Collapse

Synthesizing across the documented Stage IV events and the partial Stage III approaches:

**Necessary condition 1 — Sustained legitimacy assault.** Not a single attack but a *campaign*, long enough that the cumulative cognitive load becomes itemizable. The Hauser-analog broadcasts over many months; the Gyrich-era institutional condescension over a tenure; the slow weaponization of his image by adversaries he cannot fight directly. A single bad day does not move him. A bad year does.

**Necessary condition 2 — Demonstrated structural unfixability.** Wilson can absorb almost any amount of personal cost if he believes the role can still be performed with integrity. The threshold is reached when he concludes the *structure* — not the individuals, not the news cycle, not the mission — makes integrity impossible. This is why he is more vulnerable to slow institutional rot than to dramatic crises: the dramatic crisis can be answered; the rot cannot.

**Necessary condition 3 — Availability of an honorable exit.** Wilson does not collapse into incapacity. He collapses into a *decision*, and the decision requires a door. The Spencer-era surrender required Rogers' return as a credible successor; the Gyrich-era exit required the Avengers as an institution that could continue without him. If no honorable exit is available — if setting the role down would itself constitute abandonment — Wilson does not break. He keeps carrying it, at escalating cost, indefinitely. *This is the scenario in which his body, not his psyche, becomes the failure point.*

**Necessary condition 4 — Intact relational network.** Counterintuitively, Wilson's withdrawals occur when his support structure is *strong*, because the withdrawal is held by it. When the network is degraded (Rogers dead or compromised, Barnes off-grid, Misty out of contact, Sarah unreachable), Wilson does not withdraw. He doubles down, because there is no one to receive the resignation. The protective network is also the *permission* network.

**Sufficient trigger.** Given the four necessary conditions, the sufficient trigger is almost always a **moral-injury event involving a community he is sworn to protect** — a death the role could not prevent, a harm the role enabled, a use of his symbol against the people whose service was the original point. The Americops arc is the textbook instance.

---

### 6.6 The Unfailed Tests (Vulnerabilities Not Yet Probed)

A complete failure-mode file must catalogue not only what has broken him but what has been *insufficiently tested* and therefore remains uncharacterized.

- **Sustained loss of the inner circle.** Wilson has experienced individual losses (Rogers' apparent death; Riley pre-canon) but never the simultaneous loss of *the network*. Behavioral prediction: this is the condition under which his internalizing pattern would most likely fail. If the holding environment is removed, the withdrawal has nowhere to go. The likeliest decompensation in this scenario would be **compulsive over-functioning to the point of physical collapse** — he would absorb the entire load of the work the network used to share, and his unenhanced body would be the failure point. *Not* depression; *not* aggression; *exhaustion as somatic event*.
- **Forced sustained occupation of a role he has withdrawn consent from.** What happens if no honorable exit is available *and* the structural unfixability is unambiguous? Untested. The behavioral prediction: a slow, observable hollowing of the operational presence — competence preserved, generativity gone, the room-reading still on but the room-changing off. Effective performance, dead behind the eyes. The closest historical analog in the file is the late Gyrich tenure, but that had an exit.
- **A community-rooted moral injury he cannot articulate to himself.** Wilson's regulation depends heavily on his capacity to *narrate* what has happened to him. A trauma that resists narration — an ambiguous failure, a death whose causal chain is genuinely unclear, a community judgment he cannot decide whether to accept — would deprive him of his most reliable defense. Untested. Prediction: prolonged Stage III without resolution to Stage IV, with cumulative quiet damage.
- **Reactivation of the Snap material as present-tense rather than historical.** If the dissociation he has integrated were to be re-induced — by Cosmic Cube, by telepathic assault, by something analogous — the question is whether the integration would hold. The file's strong prior is that it would, because the integration is the work of decades of stable functioning, not a fragile recent reconciliation. But this is a prior, not a finding.
- **Direct confrontation with a version of himself made wrong.** Wilson has watched Rogers turned Hydra; he has not, in any sustained way, been forced to confront a *Sam Wilson* made into an instrument of harm. The pressure-point analysis in Section 5 (authorship of self) suggests this would land at the deepest available nerve. Prediction: the cold, articulate anger state, sustained longer and at higher intensity than any recorded instance, and a willingness to use force he would not otherwise use — bounded, still, but expanded.

---

### 6.7 Summary

Wilson's failure mode is the most analytically interesting in the principal-class file precisely because it does not look like failure. He breaks by **withdrawing consent from roles whose structure has become incompatible with his integrity**, after long deliberation, with his relational network intact and his affective regulation preserved. The collapse is articulate, public, and final-to-that-role but not final-to-the-self — he sets the symbol down and remains, recognizably, the man who was carrying it.

The handlers' error, with a subject like this, is to look for the wrong signals. There will be no rage, no spiral, no bottle, no betrayal. There will be a quieter "we," a return to the older name in private monologue, longer evenings with Sarah, a flight rig left in the case more often, and — when the four necessary conditions align — a press conference, calmly delivered, in which the most reliable man in the room explains why he is no longer available for the job as constituted.

The collapse, properly understood, is **not a failure of the man**. It is the man refusing to fail the project by continuing to perform a counterfeit of it. That this is legible as collapse at all is a fact about the institutions that needed him, not about him.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: SAMUEL THOMAS WILSON
## Section 6 — TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

---

### 6.1 Baseline Projection: The Default Arc

Absent significant exogenous shock, Sam Wilson's most probable ten-year trajectory is a continuation of the *Symbol of Truth* mature-state pattern with progressive externalization of his work. The vector is observable: he has already moved from solo Harlem operator (1970s–80s) → reluctant Avenger (1979) → equal partner (1990s–2000s) → embattled inheritor (2015–17) → re-integrated bearer (2018–21) → internationally-scoped principal (2022–present). Each step has widened the radius of operation while narrowing the radius of personal need. The arrow points toward **institution-building**.

The probable concrete forms this takes:

- **A standing operational unit, not S.H.I.E.L.D.-derived.** Sam has demonstrated repeatedly (the civilian hotline of the Spencer run, the Wakanda-coordinated work of *Symbol of Truth*, the deliberate mentorship of Torres) that he gravitates toward small, accountable, mission-specific structures rather than blanket institutions. Expect this to formalize: a Wilson-led entity — possibly Harlem-headquartered, possibly with Wakandan technical partnership, possibly with Misty Knight's Nightwing Restorations as a sister org — that handles cases the Avengers are too blunt for and S.H.I.E.L.D. is too compromised for. Headcount under twenty, deliberately multiracial, deliberately civilian-facing, deliberately undeputized.

- **Progressive transfer of the shield-bearing function to Torres or a successor**, on a timeline of perhaps five to eight in-universe years. Sam has done the work of proving the shield can change hands without diminishment; he will be the first holder to *plan* the next handoff rather than be ended into it. Expect Sam, late-career, to occupy a role analogous to what Rogers once was for him: the trainer, the conscience, the radio in the ear.

- **Public-facing civic work outside the cape**. Probable forms: testimony before congressional committees on policing and super-human oversight (he is one of the few principals whose testimony would be heard across partisan lines); an ongoing relationship with the social-work credentialing world he never fully left; possibly a foundation in his father's name. Sam is the rare hero who could plausibly run for office and the rare hero who almost certainly will not — the pressure point on *authorship of self* makes electoral life intolerable to him.

### 6.2 The Open Questions

Five questions will determine which version of the next two decades obtains. They are not equally weighted; the first two dominate.

**Q1 — Can he stay in the mantle this time?** The Spencer-era surrender is the single most diagnostic event in his file, and the question is whether the Coates-era re-acceptance was a stable resolution or a deferred recurrence. The honest read: it was *partially* stable. Sam came back to the shield having renegotiated his relationship to it (he carries it as Sam Wilson, not as a successor-to-Steve), but the underlying conditions that broke him the first time — the media polarization, the racialized adjudication of his right to the symbol, the structural loneliness of being The Black Captain America — have not improved and in most measurable ways have worsened. The protective factor is that Sam now knows the failure mode and has built scaffolding (Torres, the Harlem network, the explicit refusal to live in the Tower) against it. The risk factor is that the scaffolding is finite and the load is not.

**Q2 — What happens when Steve Rogers is gone for good?** Rogers' eventual permanent removal (death, aging-out, retirement to a function Sam cannot reach) is the largest unmodeled stressor in Sam's future. Their relationship is the longest stable peer attachment of Sam's adult life and the only one in which he is reliably the *junior* partner in symbolic weight even when senior in operational role. The loss of Rogers removes both a confidant and a reference point against which Sam has organized half a century of self-definition. Sam will not decompensate — his attachment baseline is too durable — but the *style* of his subsequent work will shift. Expect a quieter, more elegiac period; expect increased turn toward Barnes (the other inheritor of that loss); expect a re-examined relationship to the shield in which the Rogers-shaped permission is gone and Sam carries it on no authority but his own. This is, paradoxically, where he will become *most* fully Captain America.

**Q3 — Does the Snap retcon return?** It has been narratively dormant for two decades, but it is not erased, and the structure of comics ensures that any sufficiently bold writer can re-raise it. The forward question is not whether Sam could survive a Snap revisitation — he could — but what the *terms* of his response would be. The mature Sam would not relitigate whether the implanted memories were "real"; he would treat the question as resolved by the life he has subsequently lived. The pressure point would not be the retcon itself but anyone (Red Skull derivative, Hydra cell, Mephisto-class entity) attempting to use it as leverage on his self-concept. Such an attempt would produce one of the rare sustained-anger states.

**Q4 — Does the body hold?** Sam is unenhanced. He has fifty in-universe years of cumulative combat trauma on a body that was never built to absorb it. The sports-medicine analog predicts: progressive cervical and lumbar degeneration; cumulative mTBI burden with executive-function and mood implications appearing in the seventh decade; rotator-cuff and knee deterioration that will eventually constrain the flight rig before it constrains his ground game. The forward question is whether Sam will *accept* the body's limits when they arrive or whether the over-functioning pattern (§3) will push him past them. Best guess: he accepts, with one or two costly delays. He is too psychologically integrated to die of denial, but he is too responsibility-bound to retire on schedule.

**Q5 — Harlem.** Sam's psychic homeostasis is contingent on Harlem's continued existence as a community he can return to and serve. Gentrification, displacement, the slow dilution of the neighborhood his parents died in — these are the slow-motion stressors whose effect will only be visible in aggregate. If Harlem-as-Sam-knows-it ceases to be reachable, the *community legitimacy* pressure point becomes structurally unsatisfiable, and his work will lose its primary somatic anchor. This is the threat he is least equipped to fight because it is not opposable by force.

### 6.3 Fork Points (Discrete Events That Branch the Trajectory)

**Fork A — A second forced shield surrender.** If political or institutional pressure escalates to the point that Sam is again asked or required to relinquish the mantle, the second surrender will not look like the first. The first was values-driven withdrawal. A second would be either (a) a flat refusal to surrender — the first time in Sam's life he stands on the symbol rather than steps off it — or (b) a permanent walk-away with no return. The determining variable is whether the pressure comes from *the state* (refuse) or *from communities he respects* (walk). 

**Fork B — Torres killed or compromised in the field.** Joaquin Torres is the first person Sam has unambiguously *mentored from zero*. His loss would activate the parental-loss substrate that Sam has spent fifty years sublimating and would constitute the single greatest test of his affect regulation. Probable response: not aggression, not collapse, but a several-month operational withdrawal followed by re-emergence in a markedly more institutional, less personal mode — Sam would protect himself from future Torreses by building structures that absorb the loss rather than individuals who carry it. Cost: a real diminution of warmth, recoverable but not automatic.

**Fork C — Public restitution / state recognition.** The trajectory in which the United States formally apologizes for the Isaiah Bradley history (and the broader history that surrounds him) and Sam is positioned as the public face of that reckoning. Growth-positive *if* he is permitted to define his own role within it; catastrophic *if* he is instrumentalized as the comfortable Black face of an incomplete reckoning. Sam will be acutely aware of which is which. Expect him to demand structural concessions (reparative funding, Bradley's full record, oversight changes) as conditions of participation and to walk if those concessions are theater.

**Fork D — Rogers returns as antagonist (the Hydra-Cap echo).** A future scenario in which Rogers is again subverted (cosmic, telepathic, alternate-timeline incursion) and Sam must oppose him directly. The Spencer-era version of this nearly broke Sam because the betrayal of the symbol was inseparable from the betrayal of the friend. The mature Sam would absorb it differently — he has done the work of separating Rogers-the-man from Rogers-the-symbol — but the cost would be real and the relationship, even after restoration, would be permanently different.

**Fork E — Discovery that the avian link is mutational and heritable / locatable in a broader population.** This is the dormant medical question. If the link is revealed to be the marker of a population rather than an individual peculiarity, Sam acquires an unwanted community responsibility that he is temperamentally suited for and operationally over-extended for. Expect acceptance, expect exhaustion.

### 6.4 What Pushes Toward Growth

The growth-positive interventions are remarkably specific and largely *relational and structural* rather than therapeutic:

- **Durable co-leadership.** Sam thrives in dyads and degrades in solitude. Any structure that institutionalizes a co-principal (Misty Knight on the civilian side, Barnes on the operational side, Torres on the symbolic-successor side) is protective. The growth-state Sam is never the lone Black Captain America again; the failure-state Sam is.

- **Permission to put the work down without the symbol down.** The single most growthful thing the surrounding world can offer Sam is the structural possibility of *sabbatical* — leave that is not surrender. Sam has never had this; every withdrawal has cost him the mantle. A standing arrangement under which the shield can be safely paused would defuse the over-functioning pattern at its root.

- **Explicit, repeated authorization from communities whose judgment he respects.** Not from the press, not from the state. From Harlem; from Bradley; from the Wakandan principals he has worked with; from Black veteran communities. Sam's self-concept is examined rather than restful, and the only thing that quiets the examination is the *right* witnesses saying the right things, periodically, over time.

- **Continued therapeutic-adjacent practice without formal pathologization.** Sam will probably never be in conventional therapy and does not appear to need it; what he needs and uses is the social-work peer community, the church-of-his-father echo (less observance than ethical accountability), and the discipline of his physical practice. Anything that preserves these is protective.

- **A successor he trusts.** Growth and exit are the same door for Sam. The clearest growth-state is the one in which he has, by intention and on a schedule of his choosing, handed the work to people who carry it without him.

### 6.5 What Pushes Toward Catastrophe

The catastrophe vectors are correspondingly specific. Sam will not be destroyed by anything he can punch.

- **Isolation in the symbol.** The single most dangerous configuration is a Sam who is the only Black principal in his operational radius, who has lost Rogers, who has lost or distanced Torres and Barnes, and whose Harlem anchorage has been hollowed out. This is not a probable configuration but it is constructible from current trends, and it is the configuration in which the over-functioning pattern becomes self-consuming. Outcome: not breakdown, but a slow drift into a joyless, machine-like execution of the role — Sam without humor is the early-warning sign, and there is no other.

- **Instrumentalization that he cannot exit.** The state, or an institutional actor he cannot disengage from, weaponizes the symbol of him against constituencies he is sworn to. Sam's defense against this has historically been the right of refusal; remove the right of refusal (legal compulsion, blackmail-grade leverage, hostage-grade leverage against his small circle) and the result is moral injury at the structural level. This is the scenario most likely to produce the first depressive episode of his adult life.

- **A betrayal from within the small circle.** Not Rogers-as-Hydra (cosmic, abstractable); a chosen, sober betrayal by Barnes, Misty, or Torres. Sam's attachment durability is built on the assumption that the small circle is the one place that does not require argument. Genuine betrayal there would not produce rage; it would produce a permanent contraction of the trust radius, and a contracted Sam is a less effective Sam in every dimension that matters.

- **A child of his own.** This is the unspoken variable in his file. Sam has never been a father in canon, and the parental-loss substrate has been sublimated through mentorship rather than reproduction. A biological or adoptive child would be the single largest reorganization of his psychic economy he has ever undertaken — growth-positive if it occurs in a stable period, catastrophe-adjacent if it occurs under operational load, because the *child as hostage to the work* is the configuration his own father died demonstrating.

- **The Snap weaponized at scale.** Not a private revisitation but a public one — the retcon surfaced as propaganda, used by a political actor to delegitimize him before the constituencies whose judgment he depends on. This is the only currently-constructible scenario in which the community-legitimacy pressure point and the authorship-of-self pressure point activate simultaneously. Even Sam's regulation has limits, and that is where they would be tested.

### 6.6 Long Horizon — The Twenty-Year View

The probable end-state, if the trajectory holds: Sam in his late sixties or early seventies, the shield handed off, the wings retired or radically simplified, working out of a Harlem office, advising rather than operating, the Captain America title held by someone he trained, the *name* Sam Wilson having acquired the kind of weight Steve Rogers' name had when Sam first inherited it. He will not write a memoir. He will give the occasional interview. He will be at the funerals of his peers. He will be, in the assessment of this file, the rare principal who exits the operational life with his psychological integrity not merely intact but enlarged — the man who answered the question of whether the symbol could be carried by someone who refused to let the symbol carry him.

The catastrophe end-state, if the vectors of §6.5 converge: a Sam who is still effective, still functional, still humorous in public, but who has contracted his trust radius to one or two people, who carries the shield without joy, who declines to mentor because he cannot afford another loss, and who dies in the field at an age at which the body finally fails him before the will does. This is the *quiet* catastrophe — no breakdown, no scandal, just the slow loss of the warmth that was the single most distinctive thing about him. It is constructible from the current evidence. It is not yet probable.

The fork between these two end-states is not, in this analyst's read, determined by Sam. He has done the internal work. The fork is determined by whether the people and institutions around him allow him the conditions under which his demonstrated psychological health can continue to be expressed — whether he is permitted, in the simplest possible terms, to keep being the version of himself he has fought his whole life to author.

The file's standing recommendation: *protect the conditions, not the man*. He has never needed protecting. He has needed, and rarely been given, the room.

## Relationship Graph
### [[Steve Rogers (Captain America)]]
- Oldest deep bond and the relational template for the rest of his adult life - peer, not mentor-mentee, despite the optics
- Loves Steve without idealizing him; will argue ideology for hours and not damage the friendship
- Failure mode: if Steve were ever again to be the face of something Sam had to fight (Hydra-Cap recurrence, ideological capture), Sam would fight him with grief and without hesitation - the trust does not buy compliance
- Leverage: an authentic message verifiably from Steve will get a hearing from Sam that almost nothing else will; a forged one is the single highest-value deception any adversary could attempt

### [[James Buchanan Barnes (Winter Soldier / White Wolf (formerly Bucky))]]
- Hard-won partnership earned across years of mutual operational dependence; deep mutual protective custody
- Sam is one of the few people Bucky will let close when destabilized; Bucky is one of the few people Sam will accept rescue from without arguing
- Failure mode: a triggered or hijacked Bucky aimed at Sam's small circle would force Sam into the rare sustained-anger state, and Sam would still try to bring him home alive
- Leverage: threats to Bucky reach Sam faster than threats to himself

### Joaquin Torres
- Mentee, the new Falcon, developmental relationship that lets Sam give what he was denied
- Public cover, private debrief; trust not withdrawn for mistakes
- Failure mode: Torres killed or maimed on Sam's watch would be the closest canonical trigger to a sustained guilt episode - it would route through the Riley wound
- Leverage: Torres in genuine danger reorders Sam's priority stack

### Misty Knight
- Intermittent intimate partner, durable peer, professional respect
- One of the rare relationships in which Sam is not the most competent person in the room and likes it that way
- Failure mode: a betrayal or manipulation routed through Misty would be the deepest interpersonal wound short of Steve
- Leverage: shared community-policing values give them a common operational frame no one else in Sam's life occupies

### Sarah Wilson Casper
- Younger sister, family-of-origin anchor, the part of Harlem that is literally his
- Failure mode: any threat to Sarah collapses Sam back to the eight-year-old who lost his parents - and produces the most dangerous, least negotiable version of him
- Leverage: she is the single highest-value protective referent in his life and the lowest-cost way to find him

### Redwing
- Reciprocal empathic-telepathic bond, sensory augmentation, and a genuine relationship - not a tool
- Failure mode: injury to or weaponization of Redwing grounds Sam cognitively and emotionally in the same stroke
- Leverage: an adversary who studies the link can predict his aerial decision-tree

### Nick Fury And Shield
- Working relationship of conditional cooperation; Sam split publicly over surveillance demands on communities he serves
- Failure mode: any S.H.I.E.L.D. successor demanding data on Harlem or analogous communities will lose him on contact
- Leverage: Fury can get him in the room; cannot get him to comply once there

### Henry Peter Gyrich
- Historical antagonist of the bureaucratic variety - the man who put him on the Avengers as a quota
- Failure mode: a Gyrich-class figure attempting to instrumentalize him again triggers immediate, articulate refusal
- Leverage: the template for everything Sam will not accept again

### Red Skull
- The author of the iatrogenic identity trauma (Snap retcon); the wound that made the authorship drive permanent
- Failure mode: a Cosmic-Cube-class identity attack would reopen the deepest wound and is the rare condition under which Sam's decision-making can momentarily stall
- Leverage: the Skull or any successor with Cube-equivalent capability is the single largest psychiatric threat in his rogues gallery

### Harlem Community
- The constituency that predates and outlasts every cape he has worn; the metric by which he privately measures himself
- Failure mode: a sustained loss of legitimacy in Harlem is the closest thing to a depressive trigger he has
- Leverage: a credible Harlem voice telling him to step up or step back will move him when national authority cannot
